// ================================================================
// ✅ GLOBAL CONSTANTS — File ke top pe define karo
// ================================================================
var DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('DEFAULT_PASSWORD') || 'Rrn@1234';
var SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS    = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 8 hours

// ================================================================
// ✅ FULL MIGRATION — Run once after deploy
// Handles: plain text passwords, unsalted hashes, admin passwords
// After this runs, 3-way check is no longer needed
// ================================================================
function runFullMigration() {
  var results = { credentials: 0, admin: 0, skipped: 0, errors: 0 };
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  // ── 1. CREDENTIALS sheet ──────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    var credSh = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSh && credSh.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var credRows = credSh.getRange(2, 1, credSh.getLastRow()-1, 6).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < credRows.length; i++) {
        var uid  = String(credRows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var hash = String(credRows[i][1] || '').trim();
        if (!uid || !hash) { results.skipped++; continue; }

        var saltedDefault   = hashPassword(DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD, uid);
        var unsaltedDefault = hashPassword(DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD);

        // Already salted correctly? Skip
        if (hash === saltedDefault) { results.skipped++; continue; }

        var newHash;
        if (hash === unsaltedDefault) {
          // Unsalted default → salted default
          newHash = saltedDefault;
        } else if (hash === DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD || hash === 'admin123') {
          // Plain text → salted default
          newHash = saltedDefault;
        } else {
          // Unknown hash (custom password) → reset to salted default + force change
          newHash = saltedDefault;
          credSh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('YES'); // force change flag
        }

        credSh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(newHash);
        results.credentials++;
        Logger.log('✅ Migrated CREDENTIALS: ' + uid);
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('CREDENTIALS migration error: ' + e.toString());
    results.errors++;
  }

  // ── 2. ADMIN_USERS sheet ─────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    var adminSh = ss.getSheetByName('ADMIN_USERS');
    if (adminSh && adminSh.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var adminRows = adminSh.getRange(2, 1, adminSh.getLastRow()-1, 3).getValues();
      for (var j = 0; j < adminRows.length; j++) {
        var aid   = String(adminRows[j][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var ahash = String(adminRows[j][2] || '').trim();
        if (!aid || !ahash) { results.skipped++; continue; }

        // Try known admin passwords
        var knownPasswords = ['admin123', DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD, 'Admin@123', 'admin'];
        var matched = false;

        for (var k = 0; k < knownPasswords.length; k++) {
          var pw = knownPasswords[k];
          if (ahash === pw ||
              ahash === hashPassword(pw) ||
              ahash === hashPassword(pw, aid)) {
            // Re-hash with salt
            adminSh.getRange(j + 2, 3).setValue(hashPassword(pw, aid));
            Logger.log('✅ Migrated ADMIN_USERS: ' + aid + ' (matched: ' + pw + ')');
            results.admin++;
            matched = true;
            break;
          }
        }
        if (!matched) { results.skipped++; }
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ADMIN migration error: ' + e.toString());
    results.errors++;
  }

  var summary = 'runFullMigration complete!\n' +
    'Credentials upgraded: ' + results.credentials + '\n' +
    'Admin upgraded: ' + results.admin + '\n' +
    'Skipped (already ok): ' + results.skipped + '\n' +
    'Errors: ' + results.errors;

  Logger.log(summary);
  return { success: true, message: summary };
}


function saveToPendingEntries(type, operatorId, data, branchCode) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX H3: Sanitize all string fields in entryData before saving
    if (data && typeof data === 'object') {
      var skipKeys = ['date', 'loanDate', 'closerDate', 'submittedAt', 'dob'];
      Object.keys(data).forEach(function(key) {
        if (skipKeys.indexOf(key) === -1 && typeof data[key] === 'string') {
          data[key] = sanitizeInput(data[key]);
        }
      });
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');

    if (!pendingSheet) {
      pendingSheet = ss.insertSheet('PENDING_ENTRIES');
      pendingSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([[
        'Entry ID', 'Type', 'Data (JSON)', 'Operator',
        'Submitted', 'Status', 'Supervisor Notes', 'Branch code'
      ]]);
      pendingSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#ff6b6b')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }

    // ✅ FIX 1: Force all values to correct types
    const entryId    = 'PE' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    const typeStr    = String(type        || '').trim();
    const opStr      = String(operatorId  || '').trim();
    const branchStr  = String(branchCode  || '').trim();

    // ✅ FIX 2: If branchCode still empty, try fetching from WALLET_MASTER / CREDENTIALS
    let finalBranch = branchStr;
    if (!finalBranch && opStr) {
      try {
        const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(opStr);
        if (branchResult && branchResult.success) {
          finalBranch = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();
        }
      } catch (be) {
        Logger.log('Branch fetch fallback error: ' + be.toString());
      }
    }

    // ✅ FIX 3: Force JSON to plain string — prefix with ' to prevent Sheets auto-format
    const dataJSON = JSON.stringify(data || {});

    // ✅ FIX 4: Use getRange+setValues instead of appendRow (avoids type coercion issues)
    const newRow = pendingSheet.getLastRow() + 1;
    pendingSheet.getRange(newRow, 1, 1, 8).setValues([[
      entryId,        // A: Entry ID
      typeStr,        // B: Type
      dataJSON,       // C: Data (JSON) — plain string, no auto-format
      opStr,          // D: Operator
      new Date(),     // E: Submitted
      'PENDING',      // F: Status
      '',             // G: Supervisor Notes (empty)
      finalBranch     // H: Branch code
    ]]);

    // ✅ FIX 5: Force column C (JSON) as plain text so Sheets doesn't reformat it
    pendingSheet.getRange(newRow, 3).setNumberFormat('@STRING@');

    Logger.log('✅ Pending entry saved: ' + entryId + ' | Op: ' + opStr + ' | Branch: ' + finalBranch);
    logActivity(opStr, 'PENDING_ENTRY', typeStr + ' - Entry ID: ' + entryId);

    return {
      success: true,
      entryId: entryId,
      message: '✅ Entry submitted for approval!\n\nEntry ID: ' + entryId
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveToPendingEntries error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// MEMBER ENTRY: Save approved entry
// Column structure from Image 2:
// A: Member ID | B: Name | C: Contact | D: User ID | E: Email | F: Branch Code
// ================================================================
function saveMemberEntry(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let memberSheet = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    
    if (!memberSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'MEMBER ENTRY sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if (!entryData.memberId || !entryData.name) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID and Name required' };
    }
    
    // Append row with exact 6 columns
    memberSheet.appendRow([
      entryData.memberId || '',      // A: Member ID
      entryData.name || '',           // B: Name
      entryData.contact || '',        // C: Contact
      entryData.userId || '',         // D: User ID
      entryData.email || '',          // E: Email
      entryData.branchCode || ''      // F: Branch Code
    ]);
    
   Logger.log('✅ Member entry saved: ' + entryData.memberId);

    // ✅ FIX C-3: Credential creation sirf addMemberCredentials() se — ek jagah, consistent default password
    // saveMemberEntry ke andar inline creation hatao — do alag default passwords ki problem fix
    try {
      const credResult = addMemberCredentials(entryData.userId, entryData.branchCode || '');
      if (credResult.success && !credResult.alreadyExists) {
        Logger.log('✅ CREDENTIALS created for member via addMemberCredentials: ' + entryData.userId);
      }
    } catch (ce) {
      Logger.log('Credential creation warning: ' + ce.toString());
    }

    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Member entry saved successfully',
      memberId: entryData.memberId
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveMemberEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// ACCOUNT OPEN: Save approved entry
// Column structure from Image 3:
// A: MEMBER ID | B: NAME | C: ACCOUNT NO | D: Account_Open_Date | 
// E: ACCOUNT TYPE | F: NOMINEE NAME | G: RELATIONSHIP | H: STATUS | 
// I: EMAIL | J: User ID | K: photo Url | L: DOB | M: Branch Code
// ================================================================
function saveAccountOpen(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!accountSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if (!entryData.memberId || !entryData.accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID and Account No required' };
    }
    
    // Append row with exact 13 columns
    accountSheet.appendRow([
      entryData.memberId || '',           // A: MEMBER ID
      entryData.name || '',               // B: NAME
      entryData.accountNo || '',          // C: ACCOUNT NO
      entryData.openDate || new Date(),   // D: Account_Open_Date
      entryData.accountType || '',        // E: ACCOUNT TYPE
      entryData.nomineeName || '',        // F: NOMINEE NAME
      entryData.relationship || '',       // G: RELATIONSHIP
      'ACTIVE',                           // H: STATUS
      entryData.email || '',              // I: EMAIL
      entryData.userId || '',             // J: User ID
      entryData.photoUrl || '',           // K: photo Url
      entryData.dob || '',                // L: DOB
      entryData.branchCode || ''          // M: Branch Code
    ]);
    
    Logger.log('✅ Account opened: ' + entryData.accountNo);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Account opened successfully',
      accountNo: entryData.accountNo
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveAccountOpen error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT: Save approved entry
// Column structure from Image 4:
// A: Account_Number | B: NAME | C: AMOUNT | D: Interest | 
// E: Current_Balance | F: Date | G: MONTH FOR | H: Email | 
// I: User ID | J: (skip) | K: Branch code
// ================================================================
function saveDepositEntry(entryData) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');

    if (!depositSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT sheet not found' };
    }

    if (!entryData.accountNo || !entryData.amount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account No and Amount required' };
    }

    const amount   = parseFloat(entryData.amount)   || 0;
    const interest = parseFloat(entryData.interest) || 0;

    // ✅ FIX #3: Fetch ACTUAL previous balance — last entry for this account
    let previousBalance = 0;
    if (depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const allData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (let i = allData.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (String(allData[i][0]).trim() === String(entryData.accountNo).trim()) {
          previousBalance = parseFloat(allData[i][4]) || 0; // Col E: Current_Balance
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Running balance = previous + this deposit + interest
    const currentBalance = previousBalance + amount + interest;

    const row = [
      entryData.accountNo  || '',      // A: Account_Number
      entryData.name       || '',      // B: NAME
      amount,                          // C: AMOUNT
      interest,                        // D: Interest
      currentBalance,                  // E: Current_Balance (running)
      entryData.date       || new Date(), // F: Date
      entryData.monthFor   || '',      // G: MONTH FOR
      entryData.email      || '',      // H: Email
      entryData.userId     || '',      // I: User ID
      '',                              // J: (skip/empty)
      entryData.branchCode || ''       // K: Branch code
    ];

    depositSheet.appendRow(row);

    // ✅ FIX #2: Update operator wallet after deposit approval
    if (entryData.operatorId) {
      try {
        const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId);
        if (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) {
          const newWalletBal = (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) + amount + interest;
          updateWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId, newWalletBal);
          Logger.log('✅ Wallet updated after deposit approval: ' + entryData.operatorId + ' +₹' + (amount+interest));
        }
      } catch (we) {
        Logger.log('Wallet update warning (deposit): ' + we.toString());
      }
    }

    Logger.log('✅ Deposit saved: ' + entryData.accountNo + ' ₹' + amount + ' | Prev: ₹' + previousBalance + ' | New Balance: ₹' + currentBalance);

    // ✅ AUTO EMAIL: Deposit confirmation email send karo
    try {
      sendDepositConfirmationEmail({
        userId:         entryData.userId      || '',
        name:           entryData.name        || '',
        email:          entryData.email       || '',
        accountNo:      entryData.accountNo   || '',
        amount:         amount,
        interest:       interest,
        newBalance:     currentBalance,
        date:           entryData.date        || '',
        monthFor:       entryData.monthFor    || '',
        branchCode:     entryData.branchCode  || ''
      });
    } catch (emailErr) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Deposit email warning (non-fatal): ' + emailErr.toString());
    }

    return {
      success:     true,
      message:     'Deposit saved successfully',
      newBalance:  currentBalance,
      prevBalance: previousBalance
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveDepositEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ================================================================
// LOAN MANAGEMENT: Save approved entry
// Column structure from Image 5:
// A: Member_ID | B: LOAN A/C | C: NAME | D: LOAN TYPE | E: ROI | 
// F: Loan_Amount | G: Loan_Date | H: MONTHLY EMI (IF ANY) | 
// I: TOTAL PAID | J: Remaining | K: Loan_Status | L: CLOSED DATE | 
// M: Email | N: User ID | O: Search Code
// ================================================================
function saveLoanEntry(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!loanSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'LOAN MANAGEMENT sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if (!entryData.memberId || !entryData.loanAcNo || !entryData.loanAmount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID, Loan A/C, and Amount required' };
    }
    
    const loanAmount = parseFloat(entryData.loanAmount) || 0;
    const roi = parseFloat(entryData.roi) || 0;
    const monthlyEmi = parseFloat(entryData.monthlyEmi) || 0;
    
    // Append row with exact 15 columns
    loanSheet.appendRow([
      entryData.memberId || '',           // A: Member_ID
      entryData.loanAcNo || '',           // B: LOAN A/C
      entryData.name || '',               // C: NAME
      entryData.loanType || '',           // D: LOAN TYPE
      roi,                                // E: ROI
      loanAmount,                         // F: Loan_Amount
      entryData.loanDate || new Date(),   // G: Loan_Date
      monthlyEmi,                         // H: MONTHLY EMI (IF ANY)
      0,                                  // I: TOTAL PAID (initially 0)
      loanAmount,                         // J: Remaining (full amount initially)
      'ACTIVE',                           // K: Loan_Status
      '',                                 // L: CLOSED DATE (empty)
      entryData.email || '',              // M: Email
      entryData.userId || '',             // N: User ID
      entryData.branchCode || ''          // O: Branch Code
    ]);
    Logger.log('✅ Loan saved: ' + entryData.loanAcNo + ' = ₹' + loanAmount);

    // ── Operator Wallet: DEBIT by loan amount ─────────────────────
    // Loan disbursement = operator gives cash to member → wallet decreases
    if (entryData.operatorId) {
      try {
        const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId);
        if (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) {
          const currentWallet = parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0;
          const newWalletBal  = currentWallet - loanAmount;
          updateWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId, newWalletBal);
          Logger.log('✅ Wallet DEBITED after loan disbursement approval: '
            + entryData.operatorId + ' -₹' + loanAmount
            + ' (₹' + currentWallet + ' → ₹' + newWalletBal + ')');
        }
      } catch (we) {
        Logger.log('Wallet update warning (loan disburse): ' + we.toString());
        // Non-fatal
      }
    }

    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Loan entry saved successfully',
      loanAcNo: entryData.loanAcNo,
      loanAmount: loanAmount
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveLoanEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// LOAN REPAY & DEFAULT FEE COLLECTION: Save approved entry
// Column structure:
// A: LOAN AC/SIP AC NO | B: PAID AMT | C: MONTH FOR |
// D: INTEREST | E: DEFAULT FEE | F: Branch Code
// ================================================================
function saveLoanRepayment(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');

    if (!repaySheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'LOAN REPAY sheet not found' };
    }
    if (!entryData.loanAcNo || !entryData.paidAmount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Loan A/C and Paid Amount required' };
    }

    const paidAmt    = parseFloat(entryData.paidAmount)  || 0;
    const interest   = parseFloat(entryData.interest)    || 0;
    const defaultFee = parseFloat(entryData.defaultFee)  || 0;
    const totalPaid  = paidAmt + interest + defaultFee;  // total cash collected from member

    // ── 1. Save to LOAN REPAY sheet ──────────────────────────────
    repaySheet.appendRow([
  entryData.loanAcNo   || '',        // A: LOAN AC /SIP AC NO
  paidAmt,                           // B: PAID AMT
  entryData.monthFor   || '',        // C: MONTH FOR
  interest,                          // D: INTEREST
  defaultFee,                        // E: DEFAULT FEE
  entryData.branchCode || '',        // F: Branch Code
  entryData.date       || new Date() // G: Date ✅ NAYA
]);
    Logger.log('✅ Loan repayment saved: ' + entryData.loanAcNo + ' = ₹' + paidAmt);

    // ── 2. Update LOAN MANAGEMENT: TOTAL PAID (Col I) & Remaining (Col J) ──
    let prevTotalPaid = 0;
    let prevRemaining = 0;
    let loanRowIndex  = -1;
    try {
      const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
      if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        const loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 11).getValues();
        for (let i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
          // Col B (index 1) = LOAN A/C
          if (String(loanData[i][1] || '').trim() === String(entryData.loanAcNo).trim()) {
            prevTotalPaid = parseFloat(loanData[i][8]) || 0;  // Col I (index 8): TOTAL PAID
            prevRemaining = parseFloat(loanData[i][9]) || 0;  // Col J (index 9): Remaining
            loanRowIndex  = i + 2;  // 1-based sheet row
            break;
          }
        }
        if (loanRowIndex > 0) {
          const newTotalPaid  = prevTotalPaid + paidAmt;
          const newRemaining  = Math.max(0, prevRemaining - paidAmt);
          loanSheet.getRange(loanRowIndex, 9).setValue(newTotalPaid);   // Col I
          loanSheet.getRange(loanRowIndex, 10).setValue(newRemaining);  // Col J
          // Auto-close loan if fully paid
          if (newRemaining <= 0) {
            loanSheet.getRange(loanRowIndex, 11).setValue('CLOSED');    // Col K: Loan_Status
            loanSheet.getRange(loanRowIndex, 12).setValue(new Date());  // Col L: CLOSED DATE
            Logger.log('✅ Loan CLOSED: ' + entryData.loanAcNo);
          }
          Logger.log('✅ Loan updated: Paid=' + newTotalPaid + ' Remaining=' + newRemaining);
        }
      }
    } catch (le) {
      Logger.log('Loan MANAGEMENT update warning: ' + le.toString());
      // Non-fatal — repayment already saved
    }

    // ── 3. Operator Wallet: DEBIT by total cash collected ────────
    // Loan repayment = operator collects cash from member → wallet increases
    if (entryData.operatorId) {
      try {
        const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId);
        if (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) {
          const currentWallet = parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0;
          const newWalletBal  = currentWallet + totalPaid;
          updateWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId, newWalletBal);
          Logger.log('✅ Wallet CREDITED after loan repayment approval: '
            + entryData.operatorId + ' +₹' + totalPaid
            + ' (₹' + currentWallet + ' → ₹' + newWalletBal + ')');
        }
      } catch (we) {
        Logger.log('Wallet update warning (loan repayment): ' + we.toString());
        // Non-fatal
      }
    }

    return {
      success:      true,
      message:      'Repayment saved successfully',
      paidAmount:   paidAmt,
      totalPaid:    totalPaid,
      newRemaining: Math.max(0, prevRemaining - paidAmt),
      loanClosed:   Math.max(0, prevRemaining - paidAmt) <= 0
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveLoanRepayment error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// ACCOUNT CLOSE: Save approved entry
// Column structure from Image 7:
// A: ACCOUNT NUMBER | B: NAME | C: SETTLEMENT AMT | 
// D: CLOSER DATE | E: Branch Code
// ================================================================
function saveAccountClose(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let closeSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT CLOSE');
    
    if (!closeSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT CLOSE sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if (!entryData.accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account Number required' };
    }
    
    const settlementAmt = parseFloat(entryData.settlementAmount) || 0;
    
    // Save to ACCOUNT CLOSE sheet
    closeSheet.appendRow([
      entryData.accountNo || '',          // A: ACCOUNT NUMBER
      entryData.name || '',               // B: NAME
      settlementAmt,                      // C: SETTLEMENT AMT
      entryData.closeDate || new Date(),  // D: CLOSER DATE
      entryData.branchCode || ''          // E: Branch Code
    ]);
    
    // ✅ FIX: Mark account as CLOSED in ACCOUNT OPEN sheet (Col H = Status)
    const accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (accountSheet && accountSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const accData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < accData.length; i++) {
        // Col C (index 2) = AccountNo
        if (String(accData[i][2]).trim() === String(entryData.accountNo).trim()) {
          accountSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue('CLOSED');
          Logger.log('✅ ACCOUNT OPEN status set to CLOSED for: ' + entryData.accountNo);
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Account closed: ' + entryData.accountNo + ' | Settlement: ₹' + settlementAmt);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Account closed successfully',
      accountNo: entryData.accountNo,
      settlementAmt: settlementAmt
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveAccountClose error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// SUPERVISOR APPROVAL: Route to correct save function
// ================================================================
function approveEntry(entryId, supervisorId, notes, token) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again in a moment.' };
  }
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    // ✅ Input sanitization
    entryId      = String(entryId      || '').trim();
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();

    Logger.log('approveEntry called → entryId: "' + entryId + '" | supervisor: "' + supervisorId + '"');

    if (!entryId || !supervisorId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Entry ID and Supervisor ID are required' };
    }

    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only supervisors can approve entries' };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');

    if (!pendingSheet || pendingSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No pending entries found' };
    }

    const lastRow = pendingSheet.getLastRow();
    const data = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 8).getValues();

    // ✅ CRITICAL FIX: Supervisor UI rowIndex bhej raha tha instead of entryId
    // Smart detection: agar entryId numeric hai (like "2") toh rowIndex samjho
    // Agar "PE..." format hai toh entryId se search karo
    let targetRowIndex = -1;  // 1-based sheet row
    let targetData = null;

    const isNumeric = /^\d+$/.test(entryId);

    if (isNumeric) {
      // ✅ rowIndex mode: entryId is actually a row number
      const rowIdx = parseInt(entryId);
      if (rowIdx >= 2 && rowIdx <= lastRow) {
        const arrIdx = rowIdx - 2;
        if (arrIdx < data.length) {
          targetRowIndex = rowIdx;
          targetData = data[arrIdx];
          Logger.log('rowIndex mode: using row ' + rowIdx + ' directly');
        }
      }
    } else {
      // ✅ entryId mode: search by PE... string in Col A
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        const rowEntryId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
        if (rowEntryId === entryId) {
          targetRowIndex = i + 2;
          targetData = data[i];
          Logger.log('entryId mode: found at row ' + targetRowIndex);
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // ✅ Not found
    if (targetRowIndex === -1 || !targetData) {
      const availableIds = data.map(r => String(r[0] || '').trim()).filter(id => id).join(', ');
      Logger.log('Entry not found. Searched for: "' + entryId + '" | Available: ' + availableIds);
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Entry not found: "' + entryId + '". Please refresh and try again.\n\nAvailable IDs: ' + availableIds
      };
    }

    // ✅ Status check - Col F = index 5
    const status = String(targetData[5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (status !== 'PENDING') {
      return { success: false, message: 'Entry already ' + status + '. Cannot approve again.' };
    }

    const type          = String(targetData[1] || '').trim();   // Col B: Type
    const dataJSON      = String(targetData[2] || '{}').trim(); // Col C: JSON data
    const operatorIdCol = String(targetData[3] || '').trim();   // Col D: Operator ID
    const actualEntryId = String(targetData[0] || entryId).trim(); // Col A

    // ✅ Parse JSON safely
    let entryData;
    try {
      entryData = JSON.parse(dataJSON);
    } catch (parseError) {
      Logger.log('JSON parse error: ' + parseError + ' | Raw: ' + dataJSON);
      return { success: false, message: 'Data corrupt — JSON parse failed: ' + parseError.toString() };
    }

    // ✅ Always inject operatorId from PENDING_ENTRIES Col D into entryData
    // This ensures wallet updates work for all entry types (deposit, loan, repayment etc.)
    if (!entryData.operatorId && operatorIdCol) {
      entryData.operatorId = operatorIdCol;
    }

    Logger.log('Processing → type: ' + type + ' | entryId: ' + actualEntryId + ' | operator: ' + (entryData.operatorId || 'N/A'));

    // ✅ Route to correct save function
    let saveResult;
    switch (type) {
      case 'MEMBER_ENTRY':    saveResult = saveMemberEntry(entryData);    break;
    case 'ACCOUNT_OPEN':
        saveResult = saveAccountOpen(entryData);
        // ✅ FIX P3b: Send welcome email after account open approval
        if (saveResult && saveResult.success) {
          try {
            sendWelcomeEmail(entryData);
            Logger.log('✅ Welcome email sent for: ' + entryData.userId);
          } catch (we) {
            Logger.log('Welcome email warning: ' + we.toString());
          }
        }
        break;
      case 'DEPOSIT':         saveResult = saveDepositEntry(entryData);   break;
      case 'LOAN': {
        // ✅ FIX 5: Block approval if operator wallet insufficient — no negative wallets
        const loanAmt      = parseFloat(entryData.loanAmount) || 0;
        const loanOperator = String(entryData.operatorId || targetData[3] || '').trim();
        if (loanAmt > 0 && loanOperator) {
          const loanWalletCheck = getWalletBalance(loanOperator);
          const loanWalletBal   = (loanWalletCheck && loanWalletCheck.success) ? (parseFloat(loanWalletCheck.balance) || 0) : 0;
          if (loanWalletBal < loanAmt) {
            return {
              success: false,
              message: '⛔ Approval Blocked!\n\n' +
                       'Operator wallet mein loan disbursement ke liye cash nahi hai.\n\n' +
                       'Loan Amount:  ₹' + loanAmt.toFixed(2) + '\n' +
                       'Available:    ₹' + loanWalletBal.toFixed(2) + '\n\n' +
                       'Operator ko pehle cash receive karna hoga, tab hi yeh loan approve ho sakta hai.'
            };
          }
        }
        saveResult = saveLoanEntry(entryData);
        break;
      }
      case 'LOAN_REPAYMENT':  saveResult = saveLoanRepayment(entryData);  break;
     case 'ACCOUNT_CLOSE': {
        const closeAmt      = parseFloat(entryData.settlementAmount) || 0;
        const closeOperator = String(entryData.operatorId || targetData[3] || '').trim();
        const closeBranch   = String(targetData[7] || '').trim();

        // ✅ FIX H1: Block approval if operator wallet insufficient — no negative wallets
        if (closeAmt > 0 && closeOperator) {
          const preCheck = getWalletBalance(closeOperator);
          const preBal   = (preCheck && preCheck.success) ? (parseFloat(preCheck.balance) || 0) : 0;
          if (preBal < closeAmt) {
            return {
              success: false,
              message: '⛔ Approval Blocked!\n\n' +
                       'Operator wallet mein settlement amount nahi hai.\n\n' +
                       'Required:  ₹' + closeAmt.toFixed(2) + '\n' +
                       'Available: ₹' + preBal.toFixed(2) + '\n\n' +
                       'Operator ko pehle cash receive karna hoga tab hi yeh account close ho sakta hai.'
            };
          }
        }

        saveResult = saveAccountClose(entryData);

        if (saveResult && saveResult.success && closeAmt > 0 && closeOperator) {
          const opW    = getWalletBalance(closeOperator);
          const opBal  = (opW && opW.success) ? (parseFloat(opW.balance) || 0) : 0;
          const newBal = opBal - closeAmt;
          updateWalletBalance(closeOperator, newBal);
          recordWalletTransaction(
            'AC' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8),
            closeOperator, 'ACCOUNT_CLOSE', closeAmt,
            'ACCOUNT_CLOSE_SETTLEMENT',
            'Settlement for A/C: ' + entryData.accountNo,
            closeBranch
          );
          Logger.log('✅ Wallet deducted: ' + closeOperator + ' -₹' + closeAmt + ' → ₹' + newBal);
          saveResult.walletDeducted     = true;
          saveResult.newOperatorBalance = newBal;
        }
        break;
      }
      case 'MEMBER_MODIFY':
  saveResult = saveMemberModification(entryData);
  break;

case 'ACCOUNT_MODIFY':
  saveResult = saveAccountModification(entryData);
  break;
  case 'SAVINGS_DEPOSIT':
case 'SAVINGS_WITHDRAWAL':
  saveResult = saveSavingsEntry(entryData);
  break;
      default:
        return { success: false, message: 'Unknown entry type: "' + type + '"' };
    }

    if (!saveResult || !saveResult.success) {
      Logger.log('Save failed: ' + JSON.stringify(saveResult));
      return { success: false, message: saveResult ? saveResult.message : 'Save returned null' };
    }

    // ✅ Update PENDING_ENTRIES: Col F(6)=APPROVED, Col G(7)=notes
    pendingSheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, 6).setValue('APPROVED');
    pendingSheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, 7).setValue(notes || 'Approved by ' + supervisorId);

    logActivity(supervisorId, 'APPROVE_ENTRY', type + ' approved — Entry: ' + actualEntryId);
    Logger.log('✅ Approved row ' + targetRowIndex + ' entryId: ' + actualEntryId);

    // Build return message with extra info for account close
    let approveMsg = '✅ Entry approved and saved!\n\nType: ' + type + '\nEntry ID: ' + actualEntryId;
    if (type === 'ACCOUNT_CLOSE') {
      if (saveResult.walletDeducted) {
        approveMsg += '\n\n💳 Operator wallet deducted: ₹' + (parseFloat(entryData.settlementAmount) || 0).toFixed(2);
        approveMsg += '\nNew balance: ₹' + (saveResult.newOperatorBalance || 0).toFixed(2);
      } else if (saveResult.walletWarning) {
        approveMsg += '\n\n⚠️ ' + saveResult.walletWarning;
      }
    }

    return {
      success: true,
      message: approveMsg,
      walletDeducted: saveResult.walletDeducted || false,
      walletWarning: saveResult.walletWarning || null
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('approveEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}


// ================================================================
// OPERATOR SUBMIT FUNCTIONS
// These create pending entries with proper JSON structure
// ================================================================

function operatorSubmitMemberEntry(operatorId, memberData, token) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX C-2: Session token validate karo — operator spoofing rokta hai
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    // Validate required fields
    if (!memberData.memberId || !memberData.name) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID and Name are required' };
    }
    
    // Get branch code
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    
    // Add branch code to data
    memberData.branchCode = branchCode;
    
    // Save to pending entries
    return saveToPendingEntries('MEMBER_ENTRY', operatorId, memberData, branchCode);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitMemberEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSubmitAccountOpen(operatorId, accountData, token) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX C-2: Session token validate karo
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    // ✅ SERVER-SIDE DATE VALIDATION: Backdate bypass prevent karo
    var _submittedDate = (arguments[1] && arguments[1].openDate) || '';
    if (_submittedDate && !isToday(_submittedDate)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid date! Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai. Backdate submit nahi kar sakte.' };
    }


    if (!accountData.memberId || !accountData.accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID and Account No are required' };
    }
    
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    accountData.branchCode = branchCode;
    
    return saveToPendingEntries('ACCOUNT_OPEN', operatorId, accountData, branchCode);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitAccountOpen error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
function operatorSubmitDeposit(operatorId, depositData, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    var _dateCheck = isTodayOrCurrentMonth(
      (arguments[1] && arguments[1].date)     || '',
      (arguments[1] && arguments[1].monthFor) || ''
    );
    if (!_dateCheck.dateOk)  return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid date! Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai.' };
    if (!_dateCheck.monthOk) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid month! Sirf current month allowed hai.' };

    if (!depositData.accountNo || !depositData.amount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account No and Amount are required' };
    }

    // ✅ LOCK: SAVINGS account is form se submit nahi ho sakta
    var schemeCheck = getAccountScheme(depositData.accountNo);
    if (schemeCheck.success && schemeCheck.scheme === 'SAVINGS') {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ SAVINGS account ka deposit Savings tab se karo.' };
    }

    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode   = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    depositData.branchCode = branchCode;

    return saveToPendingEntries('DEPOSIT', operatorId, depositData, branchCode);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitDeposit error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSubmitLoan(operatorId, loanData, token) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX C-2: Session token validate karo
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    // ✅ SERVER-SIDE DATE VALIDATION: Backdate bypass prevent karo
    var _submittedDate = (arguments[1] && arguments[1].loanDate) || '';
    if (_submittedDate && !isToday(_submittedDate)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid date! Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai. Backdate submit nahi kar sakte.' };
    }


    if (!loanData.memberId || !loanData.loanAcNo || !loanData.loanAmount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID, Loan A/C, and Amount are required' };
    }
    
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    loanData.branchCode = branchCode;
    
    return saveToPendingEntries('LOAN', operatorId, loanData, branchCode);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitLoan error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSubmitLoanRepayment(operatorId, repaymentData, token) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX C-2: Session token validate karo
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    // ✅ SERVER-SIDE DATE VALIDATION: Backdate/future-month bypass prevent karo
    var _dateCheck = isTodayOrCurrentMonth(
      (arguments[1] && arguments[1].paymentDate) || '',
      (arguments[1] && arguments[1].monthFor) || ''
    );
    if (!_dateCheck.dateOk) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid date! Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai. Backdate submit nahi kar sakte.' };
    }
    if (!_dateCheck.monthOk) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid month! Sirf current month allowed hai.' };
    }


    if (!repaymentData.loanAcNo || !repaymentData.paidAmount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Loan A/C and Paid Amount are required' };
    }
    
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    repaymentData.branchCode = branchCode;
    
    return saveToPendingEntries('LOAN_REPAYMENT', operatorId, repaymentData, branchCode);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitLoanRepayment error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSubmitAccountClose(operatorId, closeData, token) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX C-2: Session token validate karo
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    // ✅ SERVER-SIDE DATE VALIDATION: Backdate bypass prevent karo
    var _submittedDate = (arguments[1] && arguments[1].closeDate) || '';
    if (_submittedDate && !isToday(_submittedDate)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Invalid date! Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai. Backdate submit nahi kar sakte.' };
    }


    if (!closeData.accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account Number is required' };
    }
    
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    closeData.branchCode = branchCode;
    closeData.operatorId  = operatorId; // ✅ Store for wallet deduction on approval
    
    return saveToPendingEntries('ACCOUNT_CLOSE', operatorId, closeData, branchCode);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitAccountClose error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function doGet(e) {
  // Check if operator parameter exists
  const isOperator = e && e.parameter && e.parameter.operator;
  
  // ============================================
  // OPERATOR FORMS (PENDING APPROVAL SYSTEM)
  // ============================================
  if (isOperator) {
    // ✅ FIX M-2: URL parameter whitelist sanitize karo — XSS prevent karta hai
    // Sirf alphanumeric + underscore + hyphen allowed — koi script inject nahi ho sakta
    const rawOp = String(e.parameter.operator || '');
    const operatorId = rawOp.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9_\-]/g, '').substring(0, 50);
// ✅ FIX: Token bhi URL se read karo
    const rawToken = String(e.parameter.token || '');
    const safeToken = rawToken.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9+\/=]/g, '').substring(0, 200);  // ← YEH 2 LINES ADD KARO
    if (!operatorId) {
      return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput('<h3>Invalid operator ID</h3>')
        .setTitle('Error');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'member-entry') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorMemberEntryForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Member Entry (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      
     // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'account-open') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorAccountOpenForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Account Open (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
     // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'deposit') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorDepositForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Deposit Entry (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      
    // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'loan') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorLoanForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Loan Entry (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'loan-repayment') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorLoanRepaymentForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Loan Repayment (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      
      // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    
    if (e.parameter.page === 'account-close') {
      const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorAccountCloseForm')
        .setTitle('OPERATOR - Account Close (Pending Approval)')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      
      // NAYA — token bhi inject:
return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
    }
    if (e.parameter.page === 'savings') {
  const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorSavingsForm')
    .setTitle('OPERATOR - Savings Deposit / Withdrawal')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
}

if (e.parameter.page === 'modify') {
  const template = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('OperatorModifyForm')
    .setTitle('OPERATOR - Modify Member / Account')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  return template.append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.OPERATOR_TOKEN = "' + safeToken + '";</script>');
}
    // ✅ FIX: Passbook print also available to operators (with operator context)
    if (e.parameter.page === 'passbook-print') {
      // ✅ FIX M-2: branch parameter bhi sanitize karo
      const rawBranch = String(e.parameter.branch || '');
      const branchCode = rawBranch.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9_\-]/g, '').substring(0, 20);
      return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('PassbookPrint')
        .setTitle('Passbook Print')
        .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL)
        .append('<script>window.OPERATOR_ID = "' + operatorId + '"; window.BRANCH_CODE = "' + branchCode + '";</script>');
    }
  }

  // Forms page
  if (e && e.parameter && e.parameter.page === 'pdf') {
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('futurelifeform')
      .setTitle('DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION- Admin Forms')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  }

  // Treasurer Login Page
  if (e && e.parameter && e.parameter.page === 'treasurer') {
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('CashOffice')
      .setTitle('Treasurer Login')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL)
      .append('<script>window.TREASURER_MODE = true;</script>');
  }
  // ADD THIS - Admin Login Page
  if (e && e.parameter && e.parameter.page === 'admin-login') {
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('AdminLogin')
      .setTitle('Admin Login - Branch Management')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  }
  // ADD THIS - Admin Login Page
  if (e && e.parameter && e.parameter.page === 'admin-massage') {
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('Annoucement')
      .setTitle('Admin Login - Branch Management')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  }
  // Default: Member Portal
  return HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('Index')
    .setTitle('DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION- Member Portal')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}
