function getWebAppUrl() {
  return ScriptApp.getService().getUrl();
}

// ============================================
// TREASURER LOGIN
// ============================================
function treasurerLogin(userId, password) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!userId || !password) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User ID and Password required' };
    }
     // ✅ FIX M-3: Brute force lockout check
    var lockCheck = checkLoginLockout(userId);
    if (lockCheck.locked) return { success: false, message: lockCheck.message };
    // ✅ FIX 13: holidayCheck only runs after lockout check — not at global scope
    var holidayCheck = isHolidayToday();
    // ✅ FIX: Holiday pe block nahi — sirf warning flag return karo
    // Frontend Day Begin pe warning dikhayega, login hoga normally
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet || credSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No credentials found' };
    }

    const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();

    for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
      const credId   = String(credData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const credPwd  = String(credData[i][1] || '').trim();
      const credRole = String(credData[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const credStatus = String(credData[i][4] || 'ACTIVE').trim().toUpperCase();

      if (credId === userId && credRole === 'TREASURER' && credStatus === 'ACTIVE') {
        // ✅ FIX: Salted hash — same as all other login functions
        const inputHashSalted = hashPassword(String(password), userId);
        if (inputHashSalted !== credPwd) {
          logFailedLogin(userId, 'Invalid password (Treasurer)');
          recordFailedLogin(userId);
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }
        if (true) { // password matched
          // Find mapped cash office — Col G (index 6) = Treasurer ID
          const officeSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
          let officeId = null;
          let officeName = null;
          if (officeSheet && officeSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
            const offData = officeSheet.getRange(2, 1, officeSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
            for (let j = 0; j < offData.length; j++) {
              if (String(offData[j][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId &&
                  String(offData[j][4] || 'ACTIVE').trim().toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
                officeId   = String(offData[j][0] || '').trim();
                officeName = String(offData[j][1] || '').trim();
                break;
              }
            }
          }
          logActivity(userId, 'TREASURER_LOGIN', 'Treasurer logged in' + (officeId ? ' - Office: ' + officeId : ' - No office assigned'));
          const sessionToken = createSession(userId);  // ✅ Session create karo
          var hCheck = isHolidayToday();
          return {
            success:        true,
            userId:         userId,
            role:           'TREASURER',
            officeId:       officeId,
            officeName:     officeName,
            token:          sessionToken,
            isHoliday:      hCheck.isHoliday || false,
            holidayWarning: hCheck.isHoliday
              ? '🏖️ Aaj Holiday hai: ' + (hCheck.description || 'Office Holiday') + '\nEmergency kaam ke liye logged in hain.'
              : null
          };
        }
      }
    }

    return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Treasurer login error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Login error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ============================================
// 🔐 SECURITY SYSTEM - PASSWORD HASHING
// ============================================

function checkCredentials() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
  
  // Example: Password column B, row 2 se start
  const password = sheet.getRange('B2').getValue();
  
  // Null/empty check BEFORE hashing
  if (!password || password.toString().trim() === '') {
    Logger.log('Password is empty in sheet');
    return;
  }
  
  const hashedPassword = hashPassword(password.toString());
  
  if (hashedPassword) {
    Logger.log('Hashed: ' + hashedPassword);
  }
}

function hashPassword(password, salt) {
  try {
    // Double check yahan bhi
    if (!password || password.trim() === '') {
      Logger.log('Password cannot be null or empty');
      return null;
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX: Salt add karo — rainbow table attacks se protection
    // salt optional hai (backward compatible) — agar diya toh use karo
    var input = salt ? (password + '::SALT::' + String(salt).toUpperCase()) : password;
    
    const hash = Utilities.computeDigest(
      Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.SHA_256,
      input,
      Utilities.Charset.UTF_8
    );
    
    return hash.map(byte => ('0' + (byte & 0xFF).toString(16)).slice(-2)).join('');
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Hash error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}
// ================================================================
// ✅ PASSWORD MIGRATION FUNCTION
// Deploy ke baad SIRF EK BAAR run karo:
//   1. GAS Editor → Run → migratePasswordsToSaltedHash
//   2. Execution complete hone ka wait karo
//   3. Phir kabhi mat chalao
//
// Kya karta hai: CREDENTIALS sheet mein sab unsalted SHA-256
// hashes ko salted hashes se replace karta hai.
// ================================================================
function migratePasswordsToSaltedHash() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      Logger.log('❌ CREDENTIALS sheet not found or empty');
      return { success: false, message: 'CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };
    }

    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    var rows    = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 6).getValues();
    var migrated = 0;
    var skipped  = 0;

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var userId     = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var storedHash = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
      if (!userId || !storedHash) { skipped++; continue; }

      // Already salted with default password? Skip.
      var saltedDefault   = hashPassword(DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD, userId);
      if (storedHash === saltedDefault) { skipped++; continue; }

      // Unsalted default password? Migrate cleanly.
      var unsaltedDefault = hashPassword(DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD);
      if (storedHash === unsaltedDefault) {
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(saltedDefault);
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('YES'); // force password change
        Logger.log('✅ Migrated (default pwd): ' + userId);
        migrated++;
        continue;
      }

      // Custom password — cannot reverse hash.
      // Reset to salted default + force change on next login.
      sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(saltedDefault);
      sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('YES');
      Logger.log('🔄 Reset to default (custom pwd): ' + userId);
      migrated++;
    }

    var summary = '✅ Migration complete! Migrated: ' + migrated + ' | Skipped: ' + skipped + '\n' +
                  '⚠️ Users whose passwords were reset must login with default password: ' + DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD;
    Logger.log(summary);
    return { success: true, message: summary, migrated: migrated, skipped: skipped };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ migratePasswordsToSaltedHash error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ── Input Sanitizer — XSS se bachao ──────────────────────────
function sanitizeInput(value) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return '';
  return String(value)
    .replace(/&/g,  '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g,  '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g,  '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g,  '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g,  '&#x27;')
    .replace(/\//g, '&#x2F;')
    .trim();
}
// ================================================================
// ✅ SERVER-SIDE DATE VALIDATOR
// Operator ke submitted date ko today se compare karta hai
// Backdate bypass prevent karta hai even if JS readonly hata diya
// ================================================================
function isToday(dateStr) {
  try {
    if (!dateStr) return false;
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var inputStr = String(dateStr).trim().substring(0, 10); // take only YYYY-MM-DD part
    return inputStr === todayStr;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('isToday error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

function isTodayOrCurrentMonth(dateStr, monthStr) {
  try {
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var todayStr   = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var currentMon = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM');

    var dateOk  = !dateStr  || String(dateStr).trim().substring(0, 10) === todayStr;
    var monthOk = !monthStr || String(monthStr).trim().substring(0, 7) === currentMon;

    return { dateOk: dateOk, monthOk: monthOk };
  } catch (e) {
    return { dateOk: true, monthOk: true }; // non-fatal — don't block on error
  }
}


function generateSessionToken(userId) {
  const timestamp = new Date().getTime();
  const random = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2);
  const raw = userId + timestamp + random;
  return Utilities.base64Encode(raw);
}

function createSession(userId) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const token = generateSessionToken(userId);
  const sessionKey = 'SESSION_' + userId.toUpperCase();
  
  props.setProperty(sessionKey, token);
  props.setProperty(sessionKey + '_TIME', new Date().getTime().toString());
  
  return token;
}
// ── Session Validator — sensitive functions ke liye ───────────
// SESSION_TIMEOUT: 8 hours (28800000 ms)
function validateSession(userId, token) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    token  = String(token  || '').trim();
    if (!userId || !token) return { valid: false, reason: 'Missing credentials' };

    var props      = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var sessionKey = 'SESSION_' + userId;
    var storedToken = props.getProperty(sessionKey);
    var storedTime  = props.getProperty(sessionKey + '_TIME');

    if (!storedToken || storedToken !== token) {
      return { valid: false, reason: 'Invalid session token. Please login again.' };
    }

    var elapsed = new Date().getTime() - parseInt(storedTime || '0');
    if (elapsed > SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS) {
      props.deleteProperty(sessionKey);
      props.deleteProperty(sessionKey + '_TIME');
      return { valid: false, reason: 'Session expired. Please login again.' };
    }

    // Refresh session time on activity
    props.setProperty(sessionKey + '_TIME', new Date().getTime().toString());
    return { valid: true };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('validateSession error: ' + e.toString());
    return { valid: false, reason: 'Session check error' };
  }
}
function clearSession(userId) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const sessionKey = 'SESSION_' + userId.toUpperCase();
  props.deleteProperty(sessionKey);
  props.deleteProperty(sessionKey + '_TIME');
}

// ✅ FIX M-3: Login Rate Limiter — brute force protection
// 5 failed attempts in 15 minutes → 30 minute lockout
var LOGIN_MAX_ATTEMPTS = 5;
var LOGIN_WINDOW_MS    = 15 * 60 * 1000;  // 15 minutes
var LOGIN_LOCKOUT_MS   = 30 * 60 * 1000;  // 30 minute lockout

function checkLoginLockout(userId) {
  try {
    var props   = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var key     = 'LOGIN_LOCK_' + userId.toUpperCase();
    var dataStr = props.getProperty(key);
    if (!dataStr) return { locked: false };

    var data = JSON.parse(dataStr);
    var now  = new Date().getTime();

    // Lockout active check
    if (data.lockedUntil && now < data.lockedUntil) {
      var minsLeft = Math.ceil((data.lockedUntil - now) / 60000);
      return { locked: true, message: '🔒 Account temporarily locked. Try again in ' + minsLeft + ' minutes.' };
    }

    // Window expire ho gaya — reset
    if (data.windowStart && (now - data.windowStart) > LOGIN_WINDOW_MS) {
      props.deleteProperty(key);
      return { locked: false };
    }

    return { locked: false };
  } catch (e) {
    return { locked: false }; // Error pe block mat karo
  }
}

function recordFailedLogin(userId) {
  try {
    var props   = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var key     = 'LOGIN_LOCK_' + userId.toUpperCase();
    var now     = new Date().getTime();
    var dataStr = props.getProperty(key);
    var data    = dataStr ? JSON.parse(dataStr) : { attempts: [], windowStart: now };

    // Window expire check — fresh start
    if ((now - (data.windowStart || now)) > LOGIN_WINDOW_MS) {
      data = { attempts: [], windowStart: now };
    }

    data.attempts.push(now);

    if (data.attempts.length >= LOGIN_MAX_ATTEMPTS) {
      data.lockedUntil = now + LOGIN_LOCKOUT_MS;
      Logger.log('🔒 Account locked for 30 min: ' + userId);
    }

    props.setProperty(key, JSON.stringify(data));
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('recordFailedLogin error: ' + e.toString());
  }
}

function clearLoginLockout(userId) {
  try {
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties()
      .deleteProperty('LOGIN_LOCK_' + userId.toUpperCase());
  } catch (e) {}
}

function logFailedLogin(userId, reason) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sh = ss.getSheetByName('FAILED_LOGINS');
    
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('FAILED_LOGINS');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([
        ['Timestamp', 'User ID', 'Reason', 'IP']
      ]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#dc3545')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    sh.appendRow([
      new Date(),
      userId,
      reason,
      ''
    ]);
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Failed login log error: ' + e.toString());
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔐 ENHANCED LOGIN SYSTEM
// ============================================
function login(userId, password) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim();
    password = String(password || '').trim();
    
    if (!userId || !password) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter User ID & Password' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX M-3: Brute force lockout check
    var lockCheck = checkLoginLockout(userId);
    if (lockCheck.locked) return { success: false, message: lockCheck.message };
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No users found' };
    
    // Read all columns including status
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      const uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      const storedHash = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
      const role = String(rows[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const branchCode = String(rows[i][3] || '').trim(); // ✅ ADDED - Column D
      const status = String(rows[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (uid.toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        // Check if account is active
        if (status !== 'ACTIVE') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }
        
        // ✅ FIX: Use stored uid (uppercase) as salt — consistent with credential creation
        const inputHashSalted = hashPassword(password, uid);
        const pwdOk = (inputHashSalted === storedHash);

        if (!pwdOk) {
          logFailedLogin(userId, 'Invalid password');
          recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3: Brute force counter
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }

        
        if (['OPERATOR', 'SUPERVISOR'].indexOf(role) >= 0) {
          return { success: false, message: 'Use appropriate login portal' };
        }
        
        const token = createSession(userId);
        const profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
        // ✅ ADD THIS - Get day status for supervisor
        let dayStatus = 'CLOSED';
        if (role === 'SUPERVISOR') {
          dayStatus = getSupervisorDayStatus(branchCode);
        }
        // ✅ ADDED - Get member branch info
        const branchInfo = getMemberBranchInfo(userId);
        
        logActivity(userId, 'LOGIN', 'Member logged in');
        
        return {
          success: true,
          userId: uid,
          name: profile ? profile.name : uid,
          token: token,
          isHoliday:      holidayCheck.isHoliday || false,
          holidayWarning: holidayCheck.isHoliday ? '🏖️ Aaj Holiday hai: ' + (holidayCheck.description || 'Office Holiday') + '\nEmergency kaam ke liye logged in hain.' : null,
          branchCode: branchInfo.success ? branchInfo.branchCode : branchCode, // ✅ ADDED
          branchName: branchInfo.success ? branchInfo.branchName : branchCode, // ✅ ADDED
          dayStatus: dayStatus ,
          profile: profile
        };
      }
    }
    
    logFailedLogin(userId, 'User not found');
    recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3
    return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Login error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
function operatorLogin(userId, password) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim();
    password = String(password || '').trim();
    
    if (!userId || !password) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter credentials' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX M-3: Brute force lockout check
    var lockCheck = checkLoginLockout(userId);
    if (lockCheck.locked) return { success: false, message: lockCheck.message };
    // ✅ FIX 13: holidayCheck only runs after lockout check — not at global scope
    var holidayCheck = isHolidayToday();
    // ✅ FIX: Holiday pe block nahi — sirf warning flag return karo
    // Frontend Day Begin pe warning dikhayega, login hoga normally
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No users' };
    
    // Read all columns (User ID, Password Hash, Role, Branch Code, ..., Status)
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      const uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      const storedHash = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
      const role = String(rows[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const branchCode = String(rows[i][3] || '').trim(); // ✅ ADDED - Column D
      const status = String(rows[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (uid.toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        // Check if account is active
        if (status !== 'ACTIVE') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }
        
        // ✅ FIX: Use stored uid (uppercase) as salt — consistent with credential creation
        const inputHashSalted = hashPassword(password, uid);
        const pwdOk = (inputHashSalted === storedHash);

        if (!pwdOk) {
          logFailedLogin(userId, 'Invalid password (Operator)');
          recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }


        if (role !== 'OPERATOR') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' }; // ✅ FIX: role leak removed
        }
        
        const token = createSession(userId);
        
        logActivity(userId, 'OPERATOR_LOGIN', 'Operator logged in');

        // ✅ FEATURE 1: Check if operator has open counter from previous day
        const counterStatus = getLastCounterStatus(uid);

        // BUG FIX: Also check branch day status - previous day open?
        var branchDayStatus = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
        var branchPrevDay   = branchDayStatus.started && branchDayStatus.isPreviousDay;

        // mustCloseFirst = true if counter open from prev day OR branch day open from prev day
        var mustCloseCounter = counterStatus.hasOpen && (counterStatus.isPreviousDay || branchPrevDay);

        return {
          success:            true,
          userId:             uid,
          role:               'OPERATOR',
          name:               uid,
          token:              token,
          isHoliday:          holidayCheck.isHoliday || false,
          holidayWarning:     holidayCheck.isHoliday ? '🏖️ Aaj Holiday hai: ' + (holidayCheck.description || 'Office Holiday') + '\nEmergency kaam ke liye logged in hain.' : null,
          branchCode:         branchCode,
          branchName:         branchCode,
          hasOpenCounter:     counterStatus.hasOpen,
          counterDate:        counterStatus.dateDisplay || '',
          isPreviousDay:      counterStatus.isPreviousDay || false,
          branchPreviousDay:  branchPrevDay,
          mustCloseFirst:     mustCloseCounter,
          openDayDate:        branchDayStatus.dayDateDisplay || ''
        };
      }
    }
    
    logFailedLogin(userId, 'Operator not found');
    recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3
    return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Operator login error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
function supervisorLogin(userId, password) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim();
    password = String(password || '').trim();
    
    if (!userId || !password) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter credentials' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX M-3: Brute force lockout check
    var lockCheck = checkLoginLockout(userId);
    if (lockCheck.locked) return { success: false, message: lockCheck.message };
    // ✅ FIX 13: holidayCheck only runs after lockout check — not at global scope
    var holidayCheck = isHolidayToday();
    // ✅ FIX: Holiday pe block nahi — sirf warning flag return karo
    // Frontend Day Begin pe warning dikhayega, login hoga normally
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No users' };
    
    // Read all columns including status
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      const uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      const storedHash = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
      const role = String(rows[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const branchCode = String(rows[i][3] || '').trim(); // ✅ ADDED - Column D
      const status = String(rows[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (uid.toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        // Check if account is active
        if (status !== 'ACTIVE') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }
        
        // ✅ FIX: Use stored uid (uppercase) as salt — consistent with credential creation
        const inputHashSalted = hashPassword(password, uid);
        const pwdOk = (inputHashSalted === storedHash);

        if (!pwdOk) {
          logFailedLogin(userId, 'Invalid password (Supervisor)');
          recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }


        if (role !== 'SUPERVISOR') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' }; // ✅ FIX: role leak removed
        }
        
        const token = createSession(userId);
        
        logActivity(userId, 'SUPERVISOR_LOGIN', 'Supervisor logged in');

        // ✅ FEATURE 1: Get full day status — date independent
        const dayStatusResult = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
        const dayStatus       = dayStatusResult.started ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSED';
        const isPreviousDay   = dayStatusResult.isPreviousDay || false;
        const openDayDate     = dayStatusResult.dayDateDisplay || '';

        return {
          success:       true,
          userId:        uid,
          role:          'SUPERVISOR',
          name:          uid,
          token:         token,
          isHoliday:     holidayCheck.isHoliday || false,
          holidayWarning: holidayCheck.isHoliday ? '🏖️ Aaj Holiday hai: ' + (holidayCheck.description || 'Office Holiday') + '\nEmergency kaam ke liye logged in hain.' : null,
          branchCode:    branchCode,
          branchName:    branchCode,
          dayStatus:     dayStatus,
          isPreviousDay: isPreviousDay,   // ✅ true = previous day still open
          openDayDate:   openDayDate,     // ✅ e.g. "20/02/2026"
          mustCloseFirst: isPreviousDay   // ✅ show only Day End option
        };
      }
    }
    
    logFailedLogin(userId, 'Supervisor not found');
    recordFailedLogin(userId); // ✅ FIX M-3
    return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Supervisor login error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// ðŸ“ PENDING ENTRIES SYSTEM
// ============================================
function savePendingEntry(entryType, entryData, operatorId) {
  try {
    // ✅ VALIDATION: Operator ID check
    if (!operatorId || operatorId === '' || operatorId === 'null' || operatorId === 'undefined') {
      Logger.log('❌ CRITICAL: savePendingEntry called with invalid operator ID');
      Logger.log('Entry Type: ' + entryType);
      Logger.log('Operator ID received: ' + operatorId);
      
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ CRITICAL ERROR: Operator ID is missing!\n\n' +
                 'This entry cannot be submitted without operator identification.\n\n' +
                 'Please contact administrator if this error persists.'
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ GET OPERATOR BRANCH CODE
    Logger.log('=== Getting branch code for operator: ' + operatorId);
    const operatorInfo = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    
    if (!operatorInfo || !operatorInfo.success) {
      Logger.log('❌ ERROR: Could not get branch code for operator: ' + operatorId);
      Logger.log('Error: ' + (operatorInfo ? operatorInfo.message : 'Unknown'));
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Could not determine operator branch. Please contact administrator.'
      };
    }
    
    const branchCode = operatorInfo.branchCode;
    Logger.log('✅ Operator branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    // Create sheet if doesn't exist
    if (!sh) {
      Logger.log('Creating PENDING_ENTRIES sheet with branch code column');
      sh = ss.insertSheet('PENDING_ENTRIES');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([
        ['Entry ID', 'Type', 'Data (JSON)', 'Operator', 'Submitted', 'Status', 'Supervisor Notes', 'Branch Code']
      ]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#ff9800')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    const entryId = 'PE' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    const dataJSON = JSON.stringify(entryData);
    
    // ✅ LOG: Backend confirmation
    Logger.log('✅ Saving pending entry:');
    Logger.log('  Entry ID: ' + entryId);
    Logger.log('  Type: ' + entryType);
    Logger.log('  Operator: ' + operatorId);
    Logger.log('  Branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    // ✅ SAVE WITH BRANCH CODE (Column 8)
    sh.appendRow([
      entryId,           // Column 1: Entry ID
      entryType,         // Column 2: Type
      dataJSON,          // Column 3: Data (JSON)
      operatorId,        // Column 4: Operator
      new Date(),        // Column 5: Submitted
      'PENDING',         // Column 6: Status
      '',                // Column 7: Supervisor Notes
      branchCode         // Column 8: Branch Code ✅
    ]);
    
    logActivity(operatorId, 'PENDING_ENTRY', entryType + ' submitted for approval (ID: ' + entryId + ', Branch: ' + branchCode + ')');
    
    Logger.log('✅ Entry saved successfully to PENDING_ENTRIES sheet');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Entry submitted for supervisor approval!',
      entryId: entryId,
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Save pending entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Get All Pending Entries (Supervisor)
 */
function getPendingEntries(supervisorId) {
  try {
    // ✅ ADDED: Input validation
    if (!supervisorId) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: supervisorId is missing');
      return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID is required' };
    }
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: USER_DETAILS sheet not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'USER_DETAILS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Get supervisor's branch code
    let supervisorBranch = '';
    const userData = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, Math.max(1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1), 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < userData.length; i++) {
      if (String(userData[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(supervisorId).toUpperCase()) {
        supervisorBranch = String(userData[i][3] || ''); // Column D - Branch Code
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (!supervisorBranch) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: Branch code not found for supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found for supervisor ' + supervisorId };
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Supervisor: ' + supervisorId + ', Branch: ' + supervisorBranch);
    
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh) {
      Logger.log('INFO: PENDING_ENTRIES sheet does not exist yet');
      return { success: true, entries: [], supervisorBranch: supervisorBranch, count: 0 };
    }
    
    if (sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      Logger.log('INFO: No pending entries in sheet');
      return { success: true, entries: [], supervisorBranch: supervisorBranch, count: 0 };
    }
    
    // Get all columns including branch code
    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 8).getValues();
    const entries = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const status = String(data[i][5] || '').toUpperCase();
      const entryBranch = String(data[i][7] || ''); // Column H - Branch Code
      
      // ✅ FILTER: Only PENDING entries from SAME BRANCH
      if (status === 'PENDING' && entryBranch === supervisorBranch) {
        entries.push({
          rowIndex: i + 2,
          entryId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          type: String(data[i][1] || ''),
          dataJSON: String(data[i][2] || '{}'),
          operator: String(data[i][3] || ''),
          submitted: data[i][4] ? formatDate(data[i][4]) : '',
          status: String(data[i][5] || ''),
          notes: String(data[i][6] || ''),
          branchCode: entryBranch
        });
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Found ' + entries.length + ' pending entries for branch ' + supervisorBranch);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      entries: entries,
      supervisorBranch: supervisorBranch,
      count: entries.length
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Get pending entries error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'System error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
function getBranchCodeFromUser(userId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet || userSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return null;
    }
    
    const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(userId).toUpperCase()) {
        return String(data[i][3]); // Column D - Branch Code
      }
    }
    
    return null;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}

function getOperatorRejectedEntries(operatorId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, entries: [] };
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
    const entries = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const entryOperator = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const status = String(data[i][5] || '').toUpperCase();
      
      if (entryOperator === operatorId.toUpperCase() && status === 'REJECTED') {
        entries.push({
          rowIndex: i + 2,
          entryId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          type: String(data[i][1] || ''),
          dataJSON: String(data[i][2] || ''),
          operator: String(data[i][3] || ''),
          submitted: data[i][4] ? formatDate(data[i][4]) : '',
          status: String(data[i][5] || ''),
          notes: String(data[i][6] || '')
        });
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, entries: entries };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get rejected entries error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function deleteRejectedEntry(rowIndex, operatorId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found' };
    
    const entryOperator = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 4).getValue();
    if (String(entryOperator || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== operatorId.toUpperCase()) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Not authorized to delete this entry' };
    }
    
    const entryId = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1).getValue();
    
    sh.deleteRow(rowIndex);
    
    logActivity(operatorId, 'DELETE_REJECTED', 'Deleted rejected entry: ' + entryId);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Rejected entry deleted successfully!'
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Delete rejected entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 📊 SUPERVISOR - TODAY'S ENTRIES DELETE - FIXED
// ============================================

function getDateColumnIndex(sheetName) {
  var dateColumns = {
    'ACCOUNT OPEN': 3,
    'DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT': 5,
    'SAVINGS MANAGEMENT': 6,   
    'LOAN MANAGEMENT': 6,
    'LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION': 6,
    'ACCOUNT CLOSE': 3
  };
  
  return dateColumns[sheetName] !== undefined ? dateColumns[sheetName] : -1;
}

function getTodaysEntries(sheetName, supervisorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('🔍 getTodaysEntries - Sheet: ' + sheetName + ', Supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
    
    if (!supervisorId || !isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only supervisors can view/delete entries', entries: [] };
    }
    
    if (!sheetName || typeof sheetName !== 'string' || sheetName.trim() === '') {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid sheet name', entries: [] };
    }
    
    sheetName = sheetName.trim();
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found: ' + sheetName, entries: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, entries: [], message: 'No data in sheet' };
    }
    
    var dateColIndex = getDateColumnIndex(sheetName);
    if (dateColIndex === -1) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No date column configured for this sheet', entries: [] };
    }
    
    var lastCol = sh.getLastColumn();
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol).getValues();
    
    var today = new Date();
    today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var todayTime = today.getTime();
    
    var entries = [];
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var cellValue = data[i][dateColIndex];
      
      if (cellValue && cellValue instanceof Date) {
        var entryDate = new Date(cellValue);
        entryDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        
        if (entryDate.getTime() === todayTime) {
          var rowData = [];
          for (var j = 0; j < data[i].length; j++) {
            if (data[i][j] instanceof Date) {
              rowData.push(Utilities.formatDate(data[i][j], Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy'));
            } else if (data[i][j] === null || data[i][j] === undefined) {
              rowData.push('');
            } else {
              rowData.push(String(data[i][j]));
            }
          }
          
          entries.push({
            rowIndex: i + 2,
            data: rowData,
            canEdit: false,
            canDelete: true
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Found ' + entries.length + ' today\'s entries');
    return { success: true, entries: entries, sheetName: sheetName };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString(), entries: [] };
  }
}

function isSupervisor(userId) {
  try {
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh) return false;
    
    var last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return false;
    
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 3).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var role = String(rows[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (uid === userId.toUpperCase() && role === 'SUPERVISOR') {
        return true;
      }
    }
    
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('isSupervisor error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

function deleteEntry(sheetName, rowIndex, supervisorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('🗑️ DELETE - Sheet: "' + sheetName + '", Row: ' + rowIndex + ', Supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
    
    sheetName = String(sheetName || '').trim();
    rowIndex = parseInt(rowIndex);
    
    if (!sheetName || sheetName === '' || sheetName === 'undefined') {
      Logger.log('❌ Invalid sheet name');
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid sheet name' };
    }
    
    if (isNaN(rowIndex) || rowIndex < 2) {
      Logger.log('❌ Invalid row: ' + rowIndex);
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid row number' };
    }
    
    if (!supervisorId || !isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only supervisors can delete entries' };
    }
    
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    
    if (!sh) {
      Logger.log('❌ Sheet not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found: ' + sheetName };
    }
    
    var dateColIndex = getDateColumnIndex(sheetName);
    Logger.log('📅 Date column index: ' + dateColIndex);
    
    if (dateColIndex >= 0) {
      var entryDate = sh.getRange(rowIndex, dateColIndex + 1).getValue();
      Logger.log('📆 Entry date: ' + entryDate);
      
      if (!entryDate || !(entryDate instanceof Date)) {
        return { success: false, message: 'No valid date found in this row' };
      }
      
      var today = new Date();
      today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      
      var entry = new Date(entryDate);
      entry.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      
      if (entry.getTime() !== today.getTime()) {
        return { 
          success: false, 
          message: '❌ Only today\'s entries can be deleted!\n\nEntry date: ' + 
                   Utilities.formatDate(entry, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
        };
      }
    }
    
    try {
      logDeletedEntry(sheetName, rowIndex, supervisorId);
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Backup failed: ' + e);
    }
    
    sh.deleteRow(rowIndex);
    Logger.log('✅ Row ' + rowIndex + ' deleted by supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
    
    logActivity(supervisorId, 'DELETE_ENTRY', sheetName + ' Row ' + rowIndex + ' deleted');
    
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Entry deleted successfully!' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Exception: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function logDeletedEntry(sheetName, rowIndex, supervisorId) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var src = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    var audit = ss.getSheetByName('DELETED_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!audit) {
      audit = ss.insertSheet('DELETED_ENTRIES');
      audit.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setValues([
        ['Deleted Date', 'Sheet', 'Data', 'Supervisor', 'Reason', 'Row']
      ]);
      audit.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#dc3545')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    var data = src.getRange(rowIndex, 1, 1, src.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    audit.appendRow([
      new Date(), 
      sheetName, 
      JSON.stringify(data), 
      supervisorId, 
      'Same-day deletion by supervisor', 
      rowIndex
    ]);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Audit error: ' + e);
  }
}
// ============================================
// ✏️ FIX #7: MODIFY REJECTED ENTRIES
// ============================================

/**
 * Get rejected entry data for modification
 * @param {number} rowIndex - Row index in PENDING_ENTRIES sheet
 * @param {string} operatorId - Operator ID requesting modification
 * @returns {object} - Entry data for pre-filling form
 */
function getRejectedEntryForModification(rowIndex, operatorId) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'PENDING_ENTRIES sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Get entry data
    var entryData = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1, 1, 7).getValues()[0];
    
    var entryId = String(entryData[0] || '');
    var type = String(entryData[1] || '');
    var dataJSON = String(entryData[2] || '');
    var operator = String(entryData[3] || '');
    var submitted = entryData[4];
    var status = String(entryData[5] || '');
    var notes = String(entryData[6] || '');
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.1: Verify operator owns this entry
    if (operator.toUpperCase() !== operatorId.toUpperCase()) {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: '⚠️ Access Denied\n\nYou can only modify your own rejected entries.' 
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.2: Verify entry is rejected
    if (status.toUpperCase() !== 'REJECTED') {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'Entry is not in REJECTED status' 
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.3: Parse entry data
    var data = {};
    try {
      data = JSON.parse(dataJSON);
    } catch (e) {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'Failed to parse entry data' 
      };
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Retrieved rejected entry for modification');
    Logger.log('   Entry ID: ' + entryId);
    Logger.log('   Type: ' + type);
    Logger.log('   Operator: ' + operator);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      entry: {
        rowIndex: rowIndex,
        entryId: entryId,
        type: type,
        data: data,
        operator: operator,
        submitted: Utilities.formatDate(submitted, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm'),
        rejectionNotes: notes
      }
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Get rejected entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Update rejected entry with modified data and resubmit
 * @param {number} rowIndex - Row index in PENDING_ENTRIES sheet
 * @param {object} modifiedData - Modified entry data
 * @param {string} operatorId - Operator ID resubmitting
 * @returns {object} - Success status
 */
function resubmitModifiedEntry(rowIndex, modifiedData, operatorId) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'PENDING_ENTRIES sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.4: Verify operator owns this entry
    var currentOperator = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 4).getValue();
    if (String(currentOperator).toUpperCase() !== operatorId.toUpperCase()) {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'Access denied: You can only modify your own entries' 
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.5: Update entry with modified data
    var newDataJSON = JSON.stringify(modifiedData);
    var newSubmitTime = new Date();
    
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 3).setValue(newDataJSON);      // Column C: Data (JSON)
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 5).setValue(newSubmitTime);    // Column E: Submitted
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 6).setValue('PENDING');        // Column F: Status (reset to PENDING)
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 7).setValue('Modified and resubmitted by operator'); // Column G: Notes
    
    var entryId = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1).getValue();
    var entryType = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 2).getValue();
    
    Logger.log('✅ Entry modified and resubmitted');
    Logger.log('   Entry ID: ' + entryId);
    Logger.log('   Type: ' + entryType);
    Logger.log('   Operator: ' + operatorId);
    
    // ✅ FIX 7.6: Log activity
    logActivity(operatorId, 'MODIFY_RESUBMIT', entryType + ' entry modified and resubmitted (ID: ' + entryId + ')');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ Entry Modified & Resubmitted!\n\n' +
               'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n' +
               'Type: ' + entryType + '\n\n' +
               'Status: Pending supervisor approval\n' +
               'Your modified entry is now in the approval queue.',
      entryId: entryId
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Resubmit modified entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function createNotification(userId, message, type) {
try {
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
var sh = ss.getSheetByName('NOTIFICATIONS');
if (!sh) {
  sh = ss.insertSheet('NOTIFICATIONS');
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['User ID', 'Message', 'Type', 'Date', 'Status']]);
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
}

var today = new Date();
sh.appendRow([userId, message, type, today, 'UNREAD']);

return { success: true };
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Create notification error: ' + e.toString());
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}
function getNotifications(userId) {
try {
userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
var sh = ss.getSheetByName('NOTIFICATIONS');
if (!sh) {
  sh = ss.insertSheet('NOTIFICATIONS');
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['User ID', 'Message', 'Type', 'Date', 'Status']]);
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
  return { success: true, notifications: [] };
}

var last = sh.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return { success: true, notifications: [] };

var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 5).getValues();
var notifications = [];

for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
  var notifUserId = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  
  if (notifUserId === userId) {
    notifications.push({
      rowIndex: i + 2,
      userId: String(rows[i][0] || ''),
      message: String(rows[i][1] || ''),
      type: String(rows[i][2] || ''),
      date: rows[i][3] ? formatDate(rows[i][3]) : '',
      status: String(rows[i][4] || 'UNREAD')
    });
  }
}

notifications.sort(function(a, b) {
  return b.rowIndex - a.rowIndex;
});

return { success: true, notifications: notifications };
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Get notifications error: ' + e.toString());
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}
function markAllNotificationsRead(userId) {
try {
userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
var sh = ss.getSheetByName('NOTIFICATIONS');
if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'NOTIFICATIONS sheet not found' };

var last = sh.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return { success: true };

var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 5).getValues();

for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
  var notifUserId = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  
  if (notifUserId === userId) {
    sh.getRange(i + 2, 5).setValue('READ');
  }
}

return { success: true };
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Mark all notifications read error: ' + e.toString());
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}
function sendDailyDepositEmails() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName("DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT");
    if (!sh) return;

    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return;

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 9).getValues();
    var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM/DD/yyyy");

    var count = 0;

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      var entryDate = row[5];
      var userId = (row[8] || "").toString().trim();
      var amount = row[2];

      if (!entryDate || !(entryDate instanceof Date)) continue;

      var formattedDate = Utilities.formatDate(entryDate, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM/DD/yyyy");

      if (formattedDate === today && userId && amount > 0) {
        var depositData = {
          accountNo: row[0],
          name: row[1],
          amount: row[2],
          currentBalance: row[4],
          monthFor: row[6],
          date : row[5],
          userId: userId
        };

        sendDepositEmail(userId, depositData);
        count++;
      }
    }

    Logger.log("TOTAL EMAILS SENT: " + count);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Error: " + err);
  }
}

function sendDepositEmail(userId, depositData) {
  try {
    var profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
    if (!profile || !profile.email) return;

    var subject = '✅ Deposit Confirmation - DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION';
    var body =
      'Dear ' + profile.name + ',\n\n' +
      'Your deposit has been successfully recorded.\n\n' +
      '📌 Deposit Details:\n' +
      '--------------------------------\n' +
      'Amount: ₹' + (depositData.amount || 0) + '\n' +
      'Current Balance: ₹' + (depositData.currentBalance || 0) + '\n' +
      'Date: ' + (depositData.date || '') + '\n' +
      '--------------------------------\n\n' +
      'Thank you for your continued trust in DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION.\n\n' +
      'Regards,\n' +
      'Team DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION\n\n' +
      '📧 Email: xxxxxxxxxxxxx\n' +
      '📞 Contact: +91-XXXXXXXXXX';

    MailApp.sendEmail(profile.email, subject, body);
    Logger.log('Email sent to: ' + profile.email);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("Email Error: " + e);
  }
}

// ================================================================
// ✅ DEPOSIT CONFIRMATION EMAIL — Auto-trigger on approval
// Called from saveDepositEntry() after supervisor approves
// ================================================================
function sendDepositConfirmationEmail(data) {
  try {
    var email = String(data.email || '').trim();
    if (!email || email.indexOf('@') === -1) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Deposit email skipped — no valid email for: ' + (data.userId || ''));
      return;
    }

    var name       = String(data.name       || 'Member');
    var accountNo  = String(data.accountNo  || 'N/A');
    var amount     = parseFloat(data.amount)    || 0;
    var interest   = parseFloat(data.interest)  || 0;
    var newBalance = parseFloat(data.newBalance) || 0;
    var tz         = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var date       = data.date     ? String(data.date)    : Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
    var monthFor   = data.monthFor ? String(data.monthFor): '';
    var branchCode = data.branchCode ? String(data.branchCode) : '';
    var webAppUrl  = ScriptApp.getService().getUrl();

    var subject = 'Deposit Confirmed - Rs.' + amount.toFixed(2) + ' | ' + accountNo;

    var lines = [
      'Dear ' + name + ',',
      '',
      'Your deposit has been APPROVED and recorded successfully.',
      '',
      '----------------------------------------',
      '         DEPOSIT CONFIRMATION',
      '----------------------------------------',
      '',
      'Account Number  : ' + accountNo,
      'Deposit Amount  : Rs.' + amount.toFixed(2)
    ];

    if (interest > 0) {
      lines.push('Interest Added  : Rs.' + interest.toFixed(2));
    }

    lines.push('Updated Balance : Rs.' + newBalance.toFixed(2));
    lines.push('Date            : ' + date);

    if (monthFor) {
      lines.push('Month For       : ' + monthFor);
    }
    if (branchCode) {
      lines.push('Branch          : ' + branchCode);
    }

    lines.push('');
    lines.push('----------------------------------------');
    lines.push('');
    lines.push('View your account: ' + webAppUrl);
    lines.push('');
    lines.push('Thank you for your continued trust in DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION.');
    lines.push('');
    lines.push('If you did not make this deposit, contact your branch immediately.');
    lines.push('');
    lines.push('Best Regards,');
    lines.push('Team DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION');
    lines.push('Contact: +91-XXXXXXXXXX | Email: xxxxxxxxxxxxx');

    var body = lines.join('\n');

    MailApp.sendEmail(email, subject, body);
    Logger.log('Deposit confirmation email sent to: ' + email + ' | Account: ' + accountNo + ' | Rs.' + amount.toFixed(2));

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('sendDepositConfirmationEmail error: ' + e.toString());
    // Non-fatal — deposit already saved
  }
}


function sendBirthdayWishes() {
  // ✅ FIX 12: Branch filter added — sirf current branch ke members ko email jaye
  try {
    var ss   = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh   = ss.getSheetByName("ACCOUNT OPEN");
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return "No accounts found";

    var data  = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "Asia/Kolkata", "dd/MM");
    var sentCount = 0;

    data.forEach(function(row) {
      var dob        = row[11]; // Col L
      var email      = row[8];  // Col I
      var name       = row[1];  // Col B
      var status     = String(row[7]  || '').toUpperCase().trim(); // Col H
      var branchCode = String(row[12] || '').trim();               // Col M

      // ✅ Skip inactive accounts and rows with no branch
      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') return;
      if (!dob || !email) return;

      try {
        var dobFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(dob), "Asia/Kolkata", "dd/MM");
        if (dobFormatted === today) {
          var subject = "🎉 Happy Birthday from DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION!";
          var body =
            "Dear " + name + ",\n\n" +
            '🎊 🎈 HAPPY BIRTHDAY! 🎈 🎊\n\n' +
            'Warmest Birthday Wishes,\n' +
            'Team DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION💜';
          MailApp.sendEmail(email, subject, body);
          sentCount++;
          Logger.log('🎂 Birthday email sent: ' + name + ' | Branch: ' + branchCode);
        }
      } catch (rowErr) {
        Logger.log('Birthday row error: ' + rowErr.toString());
      }
    });

    Logger.log('✅ Birthday emails sent: ' + sentCount);
    return "Birthday Emails Sent: " + sentCount;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('sendBirthdayWishes error: ' + e.toString());
    return "Error: " + e.toString();
  }
}
// ============================================
// 📅 UTILITY FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function formatDate(val) {
if (!val) return '';
if (val instanceof Date) {
return Utilities.formatDate(val, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy');
}
return String(val);
}
function _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId) {
try {
userId = (userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
var rows = _readSheetRangeSafe('ACCOUNT OPEN');
for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
  if (String(rows[i][9] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
    var photoUrl = String(rows[i][10] || '').trim();
    
    if (photoUrl && photoUrl.indexOf('drive.google.com') > -1) {
      photoUrl = getGoogleDriveImageUrl(photoUrl);
    }
    
    return {
      memberId: String(rows[i][0] || ''),
      name: String(rows[i][1] || ''),
      accountNo: String(rows[i][2] || ''),
      openDate: rows[i][3] ? formatDate(rows[i][3]) : '',
      accountType: String(rows[i][4] || ''),
      nominee: String(rows[i][5] || ''),
      relation: String(rows[i][6] || ''),
      status: String(rows[i][7] || ''),
      email: String(rows[i][8] || ''),
      userId: userId,
      photoUrl: photoUrl
    };
  }
}
return null;
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Error in _findAccountProfileByUserId: ' + e.toString());
return null;
}
}
function _readSheetRangeSafe(sheetName) {
try {
var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
if (!sh) return [];
var last = sh.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return [];
return sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues();
} catch (e) {
return [];
}
}
function getGoogleDriveImageUrl(driveUrl) {
  if (!driveUrl || driveUrl.trim() === '') return '';
  
  try {
    var fileId = '';
    var match1 = driveUrl.match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{25,})/);
    if (match1 && match1[1]) fileId = match1[1];
    
    if (!fileId) {
      var match2 = driveUrl.match(/[?&]id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{25,})/);
      if (match2 && match2[1]) fileId = match2[1];
    }
    
    if (!fileId) {
      var match3 = driveUrl.match(/open\?id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{25,})/);
      if (match3 && match3[1]) fileId = match3[1];
    }
    
    if (fileId) {
      return 'https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=' + fileId + '&sz=w400';
    }
    
    return driveUrl;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Error converting Drive URL: ' + e.toString());
    return driveUrl;
  }
}

function getUserData(userId) {
try {
userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
if (!userId) return { success: false, message: 'Missing userId' };
var profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
var deposits = [];
var depRows = _readSheetRangeSafe('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');

for (var d = 0; d < depRows.length; d++) {
  if (String(depRows[d][8] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
    deposits.push({
      accountNo: String(depRows[d][0] || ''),
      name: String(depRows[d][1] || ''),
      amount: depRows[d][2] || 0,
      interest: depRows[d][3] || 0,
      currentBalance: depRows[d][4] || 0,
      date: depRows[d][5] ? formatDate(depRows[d][5]) : '',
      monthFor: String(depRows[d][6] || '')
    });
  }
}

var loans = [];
var loanRows = _readSheetRangeSafe('LOAN MANAGEMENT');

for (var l = 0; l < loanRows.length; l++) {
  if (String(loanRows[l][13] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
    loans.push({
      memberId: String(loanRows[l][0] || ''),
      loanAccount: String(loanRows[l][1] || ''),
      name: String(loanRows[l][2] || ''),
      loanType: String(loanRows[l][3] || ''),
      roi: loanRows[l][4] || '',
      loanAmount: loanRows[l][5] || 0,
      loanDate: loanRows[l][6] ? formatDate(loanRows[l][6]) : '',
      monthlyEmi: loanRows[l][7] || '',
      totalPaid: loanRows[l][8] || 0,
      remaining: loanRows[l][9] || 0,
      loanStatus: String(loanRows[l][10] || ''),
      closedDate: loanRows[l][11] ? formatDate(loanRows[l][11]) : ''
    });
  }
}
var savings = [];
var savRows = _readSheetRangeSafe('SAVINGS MANAGEMENT');
for (var s = 0; s < savRows.length; s++) {
  if (String(savRows[s][8] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {  // Col I = UserId
    savings.push({
      accountNo:  String(savRows[s][0] || ''),
      amount:     savRows[s][2] || 0,
      txnType:    String(savRows[s][3] || 'DEPOSIT'),
      balance:    savRows[s][4] || 0,
      date:       savRows[s][5] ? formatDate(savRows[s][5]) : '',
      remarks:    String(savRows[s][6] || '')
    });
  }
}

return { success: true, data: { account: profile, deposits: deposits, loans: loans, savings: savings } };
} catch (e) {
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}


// ============================================
// 📧 PASSWORD RESET & OTHER MEMBER FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
/**
 * Send OTP to user's registered email
 * @param {string} userId - User ID requesting password reset
 * @returns {object} - Success status and message
 */
function sendOTP(userId) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX 1: Validate and normalize userId
    userId = String(userId || '').trim();
    
    if (!userId) {
      Logger.log('❌ sendOTP: Empty userId');
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter User ID' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 2: Normalize to uppercase for consistency
    userId = userId.toUpperCase();
    
    Logger.log('📧 Sending OTP for userId: ' + userId);
    
    // Find user's email from ACCOUNT OPEN sheet
    var profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
    
    if (!profile || !profile.email) {
      Logger.log('❌ User not found or no email: ' + userId);
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'User ID not found or no email registered' 
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 3: Generate 6-digit OTP
    var otp = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();
    var props  = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var otpKey = 'OTP_' + userId;
    var now    = new Date().getTime();

    // ✅ FIX H2a: Rate limiting — max 3 requests per hour
    var rateKey  = 'OTPRATE_' + userId;
    var rateData = { requests: [] };
    try {
      var rateStr = props.getProperty(rateKey);
      if (rateStr) rateData = JSON.parse(rateStr);
    } catch(re) {}
    var oneHourAgo = now - (60 * 60 * 1000);
    rateData.requests = (rateData.requests || []).filter(function(t){ return t > oneHourAgo; });
    if (rateData.requests.length >= 3) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Too many OTP requests. Please wait 1 hour and try again.' };
    }
    rateData.requests.push(now);
    props.setProperty(rateKey, JSON.stringify(rateData));

    // ✅ FIX H2b: Store OTP hash — never store plaintext OTP
    var otpHash = hashPassword(otp);
    var otpData = {
      otpHash:   otpHash,
      timestamp: now,
      userId:    userId,
      email:     profile.email
    };
    props.setProperty(otpKey, JSON.stringify(otpData));

    Logger.log('✅ OTP stored (hashed) with key: ' + otpKey);
    Logger.log('   Timestamp: ' + now);
    
    // ✅ FIX 5: Enhanced email with better formatting
    var subject = '🔐 DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION- Password Reset OTP';
    
    var body = 
      'Dear ' + profile.name + ',\n\n' +
      '━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n' +
      '       PASSWORD RESET REQUEST\n' +
      '━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n\n' +
      'Your One-Time Password (OTP) is:\n\n' +
      '       🔑  ' + otp + '  🔑\n\n' +
      '⏰ This OTP is valid for 10 minutes only.\n\n' +
      '⚠️ SECURITY WARNING:\n' +
      '   • Do NOT share this OTP with anyone\n' +
      '   • DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATIONwill NEVER ask for your OTP\n' +
      '   • If you did not request this, ignore this email\n\n' +
      '━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n' +
      'User ID: ' + userId + '\n' +
      'Generated: ' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') + '\n' +
      '━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n\n' +
      'Best Regards,\n' +
      'DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATIONTeam\n' +
      'STAY WITH US AND GROW WITH US\n\n' +
      '📧 Email: xxxxxxxxxxxxx\n' +
      '📞 Contact: +91-XXXXXXXXXX';
    
    // Send email
    try {
      MailApp.sendEmail(profile.email, subject, body);
      Logger.log('✅ OTP email sent to: ' + profile.email);
    } catch (emailError) {
      Logger.log('❌ Email sending failed: ' + emailError.toString());
      // Clean up stored OTP if email fails
      props.deleteProperty(otpKey);
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'Failed to send email. Please try again.' 
      };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 6: Mask email for security
    var maskedEmail = profile.email.replace(/(.{2})(.*)(@.)/, '$1***$3');
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      message: 'OTP sent successfully to: ' + maskedEmail 
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ sendOTP error: ' + e.toString());
    Logger.log('❌ Stack: ' + e.stack);
    return { 
      success: false, 
      message: 'Error: ' + e.message 
    };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔐 FIXED: Verify OTP and Reset Password
// ============================================

/**
 * Verify OTP and reset password
 * @param {string} userId - User ID
 * @param {string} otp - OTP entered by user
 * @param {string} newPassword - New password to set
 * @returns {object} - Success status and message
 */
function verifyOTPAndResetPassword(userId, otp, newPassword) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX 1: Validate inputs
    userId = String(userId || '').trim();
    otp = String(otp || '').trim();
    newPassword = String(newPassword || '');
    
    if (!userId || !otp || !newPassword) {
      Logger.log('❌ verifyOTP: Missing required fields');
      return { success: false, message: 'All fields required' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX 2: Normalize userId (same as sendOTP)
    userId = userId.toUpperCase();
    
    Logger.log('🔐 Verifying OTP for userId: ' + userId);
    // ✅ SECURITY: OTP value never logged — prevents log-based credential theft
    
    // ✅ FIX 3: Standardized property key (matches sendOTP)
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var otpKey = 'OTP_' + userId; // ✅ Always with underscore
    
    var otpDataStr = props.getProperty(otpKey);
    
    if (!otpDataStr) {
      Logger.log('❌ No OTP found for key: ' + otpKey);
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'OTP not found or expired. Please request a new OTP.' 
      };
    }
    
    // Parse stored OTP data
    var stored = JSON.parse(otpDataStr);
    
    Logger.log('✅ OTP data retrieved');
    // ✅ SECURITY: stored.otp NOT logged
    Logger.log('   Stored at: ' + stored.timestamp);
    
    // ✅ FIX 4: Enhanced expiry check
    var currentTime = new Date().getTime();
    var otpAge = (currentTime - stored.timestamp) / 1000 / 60; // Age in minutes
    
    Logger.log('   OTP age: ' + otpAge.toFixed(2) + ' minutes');
    
    if (otpAge > 10) {
      Logger.log('❌ OTP expired (age: ' + otpAge.toFixed(2) + ' min)');
      // Clean up expired OTP
      props.deleteProperty(otpKey);
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'OTP expired. Please request a new OTP.' 
      };
    }
    // ✅ FIX H2: Verify OTP hash — never compare plaintext
    var inputHash  = hashPassword(otp);
    var storedHash = stored.otpHash || (stored.otp ? hashPassword(stored.otp) : '');
    if (storedHash !== inputHash) {
      // ✅ FIX BRUTE FORCE: Attempt counter — max 5 tries then invalidate OTP
      stored.failedAttempts = (stored.failedAttempts || 0) + 1;
      if (stored.failedAttempts >= 5) {
        props.deleteProperty(otpKey);
        Logger.log('❌ OTP invalidated after 5 failed attempts for: ' + userId);
        return {
          success: false,
          message: '⛔ Too many wrong attempts. OTP invalidated. Please request a new OTP.'
        };
      }
      props.setProperty(otpKey, JSON.stringify(stored));
      Logger.log('❌ OTP mismatch (hash comparison) — attempt ' + stored.failedAttempts + '/5');
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Invalid OTP. ' + (5 - stored.failedAttempts) + ' attempt(s) remaining.'
      };
    }
    Logger.log('✅ OTP verified successfully');
    
    // ✅ FIX 6: Update password in CREDENTIALS sheet
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    
    if (!sh) {
      Logger.log('❌ CREDENTIALS sheet not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'System error: CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      Logger.log('❌ No users in CREDENTIALS');
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };
    }
    
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 2).getValues();
    var userFound = false;
    
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (uid === userId) {
        userFound = true;
        
        // ✅ FIX 7: Hash the new password before storing
        var hashedPassword = '';
        try {
          hashedPassword = hashPassword(newPassword, userId); // ✅ FIX: salt=userId
          Logger.log('✅ New password hashed');
        } catch (hashError) {
          Logger.log('❌ Password hashing failed: ' + hashError.toString());
          return { 
            success: false, 
            message: 'Failed to hash password: ' + hashError.message 
          };
        }
        
        // Update password in sheet
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(hashedPassword);
        Logger.log('✅ Password updated in CREDENTIALS sheet (row ' + (i + 2) + ')');
        
        // ✅ FIX 8: Clean up OTP after successful reset
        props.deleteProperty(otpKey);
        Logger.log('✅ OTP deleted after successful reset');
        
        // ✅ FIX 9: Send confirmation email
        try {
          var profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
          if (profile && profile.email) {
            var subject = '✅ DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION- Password Reset Successful';
            var body = 
              'Dear ' + profile.name + ',\n\n' +
              'Your password has been successfully reset.\n\n' +
              'User ID: ' + userId + '\n' +
              'Reset Time: ' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') + '\n\n' +
              'If you did not perform this action, please contact us immediately.\n\n' +
              'Best Regards,\n' +
              'DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATIONTeam';
            
            MailApp.sendEmail(profile.email, subject, body);
            Logger.log('✅ Confirmation email sent');
          }
        } catch (emailError) {
          Logger.log('⚠️ Confirmation email failed: ' + emailError.toString());
          // Don't fail the reset if email fails
        }
        
        return { 
          success: true, 
          message: 'Password reset successful! You can now login with your new password.' 
        };
      }
    }
    
    if (!userFound) {
      Logger.log('❌ User not found in CREDENTIALS: ' + userId);
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };
    }
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ verifyOTPAndResetPassword error: ' + e.toString());
    Logger.log('❌ Stack: ' + e.stack);
    return { 
      success: false, 
      message: 'Error: ' + e.message 
    };
  }
}
function changePasswordDirect(userId, newPassword) {
try {
userId = String(userId || '').trim();
newPassword = String(newPassword || '');
if (!userId || !newPassword) {
  return { success: false, message: 'Invalid request' };
}

var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
if (!sh) return { success: false, message: "Sheet 'CREDENTIALS' not found" };

var last = sh.getLastRow();
var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 2).getValues();

for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
  var uid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
  if (uid.toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
    sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(hashPassword(newPassword, userId));
    return { success: true, message: 'Password changed successfully!' };
  }
}
return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Change password error: ' + e.toString());
return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
}
}

// ✅ FIX M-1: changePasswordWithOldVerify — old password server-side verify karo
// Client memory mein password store karne ki zarurat nahi
function changePasswordWithOldVerify(userId, oldPassword, newPassword, token) {
  try {
    userId      = String(userId      || '').trim();
    oldPassword = String(oldPassword || '');
    newPassword = String(newPassword || '');

    if (!userId || !oldPassword || !newPassword) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid request' };
    }

    // Session validate karo
    var sess = validateSession(userId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };

    var last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };

    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 2).getValues();

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var uid        = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      var storedHash = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();

      if (uid.toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        // Old password verify karo
        if (hashPassword(oldPassword, userId) !== storedHash) { // ✅ FIX: salt=userId
          logFailedLogin(userId, 'Change password: wrong old password');
          return { success: false, message: 'Old password is incorrect' };
        }

        if (oldPassword === newPassword) {
          return { success: false, message: 'New password must be different from old password' };
        }

        sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(hashPassword(newPassword, userId));
        logActivity(userId, 'PASSWORD_CHANGED', 'Password changed via self-service');
        Logger.log('✅ Password changed for: ' + userId);
        return { success: true, message: 'Password changed successfully!' };
      }
    }

    return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('changePasswordWithOldVerify error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
