/**
 * Clean up all stored OTPs (utility function — admin use only)
 */
function cleanupAllOTPs() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var allProps = props.getProperties();
  var cleaned = 0;
  
  for (var key in allProps) {
    if (key.indexOf('OTP_') === 0) {
      props.deleteProperty(key);
      Logger.log('🗑️ Deleted: ' + key);
      cleaned++;
    }
  }
  
  Logger.log('✅ Cleaned up ' + cleaned + ' OTP entries');
}

function generateDepositStatement(userId) {
try {
userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
var profile = _findAccountProfileByUserId(userId);
if (!profile) return { success: false, message: 'Profile not found' };
var deposits = [];
var depRows = _readSheetRangeSafe('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
for (var d = 0; d < depRows.length; d++) {
if (String(depRows[d][8] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
deposits.push({
accountNo: String(depRows[d][0] || ''),
name: String(depRows[d][1] || ''),
amount: depRows[d][2] || 0,
interest: depRows[d][3] || 0,
currentBalance: depRows[d][4] || 0,
date: depRows[d][5] ? formatDate(depRows[d][5]) : '',
monthFor: String(depRows[d][6] || '')
});
}
}
return {
success: true,
profile: profile,
deposits: deposits,
generatedDate: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss')
};
} catch (e) {
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}
function getAnnouncements() {
try {
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
if (!sh) {
  sh = ss.insertSheet('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['ID', 'Title', 'Message', 'Date', 'Status']]);
  sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
  return { success: true, announcements: [] };
}

var last = sh.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return { success: true, announcements: [] };

var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 5).getValues();
var announcements = [];

for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
  if (String(rows[i][4] || '').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
    announcements.push({
      id: String(rows[i][0] || ''),
      title: String(rows[i][1] || ''),
      message: String(rows[i][2] || ''),
      date: rows[i][3] ? formatDate(rows[i][3]) : ''
    });
  }
}

return { success: true, announcements: announcements };
} catch (e) {
Logger.log('Get announcements error: ' + e.toString());
return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
}
}

/**
 * Get announcements for staff (Operator/Supervisor)
 * Filters by target: ALL, ALL_STAFF, ALL_OPERATORS, ALL_SUPERVISORS
 */
function getAnnouncementsForStaff(role) {
  try {
    role = String(role || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, announcements: [] };

    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    var announcements = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var status = String(rows[i][4] || '').toUpperCase();
      var target = String(rows[i][5] || 'ALL').toUpperCase(); // Column F: Target

      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;

      var show = (target === 'ALL' || target === 'ALL_STAFF');
      if (role === 'OPERATOR' && target === 'ALL_OPERATORS') show = true;
      if (role === 'SUPERVISOR' && target === 'ALL_SUPERVISORS') show = true;

      if (show) {
        announcements.push({
          id: String(rows[i][0] || ''),
          title: String(rows[i][1] || ''),
          message: String(rows[i][2] || ''),
          date: rows[i][3] ? formatDate(rows[i][3]) : ''
        });
      }
    }

    return { success: true, announcements: announcements };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get staff announcements error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// MEMBER ENTRY FORM - BACKEND FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function getNextMemberId() {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }

  try {
    var ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh    = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

    // ── Step 1: Last approved member ID ──
    var lastApproved = 100000; // default start - 1

    if (sh && sh.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var colA = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < colA.length; i++) {
        var num = parseInt(String(colA[i][0] || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(num) && num > lastApproved) lastApproved = num;
      }
    }

    // ── Step 2: PENDING mein reserved member IDs ──
    var pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    var reservedNums = [];

    if (pendingSheet && pendingSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var pData = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      for (var p = 0; p < pData.length; p++) {
        var pStatus = String(pData[p][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        var pType   = String(pData[p][1] || '').toUpperCase();
        if (pStatus === 'PENDING' && pType === 'MEMBER_ENTRY') {
          try {
            var pJson   = JSON.parse(String(pData[p][2] || '{}'));
            var pMembId = parseInt(String(pJson.memberId || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(pMembId) && pMembId > 0) reservedNums.push(pMembId);
          } catch (je) {}
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Step 3: PropertiesService reserved ──
    var propReserved = props.getProperty('RESERVED_MEMBER_IDS');
    if (propReserved) {
      try { reservedNums = reservedNums.concat(JSON.parse(propReserved)); } catch (pe) {}
    }

    // ── Step 4: Next available ──
    var candidate = lastApproved + 1;
    var allUsed   = reservedNums.concat([lastApproved]);
    while (allUsed.indexOf(candidate) !== -1) { candidate++; }

    if (candidate > 999999) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID limit reached (999999).' };
    }

    // ── Step 5: Reserve karo ──
    var currentReserved = [];
    try { currentReserved = JSON.parse(props.getProperty('RESERVED_MEMBER_IDS') || '[]'); } catch (e) {}
    currentReserved.push(candidate);
    if (currentReserved.length > 100) currentReserved = currentReserved.slice(-100);
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_MEMBER_IDS', JSON.stringify(currentReserved));

    var nextId = String(candidate).padStart(6, '0');
    Logger.log('✅ getNextMemberId: ' + nextId);
    return { success: true, nextId: nextId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getNextMemberId error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

/**
 * Check if User ID already exists
 */
function checkUserIdExists(userId) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    if (!userId) {
      return { exists: false };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { exists: false };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { exists: false };
    }
    
    var userIds = sh.getRange(2, 4, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues(); // Column D (User ID)
    
    for (var i = 0; i < userIds.length; i++) {
      var existingUserId = String(userIds[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (existingUserId === userId) {
        return { exists: true };
      }
    }
    
    return { exists: false };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Check user ID error: ' + e.toString());
    return { exists: false };
  }
}


function addMemberCredentials(userId, branchCode) {
  try {
    userId     = String(userId     || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();

    if (!userId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User ID empty' };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sh = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');

    // CREDENTIALS sheet banao agar nahi hai
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('CREDENTIALS');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([[
        'User ID', 'Password', 'Role', 'Branch Code', 'Status'
      ]]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#4a67ff')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
      Logger.log('✅ CREDENTIALS sheet created');
    }

    // Already exists check
    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow >= 2) {
      const existing = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < existing.length; i++) {
        if (String(existing[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          Logger.log('⚠️ Credentials already exist for: ' + userId);

          // ✅ Branch code update karo agar missing hai
          const existingBranch = String(sh.getRange(i + 2, 4).getValue() || '').trim();
          if (!existingBranch && branchCode) {
            sh.getRange(i + 2, 4).setValue(branchCode);
            Logger.log('✅ Branch code updated for existing user: ' + userId);
          }

          return {
            success:       true,
            message:       'Credentials already exist (branch updated if missing)',
            alreadyExists: true
          };
        }
      }
    }

    // Default password — ✅ FIX C-3: ek consistent default, MUST_CHANGE flag
    const defaultPassword = DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD; // ✅ FIX 14: central constant
    const hashedPassword  = hashPassword(defaultPassword, userId); // ✅ FIX: salt=userId

    // ✅ FIX C-3: 6 columns — F: MUST_CHANGE_PASSWORD flag
    sh.appendRow([
      userId,           // A: User ID
      hashedPassword,   // B: Password (hashed)
      'MEMBER',         // C: Role
      branchCode,       // D: Branch Code
      'ACTIVE',         // E: Status
      'YES'             // F: Must Change Password on first login
    ]);

    Logger.log('✅ Credentials saved: ' + userId + ' | Branch: ' + branchCode + ' | Role: MEMBER | Status: ACTIVE');

    return {
      success:         true,
      message:         'Credentials saved successfully',
      userId:          userId,
      defaultPassword: defaultPassword,  // For notification/email
      branchCode:      branchCode,
      alreadyExists:   false
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('addMemberCredentials error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 🔐 BONUS: Function to Re-Hash Existing Plain Text Passwords
// ============================================

/**
 * Convert all plain text passwords to hashed passwords
 * ⚠️ RUN THIS ONCE if you have existing plain text passwords
 */
function convertPlainTextPasswordsToHashed() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    
    if (!sh) {
      Logger.log('❌ CREDENTIALS sheet not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ No credentials to convert');
      return { success: true, message: 'No credentials found' };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getValues();
    var converted = 0;
    var skipped = 0;
    var errors = 0;
    
    Logger.log('🔄 Starting password conversion...');
    Logger.log('   Total rows: ' + data.length);
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var userId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      var currentPassword = String(data[i][1] || '').trim();
      var role = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
      
      if (!userId || !currentPassword) {
        skipped++;
        continue;
      }
      
      // Check if password is already hashed (64 characters = SHA-256 hex)
      if (currentPassword.length === 64 && /^[a-f0-9]+$/i.test(currentPassword)) {
        Logger.log('⏭️ Skipping ' + userId + ' (already hashed)');
        skipped++;
        continue;
      }
      
      // Hash the plain text password
      try {
        var hashedPassword = hashPassword(currentPassword, userId); // ✅ FIX: salted
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(hashedPassword); // Update password column
        
        Logger.log('✅ Converted: ' + userId + ' (Role: ' + role + ')');
        Logger.log('   Plain: ' + currentPassword + ' → Hash: ' + hashedPassword.substring(0, 16) + '...');
        converted++;
        
      } catch (hashError) {
        Logger.log('❌ Failed to convert ' + userId + ': ' + hashError.message);
        errors++;
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('');
    Logger.log('=== Conversion Complete ===');
    Logger.log('✅ Converted: ' + converted);
    Logger.log('⏭️ Skipped (already hashed): ' + skipped);
    Logger.log('❌ Errors: ' + errors);
    Logger.log('========================');
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      converted: converted,
      skipped: skipped,
      errors: errors,
      message: 'Conversion complete. Converted: ' + converted + ', Skipped: ' + skipped + ', Errors: ' + errors
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Conversion error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**

function getAllMembers() {

    }

    }

  } catch (e) {

    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Search member by ID or User ID
 */
function searchMember(searchTerm) {
  try {
    searchTerm = String(searchTerm || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    if (!searchTerm) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter search term' };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'MEMBER ENTRY sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No members found' };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var memberId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var userId = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (memberId === searchTerm || userId === searchTerm) {
        return {
          success: true,
          member: {
            memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
            name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            contact: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            userId: String(data[i][3] || ''),
             email: String(data[i][4] || '')
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Member not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Search member error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// ðŸ”¥ SIMPLE ACCOUNT CLOSE - NO LOAN ADJUSTMENT
// ============================================

function getActiveAccountsForClose(operatorId) {
  try {
    // ✅ Branch filter
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var accountSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSheet) return { success: true, accounts: [] };
    var lastRow = accountSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: true, accounts: [] };

    // Col M (index 12) = branchCode — read 13 cols
    var data = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accounts = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var status    = String(data[i][7]  || '').toUpperCase(); // Col H: STATUS
      var rowBranch = String(data[i][12] || '').trim();        // Col M: branchCode

      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;

      var memberId  = String(data[i][0] || '');
      var accountNo = String(data[i][2] || '');
      var loanInfo  = getMemberLoanStatus(memberId);

      accounts.push({
        accountNo:       accountNo,
        memberId:        memberId,
        name:            String(data[i][1] || ''),
        accountType:     String(data[i][4] || ''),
        openDate:        data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : '',
        userId:          String(data[i][9] || ''),  // Col J
        email:           String(data[i][8] || ''),  // Col I
        hasLoan:         loanInfo.hasLoan,
        loanOutstanding: loanInfo.totalOutstanding,
        rowIndex:        i + 2
      });
    }

    return { success: true, accounts: accounts };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get active accounts for close error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Check member's loan status
 */
function getMemberLoanStatus(memberId) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!loanSheet) {
      return { hasLoan: false, totalOutstanding: 0 };
    }
    
    var lastRow = loanSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { hasLoan: false, totalOutstanding: 0 };
    }
    
    var data = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 11).getValues();
    var totalOutstanding = 0;
    var hasActiveLoan = false;
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var loanMemberId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      var loanStatus = String(data[i][10] || '').toUpperCase();
      var remaining = parseFloat(data[i][9]) || 0;
      
      if (loanMemberId === memberId && loanStatus === 'ACTIVE' && remaining > 0) {
        hasActiveLoan = true;
        totalOutstanding += remaining;
      }
    }
    
    return { 
      hasLoan: hasActiveLoan, 
      totalOutstanding: totalOutstanding 
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get member loan status error: ' + e.toString());
    return { hasLoan: false, totalOutstanding: 0 };
  }
}

/**
 * Get account details with loan check
 */
function getAccountDetailsForClose(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    
    if (!accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account Number is required' };
    }
    
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!accountSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = accountSheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No accounts found' };
    }
    
    var data = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 12).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var currentAccountNo = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
      
      if (currentAccountNo === accountNo) {
        var memberId = String(data[i][0] || '');
        
        // Get current deposit balance
        var balanceResult = getAccountBalance(accountNo);
        var depositBalance = balanceResult.balance || 0;
        
        // Get loan outstanding
        var loanInfo = getMemberLoanStatus(memberId);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          account: {
            accountNo: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            memberId: memberId,
            name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            accountType: String(data[i][4] || ''),
            openDate: data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : '',
            status: String(data[i][7] || ''),
            userId: String(data[i][9] || ''),
            currentBalance: depositBalance,
            hasLoan: loanInfo.hasLoan,
            loanOutstanding: loanInfo.totalOutstanding,
            rowIndex: i + 2
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Account not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get account details for close error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get account balance from DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT
 */
function getAccountBalance(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    
    if (!accountNo) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 5).getValues();
    var currentBalance = 0;
    
    // Find last entry for this account
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var accNo = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      if (accNo === accountNo) {
        currentBalance = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0; // Column E: Current_Balance
        break;
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, balance: currentBalance };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get account balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get recent closed accounts
 */
function getRecentClosedAccounts(limit) {
  try {
    limit = limit || 10;
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT CLOSE');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, closedAccounts: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, closedAccounts: [] };
    }
    
    var startRow = Math.max(2, lastRow - limit + 1);
    var numRows = lastRow - startRow + 1;
    
    var data = sh.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, 4).getValues();
    var closedAccounts = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      closedAccounts.push({
        accountNo: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
        settlementAmount: data[i][2] || 0,
        closeDate: data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : ''
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, closedAccounts: closedAccounts };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get recent closed accounts error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
  }
// ============================================
// ACCOUNT OPEN FORM - BACKEND FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function getNextAccountNumber() {
  // ✅ LockService — race condition rokta hai
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000); // 10 sec wait
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again in a moment.' };
  }

  try {
    var ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh    = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

    // ── Step 1: ACCOUNT OPEN sheet se last approved number lo ──
    var lastApproved = 10000000; // default start - 1

    if (sh && sh.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      // Col C mein account numbers hain — max dhundo (last row nahi, max value)
      var colC = sh.getRange(2, 3, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < colC.length; i++) {
        var num = parseInt(String(colC[i][0] || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(num) && num > lastApproved) lastApproved = num;
      }
    }

    // ── Step 2: PENDING_ENTRIES mein reserved numbers dhundo ──
    var pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    var reservedNums = [];

    if (pendingSheet && pendingSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var pData = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      for (var p = 0; p < pData.length; p++) {
        var pStatus = String(pData[p][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        var pType   = String(pData[p][1] || '').toUpperCase();

        // Sirf PENDING ACCOUNT_OPEN entries check karo
        if (pStatus === 'PENDING' && pType === 'ACCOUNT_OPEN') {
          try {
            var pJson = JSON.parse(String(pData[p][2] || '{}'));
            var pAccNo = parseInt(String(pJson.accountNo || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(pAccNo) && pAccNo > 0) {
              reservedNums.push(pAccNo);
            }
          } catch (je) { /* JSON parse fail — skip */ }
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Step 3: PropertiesService se extra reserved numbers lo ──
    var propReserved = props.getProperty('RESERVED_ACCOUNT_NOS');
    if (propReserved) {
      try {
        var propNums = JSON.parse(propReserved);
        reservedNums = reservedNums.concat(propNums);
      } catch (pe) { /* ignore */ }
    }

    // ── Step 4: Next available number nikalo ──
    var candidate = lastApproved + 1;
    var allUsed   = reservedNums.concat([lastApproved]);

    // Skip karo agar candidate already used/reserved hai
    while (allUsed.indexOf(candidate) !== -1) {
      candidate++;
    }

    if (candidate > 99999999) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account number limit reached.' };
    }

    // ── Step 5: Is number ko PropertiesService mein reserve karo ──
    var currentReserved = [];
    try { currentReserved = JSON.parse(props.getProperty('RESERVED_ACCOUNT_NOS') || '[]'); } catch (e) {}
    currentReserved.push(candidate);
    // Max 100 reserved rakhna (cleanup)
    if (currentReserved.length > 100) currentReserved = currentReserved.slice(-100);
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_ACCOUNT_NOS', JSON.stringify(currentReserved));

    var nextAccountNo = String(candidate).padStart(8, '0');
    Logger.log('✅ getNextAccountNumber: ' + nextAccountNo + ' | Reserved pool: ' + currentReserved.length);

    return { success: true, nextAccountNo: nextAccountNo };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getNextAccountNumber error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock(); // ✅ Lock hamesha release karo
  }
}
function getMembersForDropdown(operatorId) {
  try {
    // Get operator's branch for filtering
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    if (!sh) return { success: true, members: [] };
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: true, members: [] };

    // Col F (index 5) = branchCode
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 6).getValues();
    var members = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var rowBranch = String(data[i][5] || '').trim();
      // Filter by branch if branchCode known
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;
      members.push({
        memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        name:     String(data[i][1] || ''),
        userId:   String(data[i][3] || ''),
        email:    String(data[i][4] || '')
      });
    }
    return { success: true, members: members };
     } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get members for dropdown error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Save new account to ACCOUNT OPEN sheet
 */
function getRecentAccounts(limit) {
  try {
    limit = limit || 5;
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, accounts: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, accounts: [] };
    }
    
    var startRow = Math.max(2, lastRow - limit + 1);
    var numRows = lastRow - startRow + 1;
    
    var data = sh.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, 12).getValues();
    var accounts = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      accounts.push({
        memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
        accountNo: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        accountOpenDate: data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : '',
        accountType: String(data[i][4] || ''),
        status: String(data[i][7] || ''),
        userId: String(data[i][9] || '')
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, accounts: accounts };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get recent accounts error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT - BACKEND FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function getActiveAccountsForDeposit(operatorId) {
  try {
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!sh) return { success: true, accounts: [] };
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: true, accounts: [] };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accounts = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var status      = String(data[i][7]  || '').toUpperCase();
      var rowBranch   = String(data[i][12] || '').trim();
      var accountType = String(data[i][4]  || '').toUpperCase().trim(); // Col E

      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;
      if (accountType === 'SAVINGS') continue; // ✅ LOCK — SAVINGS yahan nahi aayega

      accounts.push({
        accountNo: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        name:      String(data[i][1] || ''),
        userId:    String(data[i][9] || ''),
        email:     String(data[i][8] || '')
      });
    }

    return { success: true, accounts: accounts };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get active accounts error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Get account details by Account Number
 */
function getAccountDetailsByAccountNo(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    
    if (!accountNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account Number is required' };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No accounts found' };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var currentAccountNo = String(data[i][2] || '').trim(); // Column C
      
      if (currentAccountNo === accountNo) {
        return {
          success: true,
          account: {
            accountNo: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            userId: String(data[i][9] || ''),
            email: String(data[i][8] || '')
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Account not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get account details error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get current balance for account
 */
function getCurrentBalance(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    
    if (!accountNo) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 5).getValues();
    var currentBalance = 0;
    
    // Find last entry for this account
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var accNo = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      if (accNo === accountNo) {
        currentBalance = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0; // Column E: Current_Balance
        break;
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, balance: currentBalance };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get current balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getRecentDeposits(limit) {

/**
 * Get deposit history for specific account
 */
function getDepositHistory(accountNo, limit) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    limit = limit || 10;
    
    if (!accountNo) {
      return { success: true, deposits: [] };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, deposits: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, deposits: [] };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 9).getValues();
    var deposits = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var accNo = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      
      if (accNo === accountNo) {
        deposits.push({
          accountNo: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
          amount: data[i][2] || 0,
          interest: data[i][3] || 0,
          currentBalance: data[i][4] || 0,
          date: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : '',
          monthFor: String(data[i][6] || '')
        });
        
        if (deposits.length >= limit) break;
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, deposits: deposits };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get deposit history error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// LOAN MANAGEMENT - BACKEND FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function getNextLoanAccountNumber() {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(10000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }

  try {
    var ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh    = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

    // ── Step 1: Last approved loan number ──
    var lastApproved = 1000; // default start - 1

    if (sh && sh.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var colB = sh.getRange(2, 2, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < colB.length; i++) {
        var num = parseInt(String(colB[i][0] || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(num) && num > lastApproved) lastApproved = num;
      }
    }

    // ── Step 2: PENDING mein reserved loan numbers ──
    var pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    var reservedNums = [];

    if (pendingSheet && pendingSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var pData = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      for (var p = 0; p < pData.length; p++) {
        var pStatus = String(pData[p][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        var pType   = String(pData[p][1] || '').toUpperCase();
        if (pStatus === 'PENDING' && pType === 'LOAN') {
          try {
            var pJson  = JSON.parse(String(pData[p][2] || '{}'));
            var pLoanNo = parseInt(String(pJson.loanAcNo || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(pLoanNo) && pLoanNo > 0) reservedNums.push(pLoanNo);
          } catch (je) {}
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Step 3: PropertiesService reserved ──
    var propReserved = props.getProperty('RESERVED_LOAN_NOS');
    if (propReserved) {
      try { reservedNums = reservedNums.concat(JSON.parse(propReserved)); } catch (pe) {}
    }

    // ── Step 4: Next available ──
    var candidate = lastApproved + 1;
    var allUsed   = reservedNums.concat([lastApproved]);
    while (allUsed.indexOf(candidate) !== -1) { candidate++; }

    if (candidate > 9999) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Loan A/C number limit reached (9999).' };
    }

    // ── Step 5: Reserve karo ──
    var currentReserved = [];
    try { currentReserved = JSON.parse(props.getProperty('RESERVED_LOAN_NOS') || '[]'); } catch (e) {}
    currentReserved.push(candidate);
    if (currentReserved.length > 100) currentReserved = currentReserved.slice(-100);
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_LOAN_NOS', JSON.stringify(currentReserved));

    Logger.log('✅ getNextLoanAccountNumber: ' + candidate);
    return { success: true, nextLoanAcNo: String(candidate) };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getNextLoanAccountNumber error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function getMembersForLoan(operatorId) {
  try {
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    if (!sh) return { success: true, members: [] };
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: true, members: [] };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 6).getValues();
    var members = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var rowBranch = String(data[i][5] || '').trim();
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;
      members.push({
        memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        name:     String(data[i][1] || ''),
        contact:  String(data[i][2] || ''),
        userId:   String(data[i][3] || ''),
        email:    String(data[i][4] || '')
      });
    }
    return { success: true, members: members };
      } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get members for loan error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Get member details by Member ID for loan
 */
function getMemberDetailsForLoan(memberId) {
  try {
    memberId = String(memberId || '').trim();
    
    if (!memberId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID is required' };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'MEMBER ENTRY sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No members found' };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var currentMemberId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      
      if (currentMemberId === memberId) {
        return {
          success: true,
          member: {
            memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
            name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            contact: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            userId: String(data[i][3] || ''),
             email: String(data[i][4] || '')
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Member not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get member details for loan error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


/**
 * Save loan entry to LOAN MANAGEMENT sheet
 */
function getRecentLoans(limit) {
  try {
    limit = limit || 10;
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, loans: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, loans: [] };
    }
    
    var startRow = Math.max(2, lastRow - limit + 1);
    var numRows = lastRow - startRow + 1;
    
    var data = sh.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, 15).getValues();
    var loans = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      loans.push({
        memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        loanAcNo: String(data[i][1] || ''),
        name: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        loanType: String(data[i][3] || ''),
        roi: data[i][4] || '',
        loanAmount: data[i][5] || 0,
        loanDate: data[i][6] ? formatDate(data[i][6]) : '',
        monthlyEmi: data[i][7] || '',
        totalPaid: data[i][8] || 0,
        remaining: data[i][9] || 0,
        loanStatus: String(data[i][10] || '')
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, loans: loans };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get recent loans error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get active loans summary
 */
function getActiveLoansSummary() {
  try {
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, totalLoans: 0, totalAmount: 0, totalOutstanding: 0 };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, totalLoans: 0, totalAmount: 0, totalOutstanding: 0 };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 11).getValues();
    
    var totalLoans = 0;
    var totalAmount = 0;
    var totalOutstanding = 0;
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var status = String(data[i][10] || '').toLowerCase();
      
      if (status === 'active') {
        totalLoans++;
        totalAmount += parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0;
        totalOutstanding += parseFloat(data[i][9]) || 0;
      }
    }
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      totalLoans: totalLoans,
      totalAmount: totalAmount,
      totalOutstanding: totalOutstanding
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get active loans summary error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function getActiveLoansForRepayment(operatorId) {
  try {
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (!sh) return { success: true, loans: [] };
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: true, loans: [] };

    // Col O (index 14) = branchCode — read 15 cols
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 15).getValues();
    var loans = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var status    = String(data[i][10] || '').toUpperCase(); // Col K
      var rowBranch = String(data[i][14] || '').trim();        // Col O

      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;

      loans.push({
        loanAcNo:   String(data[i][1]  || ''),
        memberId:   String(data[i][0]  || ''),
        name:       String(data[i][2]  || ''),
        loanAmount: data[i][5] || 0,
        totalPaid:  data[i][8] || 0,
        remaining:  data[i][9] || 0,
        email:      String(data[i][12] || ''),  // Col M
        userId:     String(data[i][13] || ''),  // Col N
        rowIndex:   i + 2
      });
    }
    return { success: true, loans: loans };
     } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get active loans for repayment error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get loan details by Loan A/C Number
 */
function getLoanDetailsByLoanAc(loanAcNo) {
  try {
    loanAcNo = String(loanAcNo || '').trim();
    
    if (!loanAcNo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Loan A/C Number is required' };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'LOAN MANAGEMENT sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No loans found' };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 14).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var currentLoanAcNo = String(data[i][1] || '').trim(); // Column B
      
      if (currentLoanAcNo === loanAcNo) {
        return {
          success: true,
          loan: {
            loanAcNo: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
            name: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            loanAmount: data[i][5] || 0,
            totalPaid: data[i][8] || 0,
            remaining: data[i][9] || 0,
            status: String(data[i][10] || ''),
            rowIndex: i + 2
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Loan not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get loan details error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Save loan repayment and update loan management
 */
function getRepaymentHistory(loanAcNo, limit) {
  try {
    loanAcNo = String(loanAcNo || '').trim();
    limit = limit || 10;
    
    if (!loanAcNo) {
      return { success: true, repayments: [] };
    }
    
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, repayments: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, repayments: [] };
    }
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 6).getValues();
    var repayments = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var acNo = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      
      if (acNo === loanAcNo) {
        repayments.push({
          loanAcNo: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          paidAmount: data[i][1] || 0,
          monthFor: String(data[i][2] || ''),
          interest: data[i][3] || 0,
          defaultFee: data[i][4] || 0,
          date: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : ''
        });
        
        if (repayments.length >= limit) break;
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, repayments: repayments };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get repayment history error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get recent repayments (all loans)
 */
function getRecentRepayments(limit) {
  try {
    limit = limit || 10;
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: true, repayments: [] };
    }
    
    var lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) {
      return { success: true, repayments: [] };
    }
    
    var startRow = Math.max(2, lastRow - limit + 1);
    var numRows = lastRow - startRow + 1;
    
    var data = sh.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, 6).getValues();
    var repayments = [];
    
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      repayments.push({
        loanAcNo: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        paidAmount: data[i][1] || 0,
        monthFor: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        interest: data[i][3] || 0,
        defaultFee: data[i][4] || 0,
        date: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : ''
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, repayments: repayments };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get recent repayments error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 📊 ADMIN DASHBOARD STATISTICS
// ============================================

/**
 * Get dashboard statistics
 */
function getDashboardStats() {
  try {
    Logger.log('📊 Getting dashboard stats...');
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Total Members
    var memberSheet = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    var totalMembers = 0;
    if (memberSheet && memberSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      totalMembers = memberSheet.getLastRow() - 1;
    }
    Logger.log('Total Members: ' + totalMembers);
    
    // Active Accounts
    var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    var activeAccounts = 0;
    if (accountSheet && accountSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var accountData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 8, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < accountData.length; i++) {
        if (String(accountData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
          activeAccounts++;
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log('Active Accounts: ' + activeAccounts);
    
    // Deposits This Month
    var depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    var totalDepositsThisMonth = 0;
    var depositCountThisMonth = 0;
    
    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var today = new Date();
      var currentMonth = today.getMonth();
      var currentYear = today.getFullYear();
      
      var depositData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      
      for (var i = 0; i < depositData.length; i++) {
        var depositDate = depositData[i][5]; // Column F: Date
        if (depositDate instanceof Date) {
          if (depositDate.getMonth() === currentMonth && depositDate.getFullYear() === currentYear) {
            totalDepositsThisMonth += parseFloat(depositData[i][2]) || 0; // Column C: Amount
            depositCountThisMonth++;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log('Deposits This Month: ' + totalDepositsThisMonth + ' (' + depositCountThisMonth + ' entries)');
    
    // Active Loans
    var loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    var activeLoans = 0;
    var totalLoanAmount = 0;
    var totalOutstanding = 0;
    
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 11).getValues();
      
      for (var i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
        var status = String(loanData[i][10] || '').toUpperCase(); // Column K
        if (status === 'ACTIVE') {
          activeLoans++;
          totalLoanAmount += parseFloat(loanData[i][5]) || 0; // Column F
          totalOutstanding += parseFloat(loanData[i][9]) || 0; // Column J
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log('Active Loans: ' + activeLoans + ', Outstanding: ' + totalOutstanding);
    
    // Pending Requests
    var requestSheet = ss.getSheetByName('REQUESTS');
    var pendingRequests = 0;
    
    if (requestSheet && requestSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var requestData = requestSheet.getRange(2, 7, requestSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      
      for (var i = 0; i < requestData.length; i++) {
        var statusValue = String(requestData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase();
        // Check if status starts with "PENDING" (in case of combined status)
        if (statusValue.indexOf('PENDING') === 0) {
          pendingRequests++;
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log('Pending Requests: ' + pendingRequests);
    
    var result = {
      success: true,
      stats: {
        totalMembers: totalMembers,
        activeAccounts: activeAccounts,
        depositsThisMonth: {
          amount: totalDepositsThisMonth,
          count: depositCountThisMonth
        },
        loans: {
          active: activeLoans,
          totalAmount: totalLoanAmount,
          outstanding: totalOutstanding
        },
        pendingRequests: pendingRequests
      }
    };
    
    Logger.log('✅ Dashboard stats calculated successfully');
    return result;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Get dashboard stats error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 📥 EXPORT TO EXCEL
// ============================================

/**
 * Export sheet data to CSV format
 */
function exportSheetToCSV(sheetName) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    
    if (!sheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found' };
    }
    
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var csv = '';
    
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      for (var j = 0; j < row.length; j++) {
        var cell = row[j];
        
        // Handle dates
        if (cell instanceof Date) {
          cell = Utilities.formatDate(cell, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy');
        }
        
        // Escape commas and quotes
        if (typeof cell === 'string') {
          cell = '"' + cell.replace(/"/g, '""') + '"';
        }
        
        csv += cell;
        if (j < row.length - 1) csv += ',';
      }
      csv += '\n';
    }
    
    return {
      success: true,
      data: csv,
      filename: sheetName + '_' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss') + '.csv'
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Export error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 💾 AUTOMATIC BACKUP SYSTEM
// ============================================

/**
 * Create backup of entire spreadsheet
 */
function createBackup() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var backupFolder = getOrCreateBackupFolder();
    
    var timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd_HHmmss');
    var fileName = 'BACKUP_' + ss.getName() + '_' + timestamp;
    
    // Copy spreadsheet to backup folder
    var file = DriveApp.getFileById(ss.getId());
    var backup = file.makeCopy(fileName, backupFolder);
    
    Logger.log('Backup created: ' + fileName);
    
    // Delete backups older than 30 days
    cleanOldBackups(backupFolder);
    
    return { success: true, message: 'Backup created successfully', fileName: fileName };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Backup error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get or create backup folder in Google Drive
 */
function getOrCreateBackupFolder() {
  var folderName = 'FUTURE_LIFE_BACKUPS';
  var folders = DriveApp.getFoldersByName(folderName);
  
  if (folders.hasNext()) {
    return folders.next();
  } else {
    return DriveApp.createFolder(folderName);
  }
}

/**
 * Delete backups older than 30 days
 */
function cleanOldBackups(folder) {
  var cutoffDate = new Date();
  cutoffDate.setDate(cutoffDate.getDate() - 30);
  
  var files = folder.getFiles();
  
  while (files.hasNext()) {
    var file = files.next();
    if (file.getDateCreated() < cutoffDate) {
      file.setTrashed(true);
      Logger.log('Deleted old backup: ' + file.getName());
    }
  }
}

/**
 * Setup daily backup trigger (Run this once manually)
 */
function setupDailyBackup() {
  // Delete existing triggers
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'createBackup') {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(triggers[i]);
    }
  }
  
  // Create new daily trigger at 2 AM
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('createBackup')
    .timeBased()
    .atHour(2)
    .everyDays(1)
    .create();
  
  Logger.log('Daily backup trigger created');
}
function operatorSubmitRepayment(repaymentData, operatorId) {
  return operatorSubmitLoanRepayment(repaymentData, operatorId);
}

// 📢 SUPERVISOR ANNOUNCEMENT MANAGEMENT
// ============================================

/**
 * Get all announcements (including inactive for admin)
 */
function getAllAnnouncementsForAdmin() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['ID', 'Title', 'Message', 'Date', 'Status']]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
      return { success: true, announcements: [] };
    }
    
    var last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: true, announcements: [] };
    
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 8).getValues();
    var announcements = [];
    
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      announcements.push({
        rowIndex: i + 2,
        id: String(rows[i][0] || ''),
        title: String(rows[i][1] || ''),
        message: String(rows[i][2] || ''),
        date: rows[i][3] ? formatDate(rows[i][3]) : '',
        status: String(rows[i][4] || 'ACTIVE'),
        target: String(rows[i][5] || 'ALL'),
        branchCode: String(rows[i][6] || ''),
        createdBy: String(rows[i][7] || '')
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, announcements: announcements };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get all announcements error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Create new announcement
 */
function createAnnouncement(title, message) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([['ID', 'Title', 'Message', 'Date', 'Status']]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    var id = 'ANN' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    var today = new Date();
    
    sh.appendRow([id, title, message, today, 'ACTIVE']);
    
    Logger.log('Announcement created: ' + id);
    return { success: true, message: 'Announcement created successfully!' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Create announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Update announcement
 */
function updateAnnouncement(rowIndex, title, message) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'ANNOUNCEMENTS sheet not found' };
    
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 2).setValue(title);   // Column B: Title
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 3).setValue(message); // Column C: Message
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 4).setValue(new Date()); // Column D: Date (updated)
    
    Logger.log('Announcement updated at row: ' + rowIndex);
    return { success: true, message: 'Announcement updated successfully!' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Delete announcement (set status to INACTIVE)
 */
function deleteAnnouncement(announcementId) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'ANNOUNCEMENTS sheet not found' };
    
    var last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No announcements found' };
    
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0] || '') === announcementId) {
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 5).setValue('INACTIVE'); // Column E: Status
        Logger.log('Announcement deleted: ' + announcementId);
        return { success: true, message: 'Announcement deleted successfully!' };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Announcement not found' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Delete announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
  
}
// ============================================
// 🔄 FIXED: Delete Entry with Data Rollback
// ============================================

/**
 * Delete entry and rollback related data changes
 */
function deleteEntryWithRollback(sheetName, rowIndex, supervisorId, token) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    
    // Ab sheetName aur rowIndex defined hain
    sheetName = String(sheetName || '').trim();
    rowIndex = parseInt(rowIndex);
    
    Logger.log('🗑️ DELETE WITH ROLLBACK - Sheet: "' + sheetName + '", Row: ' + rowIndex);
    
    if (!sheetName || isNaN(rowIndex) || rowIndex < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid parameters' };
    }
    
    if (!supervisorId || !isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only supervisors can delete entries' };
    }
    
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found: ' + sheetName };
    }
    
    // Verify it's today's entry
    var dateColIndex = getDateColumnIndex(sheetName);
    if (dateColIndex >= 0) {
      var entryDate = sh.getRange(rowIndex, dateColIndex + 1).getValue();
      
      if (!entryDate || !(entryDate instanceof Date)) {
        return { success: false, message: 'No valid date found in this row' };
      }
      
      var today = new Date();
      today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      var entry = new Date(entryDate);
      entry.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      
      if (entry.getTime() !== today.getTime()) {
        return { 
          success: false, 
          message: '❌ Only today\'s entries can be deleted!\n\nEntry date: ' + 
                   Utilities.formatDate(entry, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
        };
      }
    }
    
    // ✅ ROLLBACK LOGIC: Update related tables before deleting
    var rollbackResult = rollbackRelatedData(sheetName, rowIndex);
    
    if (!rollbackResult.success) {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: '⚠️ Rollback failed: ' + rollbackResult.message + '\n\nEntry NOT deleted for data integrity.' 
      };
    }
    
    // Backup before delete
    logDeletedEntry(sheetName, rowIndex, supervisorId);
    
    // Delete row
    sh.deleteRow(rowIndex);
    Logger.log('✅ Row ' + rowIndex + ' deleted by supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
    
    logActivity(supervisorId, 'DELETE_ENTRY_ROLLBACK', sheetName + ' Row ' + rowIndex + ' deleted with rollback');
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      message: '✅ Entry deleted successfully!\n\n' + rollbackResult.message 
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Exception: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔄 FIXED: Rollback with Cascading Balance Update
// ============================================

/**
 * Rollback related data changes based on sheet type
 */
function rollbackRelatedData(sheetName, rowIndex) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Get row data before deletion
    var rowData = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    
    var rollbackMsg = '';
    
    // ============================================
    // 💵 LOAN REPAYMENT ROLLBACK
    // ============================================
    if (sheetName === 'LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION') {
      var loanAcNo = String(rowData[0] || '').trim(); // Column A
      var paidAmount = parseFloat(rowData[1]) || 0;   // Column B
      
      if (loanAcNo && paidAmount > 0) {
        // Find loan in LOAN MANAGEMENT
        var loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
        if (loanSheet) {
          var loanLastRow = loanSheet.getLastRow();
          if (loanLastRow >= 2) {
            var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanLastRow - 1, 12).getValues();
            
            for (var i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
              var currentLoanAc = String(loanData[i][1] || '').trim(); // Column B
              
              if (currentLoanAc === loanAcNo) {
                var loanAmount = parseFloat(loanData[i][5]) || 0;     // Column F
                var totalPaid = parseFloat(loanData[i][8]) || 0;      // Column I
                var remaining = parseFloat(loanData[i][9]) || 0;      // Column J
                var status = String(loanData[i][10] || '').toUpperCase(); // Column K
                
                // ✅ ROLLBACK: Subtract paid amount from total paid
                var newTotalPaid = Math.max(0, totalPaid - paidAmount);
                var newRemaining = loanAmount - newTotalPaid;
                
                // Update LOAN MANAGEMENT
                loanSheet.getRange(i + 2, 9).setValue(newTotalPaid);  // Column I
                loanSheet.getRange(i + 2, 10).setValue(newRemaining); // Column J
                
                // If loan was closed, reopen it
                if (status === 'CLOSED' && newRemaining > 0) {
                  loanSheet.getRange(i + 2, 11).setValue('ACTIVE');   // Column K
                  loanSheet.getRange(i + 2, 12).setValue('');         // Column L (clear close date)
                }
                
                rollbackMsg = '🔄 Loan A/C ' + loanAcNo + ' rolled back:\n' +
                              '  • Total Paid: ₹' + totalPaid.toFixed(2) + ' → ₹' + newTotalPaid.toFixed(2) + '\n' +
                              '  • Remaining: ₹' + remaining.toFixed(2) + ' → ₹' + newRemaining.toFixed(2);
                
                Logger.log('✅ Loan rollback successful: ' + loanAcNo);
                break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    // ============================================
    // 💰 DEPOSIT ROLLBACK WITH CASCADE UPDATE
    // ============================================
    else if (sheetName === 'DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT') {
      var accountNo = String(rowData[0] || '').trim();     // Column A
      var depositAmount = parseFloat(rowData[2]) || 0;     // Column C
      var interest = parseFloat(rowData[3]) || 0;          // Column D
      var currentBalance = parseFloat(rowData[4]) || 0;    // Column E
      
      if (accountNo && (depositAmount > 0 || interest > 0)) {
        // Calculate the amount to subtract from all future entries
        var amountToSubtract = depositAmount + interest;
        
        // ✅ PERF FIX: Batch read/write instead of cell-by-cell (1500 API calls → 2)
        var depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
        var lastRow = depositSheet.getLastRow();
        var updatedCount = 0;
        
        if (lastRow >= rowIndex + 1) {
          var remainingRows = lastRow - rowIndex;
          // Read ALL remaining rows at once — single API call
          var batchData = depositSheet.getRange(rowIndex + 1, 1, remainingRows, 5).getValues();
          
          for (var i = 0; i < batchData.length; i++) {
            if (String(batchData[i][0]).trim() === accountNo) {
              var oldBal = parseFloat(batchData[i][4]) || 0;
              var newBal = oldBal - amountToSubtract;
              batchData[i][4] = newBal; // update in memory
              updatedCount++;
              Logger.log('✅ Balance updated in memory row ' + (rowIndex + 1 + i) + ': ₹' + oldBal.toFixed(2) + ' → ₹' + newBal.toFixed(2));
            }
          }
          
          // Write ALL updated rows at once — single API call
          if (updatedCount > 0) {
            depositSheet.getRange(rowIndex + 1, 1, remainingRows, 5).setValues(batchData);
          }
        }
        
        rollbackMsg = '🔄 Account ' + accountNo + ' deposit deleted:\n' +
                      '  • Deleted amount: ₹' + amountToSubtract.toFixed(2) + '\n' +
                      '  • Updated ' + updatedCount + ' subsequent entry/entries\n' +
                      '  • All balances recalculated correctly';
        
        if (updatedCount === 0) {
          rollbackMsg += '\n  ⚠️ This was the last deposit entry';
        }
        
        Logger.log('✅ Deposit cascade rollback successful: ' + accountNo);
        Logger.log('   Entries updated: ' + updatedCount);
      }
    }
    
    // ============================================
    // 💳 LOAN MANAGEMENT ROLLBACK
    // ============================================
    else if (sheetName === 'LOAN MANAGEMENT') {
      var loanAcNo = String(rowData[1] || '').trim(); // Column B
      
      // Check if there are any repayments for this loan
      var repaymentSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
      if (repaymentSheet) {
        var repayLastRow = repaymentSheet.getLastRow();
        if (repayLastRow >= 2) {
          var repayData = repaymentSheet.getRange(2, 1, repayLastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
          var hasRepayments = false;
          
          for (var i = 0; i < repayData.length; i++) {
            if (String(repayData[i][0]).trim() === loanAcNo) {
              hasRepayments = true;
              break;
            }
          }
          
          if (hasRepayments) {
            return { 
              success: false, 
              message: '⚠️ Cannot delete loan!\n\nLoan A/C ' + loanAcNo + ' has repayment entries.\n\n' +
                       '📋 Action Required:\n' +
                       '1. Delete all repayment entries first\n' +
                       '2. Then delete the loan entry'
            };
          }
        }
      }
      
      rollbackMsg = '🔄 Loan A/C ' + loanAcNo + ' deleted\n' +
                    '  • No repayments found\n' +
                    '  • Safe to delete';
    }
    
    // ============================================
    // 🏦 ACCOUNT OPEN ROLLBACK
    // ============================================
    else if (sheetName === 'ACCOUNT OPEN') {
      var accountNo = String(rowData[2] || '').trim(); // Column C
      
      // Check for deposits or loans
      var hasDeposits = checkForDeposits(accountNo);
      var hasLoans = checkForLoans(accountNo);
      
      if (hasDeposits || hasLoans) {
        return { 
          success: false, 
          message: '⚠️ Cannot delete account!\n\nAccount ' + accountNo + ' has:\n' +
                   (hasDeposits ? '• Deposit history\n' : '') +
                   (hasLoans ? '• Loan history\n' : '') + '\n' +
                   '📋 Delete all related entries first'
        };
      }
      
      rollbackMsg = '🔄 Account ' + accountNo + ' deleted\n  • No related entries found\n  • Safe to delete';
    }
    
    // ============================================
    // 🔒 ACCOUNT CLOSE ROLLBACK
    // ============================================
    else if (sheetName === 'ACCOUNT CLOSE') {
      var accountNo = String(rowData[0] || '').trim(); // Column A
      
      // Reopen account in ACCOUNT OPEN sheet
      var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
      if (accountSheet) {
        var accLastRow = accountSheet.getLastRow();
        if (accLastRow >= 2) {
          var accData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accLastRow - 1, 8).getValues();
          
          for (var i = 0; i < accData.length; i++) {
            if (String(accData[i][2]).trim() === accountNo) { // Column C
              accountSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue('ACTIVE'); // Column H
              rollbackMsg = '🔄 Account ' + accountNo + ' reopened\n  • Status: CLOSED → ACTIVE';
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      message: rollbackMsg || 'Entry deleted (no rollback needed)' 
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Rollback error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

/**
 * Helper: Check if account has deposits
 */
function checkForDeposits(accountNo) {
  try {
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return false;
    
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === accountNo) return true;
    }
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Helper: Check if account has loans
 */
function checkForLoans(accountNo) {
  try {
    // Get Member ID from account number
    var accSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accSheet) return false;
    
    var accData = accSheet.getRange(2, 1, accSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getValues();
    var memberId = '';
    
    for (var i = 0; i < accData.length; i++) {
      if (String(accData[i][2]).trim() === accountNo) {
        memberId = String(accData[i][0]).trim();
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (!memberId) return false;
    
    // Check loans
    var loanSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (!loanSheet || loanSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return false;
    
    var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
      if (String(loanData[i][0]).trim() === memberId) return true;
    }
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    return false;
  }
}

// STEP 1: ADMIN & BRANCH MANAGEMENT SYSTEM
// Add these functions to your gs-1.txt file
