// ============================================
// 🔧 ADMIN LOGIN
// ============================================

function adminLogin(adminId, password) {
  try {
    adminId = String(adminId || '').trim();
    password = String(password || '').trim();
    
    if (!adminId || !password) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter Admin ID & Password' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ADMIN_USERS');
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Admin system not initialized. Contact system administrator.' };
    }
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No admin users found' };
    }
    
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      const aid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      const storedHash = String(rows[i][2] || '').trim();
      const name = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
      
      if (aid.toUpperCase() === adminId.toUpperCase()) {
        // ✅ FIX: Always use UPPERCASE adminId as salt — consistent with initializeAdminSystem
        const inputHashSalted = hashPassword(password, adminId.toUpperCase());
        const hashMatch = (inputHashSalted === storedHash);

        if (!hashMatch) {
          logFailedLogin(adminId, 'Invalid password (Admin)');
          return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
        }

        
        const token = createSession(adminId);
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'ADMIN_LOGIN', 'Admin logged in successfully');
        
        return {
          success: true,
          adminId: aid,
          role: 'ADMIN',
          name: name,
          email: String(rows[i][3] || ''),
          token: token
        };
      }
    }
    
    logFailedLogin(adminId, 'Admin ID not found');
    return { success: false, message: 'Invalid credentials' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Admin login error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'System error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🏢 BRANCH MANAGEMENT FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

/**
 * Create new branch
 */
function createBranch(branchData, adminId) {
  try {
    // Validate admin access
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can create branches' };
    }
    
    // Validate required fields
    if (!branchData.branchName || !branchData.pinCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch name and PIN code are required' };
    }
    
    // Validate PIN code format
    const pinCode = String(branchData.pinCode).trim();
    if (!/^\d{6}$/.test(pinCode)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'PIN code must be exactly 6 digits' };
    }
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sh = ss.getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    // Create sheet if doesn't exist
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('BRANCH_MASTER');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([
        ['Branch Code', 'Branch Name', 'PIN Code', 'Address', 'Contact', 'Created Date', 'Status', 'Supervisor ID']
      ]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#2c3e50')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff')
        .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
      
      // Set column widths
      sh.setColumnWidth(1, 120); // Branch Code
      sh.setColumnWidth(2, 200); // Branch Name
      sh.setColumnWidth(3, 100); // PIN Code
      sh.setColumnWidth(4, 250); // Address
      sh.setColumnWidth(5, 120); // Contact
      sh.setColumnWidth(6, 120); // Created Date
      sh.setColumnWidth(7, 100); // Status
      sh.setColumnWidth(8, 120); // Supervisor ID
    }
    
    // Generate branch code
    const branchCode = generateBranchCode(pinCode, sh);
    
    // Add branch
    const newRow = [
      branchCode,
      branchData.branchName.trim(),
      pinCode,
      branchData.address ? branchData.address.trim() : '',
      branchData.contact ? branchData.contact.trim() : '',
      new Date(),
      'ACTIVE',
      branchData.supervisorId ? branchData.supervisorId.trim().toUpperCase() : ''
    ];
    
    sh.appendRow(newRow);
    
    // Format the new row
    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    sh.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 8)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
      .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
    
    // Status column color
    const statusCell = sh.getRange(lastRow, 7);
    statusCell.setBackground('#d4edda').setFontColor('#155724').setFontWeight('bold');
    
    logActivity(adminId, 'CREATE_BRANCH', 'New branch created: ' + branchCode + ' - ' + branchData.branchName);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Branch created successfully!',
      branchCode: branchCode,
      branchName: branchData.branchName
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Create branch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Generate unique branch code
 * Format: PINCODE + Serial (01, 02, 03...)
 */
function generateBranchCode(pinCode, branchSheet) {
  try {
    pinCode = String(pinCode).trim();
    
    // Validate PIN code
    if (!/^\d{6}$/.test(pinCode)) {
      throw new Error('PIN code must be 6 digits');
    }
    
    // Get all existing branches
    const lastRow = branchSheet.getLastRow();
    let maxSerial = 0;
    
    if (lastRow > 1) {
      const data = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getValues();
      
      // Find highest serial number for this PIN code
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        const existingCode = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
        const existingPin = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
        
        // Check if same PIN code
        if (existingPin === pinCode && existingCode.length === 8 && existingCode.startsWith(pinCode)) {
          // Extract serial number (last 2 digits)
          const serial = parseInt(existingCode.slice(-2));
          if (!isNaN(serial) && serial > maxSerial) {
            maxSerial = serial;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Next serial number
    const nextSerial = maxSerial + 1;
    
    // Check if we've exceeded 99 branches for this PIN
    if (nextSerial > 99) {
      throw new Error('Maximum 99 branches allowed per PIN code');
    }
    
    // Format: PINCODE + 01/02/03... (8 digits total)
    const branchCode = pinCode + String(nextSerial).padStart(2, '0');
    
    return branchCode;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Generate branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    throw e;
  }
}

/**
 * Get list of all branches
 */
function getBranchList(adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can view branches' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, branches: [], message: 'No branches created yet' };
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    const branches = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      branches.push({
        rowIndex: i + 2,
        branchCode: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        branchName: String(data[i][1] || ''),
        pinCode: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        address: String(data[i][3] || ''),
        contact: String(data[i][4] || ''),
        createdDate: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : '',
        status: String(data[i][6] || ''),
        supervisorId: String(data[i][7] || '')
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, branches: branches };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get branch list error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Update existing branch
 */
function updateBranch(rowIndex, branchData, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can update branches' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'BRANCH_MASTER sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate row index
    if (rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > sh.getLastRow()) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid branch' };
    }
    
    const branchCode = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1).getValue();
    
    // Update fields (only if provided)
    if (branchData.branchName) {
      sh.getRange(rowIndex, 2).setValue(branchData.branchName.trim());
    }
    
    if (branchData.address !== undefined) {
      sh.getRange(rowIndex, 4).setValue(branchData.address.trim());
    }
    
    if (branchData.contact !== undefined) {
      sh.getRange(rowIndex, 5).setValue(branchData.contact.trim());
    }
    
    if (branchData.status) {
      const status = branchData.status.toUpperCase();
      if (status === 'ACTIVE' || status === 'INACTIVE') {
        sh.getRange(rowIndex, 7).setValue(status);
        
        // Update status cell color
        const statusCell = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 7);
        if (status === 'ACTIVE') {
          statusCell.setBackground('#d4edda').setFontColor('#155724');
        } else {
          statusCell.setBackground('#f8d7da').setFontColor('#721c24');
        }
      }
    }
    
    if (branchData.supervisorId !== undefined) {
      const supervisorId = branchData.supervisorId.trim().toUpperCase();
      sh.getRange(rowIndex, 8).setValue(supervisorId);
    }
    
    logActivity(adminId, 'UPDATE_BRANCH', 'Branch updated: ' + branchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Branch updated successfully!',
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update branch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Delete branch (with safety checks)
 */
function deleteBranch(rowIndex, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can delete branches' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'BRANCH_MASTER sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Validate row index
    if (rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > sh.getLastRow()) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid branch' };
    }
    
    const branchCode = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1).getValue();
    
    // Safety check: Check if branch has any active data
    // This prevents accidental deletion of branches with members/accounts
    const hasActiveData = checkBranchHasActiveData(branchCode);
    
    if (hasActiveData) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⚠️ Cannot delete branch with active members or accounts. Please close all accounts first.'
      };
    }
    
    // Delete the branch
    sh.deleteRow(rowIndex);
    
    logActivity(adminId, 'DELETE_BRANCH', 'Branch deleted: ' + branchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Branch deleted successfully!'
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Delete branch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Check if branch has active data
 */
function checkBranchHasActiveData(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Check ACCOUNT OPEN sheet
    const accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (accountSheet && accountSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      // For now, return false
      // TODO: In Step 3, we'll add branch code column and check here
      return false;
    }
    
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Check branch data error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Get branch details by code
 */
function getBranchByCode(branchCode, userId) {
  try {
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No branches found' };
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim() === branchCode.trim()) {
        return {
          success: true,
          branch: {
            branchCode: String(data[i][0] || ''),
            branchName: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            pinCode: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            address: String(data[i][3] || ''),
            contact: String(data[i][4] || ''),
            createdDate: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : '',
            status: String(data[i][6] || ''),
            supervisorId: String(data[i][7] || '')
          }
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Branch not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get branch by code error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Assign supervisor to branch
 */
function assignSupervisorToBranch(branchCode, supervisorId, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can assign supervisors' };
    }
    
    // Validate supervisor exists and role is SUPERVISOR
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid supervisor ID or user is not a supervisor' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No branches found' };
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim() === branchCode.trim()) {
        const rowIndex = i + 2;
        sh.getRange(rowIndex, 8).setValue(supervisorId.toUpperCase());
        
        // Also update supervisor's branch code in CREDENTIALS
        updateUserBranchCode(supervisorId, branchCode);
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'ASSIGN_SUPERVISOR', 'Supervisor ' + supervisorId + ' assigned to branch ' + branchCode);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Supervisor assigned successfully!'
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Branch not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Assign supervisor error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Update user's branch code in CREDENTIALS
 */
function updateUserBranchCode(userId, branchCode) {
  try {
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    
    if (!sh) return false;
    
    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return false;
    
    // Check if branch code column exists (column D)
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).getValues()[0];
    if (headers.length < 4 || headers[3] !== 'Branch Code') {
      // Add header if doesn't exist
      sh.getRange(1, 4).setValue('Branch Code');
      sh.getRange(1, 4).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#4a67ff').setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 4).setValue(branchCode);
        return true;
      }
    }
    
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update user branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔐 ADMIN VALIDATION HELPER
// ============================================

/**
 * Check if user is admin
 */
function isAdmin(userId) {
  try {
    if (!userId) return false;
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ADMIN_USERS');
    if (!sh) return false;
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return false;
    
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 1).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('isAdmin error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

// 🛠️ INITIALIZATION HELPER
// ============================================

/**
 * Initialize admin system (run this once)
 */
function initializeAdminSystem() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let adminSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ADMIN_USERS');
    
    if (!adminSheet) {
      // Create ADMIN_USERS sheet
      adminSheet = ss.insertSheet('ADMIN_USERS');
      adminSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([
        ['Admin ID', 'Name', 'Password Hash', 'Email', 'Created Date']
      ]);
      adminSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#e74c3c')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff')
        .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
      
      // Set column widths
      adminSheet.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
      adminSheet.setColumnWidth(2, 150);
      adminSheet.setColumnWidth(3, 200);
      adminSheet.setColumnWidth(4, 200);
      adminSheet.setColumnWidth(5, 120);
      
      // Add default admin — stored WITH salt (adminId as salt)
      var defaultAdminId  = 'ADMIN01';
      var defaultAdminPwd = 'admin123';
      var hashedPassword  = hashPassword(defaultAdminPwd, defaultAdminId); // ✅ salted

      adminSheet.appendRow([
        defaultAdminId,
        'Super Admin',
        hashedPassword,
        'admin@futurelife.com',
        new Date()
      ]);

      Logger.log('✅ Admin system initialized!');
      Logger.log('Default Admin ID: ' + defaultAdminId);
      Logger.log('⚠️ IMPORTANT: Change this password immediately!');

      return {
        success: true,
        message: 'Admin system initialized successfully!\n\nDefault Credentials:\nAdmin ID: ADMIN01\nPassword: admin123\n\n⚠️ Please change the password immediately!'
      };
    } else {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Admin system already exists'
      };
    }
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Initialize admin error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Change admin password
 */
function changeAdminPassword(adminId, oldPassword, newPassword) {
  try {
    if (!adminId || !oldPassword || !newPassword) {
      return { success: false, message: 'All fields are required' };
    }
    
    if (newPassword.length < 6) {
      return { success: false, message: 'New password must be at least 6 characters' };
    }
    
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('ADMIN_USERS');
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Admin system not found' };
    }
    
    const last = sh.getLastRow();
    if (last < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No admin users' };
    
    const rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, last - 1, 3).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === adminId.toUpperCase()) {
        const storedHash = String(rows[i][2] || '');
        const aid = String(rows[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        const oldPasswordHash = hashPassword(oldPassword, aid); // ✅ FIX: salted
        
        if (oldPasswordHash !== storedHash) {
          return { success: false, message: 'Current password is incorrect' };
        }
        
        const newPasswordHash = hashPassword(newPassword, aid); // ✅ FIX: salted
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 3).setValue(newPasswordHash);
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'PASSWORD_CHANGE', 'Admin password changed');
        
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Password changed successfully!'
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Admin not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Change admin password error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Check if user ID already exists
 */
function validateBranchExists(branchCode) {
  try {
    const branchSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    if (!branchSheet || branchSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { exists: false };
    }
    
    const data = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, branchSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim() === branchCode.trim()) {
        return {
          exists: true,
          branchName: String(data[i][1] || ''),
          status: String(data[i][6] || '')
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { exists: false };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Validate branch exists error: ' + e.toString());
    return { exists: false };
  }
}

/**
 * Get or create USER_DETAILS sheet
 */
function getOrCreateUserDetailsSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
  
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('USER_DETAILS');
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setValues([
      ['User ID', 'Name', 'Role', 'Branch Code', 'Contact', 'Email', 'Created Date', 'Status', 'Created By']
    ]);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#3498db')
      .setFontColor('#ffffff')
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
    
    // Set column widths
    sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 120); // User ID
    sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 150); // Name
    sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 100); // Role
    sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 120); // Branch Code
    sheet.setColumnWidth(5, 120); // Contact
    sheet.setColumnWidth(6, 180); // Email
    sheet.setColumnWidth(7, 120); // Created Date
    sheet.setColumnWidth(8, 100); // Status
    sheet.setColumnWidth(9, 120); // Created By
  }
  
  return sheet;
}

/**
 * Update branch supervisor
 */
function updateBranchSupervisor(branchCode, supervisorId) {
  try {
    const branchSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    if (!branchSheet) return false;
    
    const data = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, branchSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim() === branchCode.trim()) {
        branchSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(supervisorId);
        return true;
      }
    }
    
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update branch supervisor error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Get all users (for admin dashboard)

function getAllUsers(adminId) {

    const users = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      users.push({
        rowIndex: i + 2,
        userId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
        name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
        role: String(data[i][2] || ''),
        branchCode: String(data[i][3] || ''),
        contact: String(data[i][4] || ''),
        email: String(data[i][5] || ''),
        createdDate: data[i][6] ? formatDate(data[i][6]) : '',
        status: String(data[i][7] || ''),
        createdBy: String(data[i][8] || '')
      });
    }
    
    return { success: true, users: users };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get all users error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get users by branch
 */
function getUsersByBranch(branchCode, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied' };
    }
    
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userDetailsSheet || userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, users: [] };
    }
    
    const data = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    const users = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][3] || '').trim() === branchCode.trim()) {
        users.push({
          rowIndex: i + 2,
          userId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          name: String(data[i][1] || ''),
          role: String(data[i][2] || ''),
          branchCode: String(data[i][3] || ''),
          contact: String(data[i][4] || ''),
          email: String(data[i][5] || ''),
          createdDate: data[i][6] ? formatDate(data[i][6]) : '',
          status: String(data[i][7] || ''),
          createdBy: String(data[i][8] || '')
        });
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, users: users };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get users by branch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Activate/Deactivate user
 */
function toggleUserStatus(userId, newStatus, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can change user status' };
    }
    
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    newStatus = String(newStatus || '').toUpperCase();
    
    if (newStatus !== 'ACTIVE' && newStatus !== 'INACTIVE') {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid status. Use ACTIVE or INACTIVE' };
    }
    
    // Update in CREDENTIALS
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    let credUpdated = false;
    const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
      if (String(credData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
        const rowIndex = i + 2;
        credSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 5).setValue(newStatus);
        
        // Update cell color
        const statusCell = credSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 5);
        if (newStatus === 'ACTIVE') {
          statusCell.setBackground('#d4edda').setFontColor('#155724');
        } else {
          statusCell.setBackground('#f8d7da').setFontColor('#721c24');
        }
        
        credUpdated = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    // Update in USER_DETAILS
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (userDetailsSheet) {
      const userData = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < userData.length; i++) {
        if (String(userData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          const rowIndex = i + 2;
          userDetailsSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 8).setValue(newStatus);
          
          // Update cell color
          const statusCell = userDetailsSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 8);
          if (newStatus === 'ACTIVE') {
            statusCell.setBackground('#d4edda').setFontColor('#155724');
          } else {
            statusCell.setBackground('#f8d7da').setFontColor('#721c24');
          }
          
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    if (!credUpdated) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
    }
    
    const action = newStatus === 'ACTIVE' ? 'activated' : 'deactivated';
    logActivity(adminId, 'USER_STATUS_CHANGE', 'User ' + action + ': ' + userId);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'User ' + action + ' successfully!',
      userId: userId,
      newStatus: newStatus
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Toggle user status error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Transfer user to different branch
 */
function transferUserToBranch(userId, newBranchCode, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can transfer users' };
    }
    
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    // Validate new branch exists
    const branchCheck = validateBranchExists(newBranchCode);
    if (!branchCheck.exists) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Target branch not found: ' + newBranchCode };
    }
    
    // Get user current details from USER_DETAILS sheet (works for members AND staff)
    const userDetailsSheet2 = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    let oldBranchCode = null;
    let userRole = null;
    
    if (userDetailsSheet2 && userDetailsSheet2.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const udData = userDetailsSheet2.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet2.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < udData.length; i++) {
        if (String(udData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          oldBranchCode = String(udData[i][3] || '').trim();
          userRole = String(udData[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    if (!oldBranchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
    }
    
    if (oldBranchCode === newBranchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User is already in branch ' + newBranchCode };
    }
    
    // Update in CREDENTIALS
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSheet) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
        if (String(credData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          credSheet.getRange(i + 2, 4).setValue(newBranchCode);
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Update in USER_DETAILS
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (userDetailsSheet) {
      const userData = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < userData.length; i++) {
        if (String(userData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          userDetailsSheet.getRange(i + 2, 4).setValue(newBranchCode);
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // If user is supervisor, update old branch
    if (userRole === 'SUPERVISOR') {
      // Remove from old branch
      updateBranchSupervisor(oldBranchCode, '');
      // Add to new branch
      updateBranchSupervisor(newBranchCode, userId);
    }
    
    logActivity(adminId, 'USER_TRANSFER', 'User transferred: ' + userId + ' from ' + oldBranchCode + ' to ' + newBranchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'User transferred successfully!',
      userId: userId,
      oldBranch: oldBranchCode,
      newBranch: newBranchCode,
      branchName: branchCheck.branchName
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Transfer user error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Update user details (name, contact, email)
 */
function updateUserDetails(userId, updateData, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can update user details' };
    }
    
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (!userDetailsSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'USER_DETAILS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    const data = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
        const rowIndex = i + 2;
        
        // Update fields if provided
        if (updateData.name) {
          userDetailsSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 2).setValue(updateData.name.trim());
        }
        if (updateData.contact !== undefined) {
          userDetailsSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 5).setValue(updateData.contact.trim());
        }
        if (updateData.email !== undefined) {
          userDetailsSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 6).setValue(updateData.email.trim());
        }
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'UPDATE_USER', 'User details updated: ' + userId);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'User details updated successfully!',
          userId: userId
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update user details error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Reset user password (admin only)
 */
function resetUserPassword(userId, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can reset passwords' };
    }
    
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    // Check if user exists
    const userCheck = checkUserIdExists(userId);
    if (!userCheck.exists) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
    }
    
    // Generate new password (userId + "123")
    const newPassword = DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD; // ✅ FIX 14: central constant
    const hashedPassword = hashPassword(newPassword, userId); // ✅ FIX: salted with userId
    
    // Update in CREDENTIALS
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet) {
      return { success: false, message: 'CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    const data = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
        credSheet.getRange(i + 2, 2).setValue(hashedPassword);
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'RESET_PASSWORD', 'Password reset for user: ' + userId);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Password reset successfully!',
          userId: userId,
          newPassword: newPassword
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Failed to reset password' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Reset user password error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Delete user (admin only) - CAUTION!
 */
function deleteUser(userId, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can delete users' };
    }
    
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    
    // Check if user exists
    const userCheck = checkUserIdExists(userId);
    if (!userCheck.exists) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
    }
    
    // Safety check: Don't allow deleting users with active data
    // TODO: In future steps, check if user has created any entries
    
    let deletedFromCred = false;
    let deletedFromDetails = false;
    
    // Delete from CREDENTIALS
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSheet) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
        if (String(credData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          credSheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
          deletedFromCred = true;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Delete from USER_DETAILS
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (userDetailsSheet) {
      const userData = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < userData.length; i++) {
        if (String(userData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          userDetailsSheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
          deletedFromDetails = true;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // If user was supervisor, clear from branch
    if (userCheck.role === 'SUPERVISOR') {
      updateBranchSupervisor(userCheck.branchCode, '');
    }
    
    logActivity(adminId, 'DELETE_USER', 'User deleted: ' + userId + ' (' + userCheck.role + ')');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'User deleted successfully!',
      userId: userId
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Delete user error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get user statistics
 */
function getUserStatistics(adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied' };
    }
    
    const userDetailsSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userDetailsSheet || userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return {
        success: true,
        stats: {
          total: 0,
          supervisors: 0,
          operators: 0,
          active: 0,
          inactive: 0
        }
      };
    }
    
    const data = userDetailsSheet.getRange(2, 1, userDetailsSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    
    let total = data.length;
    let supervisors = 0;
    let operators = 0;
    let active = 0;
    let inactive = 0;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const role = String(data[i][2] || '').toUpperCase();
      const status = String(data[i][7] || '').toUpperCase();
      
      if (role === 'SUPERVISOR') supervisors++;
      if (role === 'OPERATOR') operators++;
      if (status === 'ACTIVE') active++;
      if (status === 'INACTIVE') inactive++;
    }
    
    return {
      success: true,
      stats: {
        total: total,
        supervisors: supervisors,
        operators: operators,
        active: active,
        inactive: inactive
      }
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get user statistics error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}// ============================================

/**
 * Add Branch Code column to ACCOUNT OPEN sheet
 * Run this ONCE to update sheet structure
 */
function addBranchCodeToAccountOpen() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!sh) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }
    
    // Check if column already exists
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 20).getValues()[0];
    let branchColIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      if (String(headers[i]).toUpperCase() === 'BRANCH CODE') {
        branchColIndex = i + 1;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (branchColIndex === -1) {
      // Add new column after existing columns
      const lastCol = sh.getLastColumn();
      sh.insertColumnAfter(lastCol);
      sh.getRange(1, lastCol + 1).setValue('Branch Code');
      sh.getRange(1, lastCol + 1)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#4a67ff')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
      
      Logger.log('✅ Branch Code column added to ACCOUNT OPEN');
    } else {
      Logger.log('ℹ️ Branch Code column already exists at column ' + branchColIndex);
    }
    
    return { success: true, message: 'Branch Code column added/verified' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

      return { success: true, message: 'Will be created with Branch Code' };

    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).getValues()[0];
    let branchColIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      if (String(headers[i]).toUpperCase() === 'BRANCH CODE') {
        branchColIndex = i + 1;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (branchColIndex === -1) {
      // Already added in saveMemberEntry function
      Logger.log('✅ Branch Code will be added via saveMemberEntry');
    }
    
    return { success: true, message: 'Branch Code column verified' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔐 BRANCH ACCESS CONTROL FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

/**
 * Check if user can access account (branch validation)
 */
function canAccessAccount(accountNo, userId) {
  try {
    // Get user's branch code
    const userBranchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(userId);
    
    if (!userBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: false,
        reason: 'User branch code not found',
        userBranch: '',
        accountBranch: ''
      };
    }
    
    // Get account's branch code
    const accountBranchCode = getAccountBranchCode(accountNo);
    
    if (!accountBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: false,
        reason: 'Account not found or no branch code',
        userBranch: userBranchCode,
        accountBranch: ''
      };
    }
    
    // Check if same branch
    if (userBranchCode === accountBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: true,
        mode: 'EDIT',
        userBranch: userBranchCode,
        accountBranch: accountBranchCode
      };
    } else {
      return {
        canAccess: true,
        mode: 'VIEW_ONLY',
        reason: 'Different branch - View only mode',
        userBranch: userBranchCode,
        accountBranch: accountBranchCode
      };
    }
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Can access account error: ' + e.toString());
    return {
      canAccess: false,
      reason: 'Error: ' + e.toString()
    };
  }
}

/**
 * Get account's branch code
 */
function getAccountBranchCode(accountNo) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return null;
    
    // Find Branch Code column
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 20).getValues()[0];
    let branchColIndex = -1;
    let accountColIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      if (String(headers[i]).toUpperCase() === 'BRANCH CODE') {
        branchColIndex = i;
      }
      if (String(headers[i]).toLowerCase().includes('account') && String(headers[i]).toLowerCase().includes('no')) {
        accountColIndex = i;
      }
    }
    
    if (branchColIndex === -1 || accountColIndex === -1) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Branch Code or Account No column not found in ACCOUNT OPEN');
      return null;
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, headers.length).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][accountColIndex]) === String(accountNo)) {
        return String(data[i][branchColIndex] || '');
      }
    }
    
    return null;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get account branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Check if user can access loan account
 */
function canAccessLoan(loanAccountNo, userId) {
  try {
    const userBranchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(userId);
    
    if (!userBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: false,
        reason: 'User branch code not found'
      };
    }
    
    const loanBranchCode = getLoanBranchCode(loanAccountNo);
    
    if (!loanBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: false,
        reason: 'Loan account not found'
      };
    }
    
    if (userBranchCode === loanBranchCode) {
      return {
        canAccess: true,
        mode: 'EDIT',
        userBranch: userBranchCode,
        loanBranch: loanBranchCode
      };
    } else {
      return {
        canAccess: true,
        mode: 'VIEW_ONLY',
        reason: 'Different branch - View only mode',
        userBranch: userBranchCode,
        loanBranch: loanBranchCode
      };
    }
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Can access loan error: ' + e.toString());
    return {
      canAccess: false,
      reason: 'Error: ' + e.toString()
    };
  }
}

/**
 * Get loan's branch code
 */
function getLoanBranchCode(loanAccountNo) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return null;
    
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 20).getValues()[0];
    let branchColIndex = -1;
    let loanColIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      if (String(headers[i]).toUpperCase() === 'BRANCH CODE') {
        branchColIndex = i;
      }
      if (String(headers[i]).toLowerCase().includes('loan') && String(headers[i]).toLowerCase().includes('account')) {
        loanColIndex = i;
      }
    }
    
    if (branchColIndex === -1 || loanColIndex === -1) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Branch Code or Loan Account column not found');
      return null;
    }
    
    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, headers.length).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][loanColIndex]) === String(loanAccountNo)) {
        return String(data[i][branchColIndex] || '');
      }
    }
    
    return null;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get loan branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🔢 GLOBAL SERIAL COUNTER MANAGEMENT
// ============================================

/**
 * Get or create SERIAL_COUNTERS sheet
 */
function getOrCreateSerialCountersSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('SERIAL_COUNTERS');
  
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('SERIAL_COUNTERS');
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3).setValues([
      ['Counter Type', 'Last Number', 'Last Updated']
    ]);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#e67e22')
      .setFontColor('#ffffff')
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
    
    // Set column widths
    sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 150); // Counter Type
    sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 150); // Last Number
    sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 150); // Last Updated
    
    // Initialize counters
    sheet.appendRow(['MEMBER_ID', 0, new Date()]);
    sheet.appendRow(['ACCOUNT_NO', 0, new Date()]);
    sheet.appendRow(['LOAN_ACCOUNT', 0, new Date()]);
    
    Logger.log('✅ SERIAL_COUNTERS sheet created with global counters');
  }
  
  return sheet;
}

/**
 * Get next GLOBAL serial number for a counter type
 * IMPORTANT: This is GLOBAL across ALL branches!
 */
function getNextSerial(counterType) {
  try {
    const sheet = getOrCreateSerialCountersSheet();
    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, Math.max(1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1), 3).getValues();
    
    // Find existing counter
    let foundRow = -1;
    let currentNumber = 0;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]) === counterType) {
        foundRow = i + 2; // +2 because header is row 1
        currentNumber = parseInt(data[i][1]) || 0;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    // Increment
    const nextNumber = currentNumber + 1;
    
    if (foundRow > 0) {
      // Update existing
      sheet.getRange(foundRow, 2).setValue(nextNumber);
      sheet.getRange(foundRow, 3).setValue(new Date());
    } else {
      // Create new counter (shouldn't happen if initialized properly)
      sheet.appendRow([
        counterType,
        nextNumber,
        new Date()
      ]);
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Global Serial - Type: ' + counterType + ', Next: ' + nextNumber);
    
    return nextNumber;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Get next serial error: ' + e.toString());
    throw new Error('Failed to generate serial number: ' + e.toString());
  }
}

// ============================================
// 🆔 GLOBAL ID GENERATION FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

/**
 * Generate Member ID (8 digits) - GLOBAL
 * Format: 10000001, 10000002, 10000003... (across ALL branches)
 */
function generateMemberId(branchCode) {
  try {
    const serial = getNextSerial('MEMBER_ID');
    
    // 8 digits, starting from 10000001
    const memberId = String(10000000 + serial);
    
    if (memberId.length !== 8) {
      throw new Error('Member ID generation error - invalid length');
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Generated Member ID: ' + memberId + ' for branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      memberId: memberId,
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Generate Member ID error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Generate Account Number (10 digits) - GLOBAL
 * Format: 1000000001, 1000000002, 1000000003... (across ALL branches)
 */
function generateAccountNumber(branchCode) {
  try {
    const serial = getNextSerial('ACCOUNT_NO');
    
    // 10 digits, starting from 1000000001
    const accountNo = String(1000000000 + serial);
    
    if (accountNo.length !== 10) {
      throw new Error('Account number generation error - invalid length');
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Generated Account Number: ' + accountNo + ' for branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      accountNo: accountNo,
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Generate Account Number error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Generate Loan Account Number (9 digits) - GLOBAL
 * Format: 100000001, 100000002, 100000003... (across ALL branches)
 */
function generateLoanAccount(branchCode) {
  try {
    const serial = getNextSerial('LOAN_ACCOUNT');
    
    // 9 digits, starting from 100000001
    const loanAccount = String(100000000 + serial);
    
    if (loanAccount.length !== 9) {
      throw new Error('Loan account generation error - invalid length');
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Generated Loan Account: ' + loanAccount + ' for branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      loanAccount: loanAccount,
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Generate Loan Account error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Generate Transaction ID (T + 7 random digits) - GLOBAL
 * Format: T1234567, T9876543...
 */
function generateTransactionId() {
  try {
    // Generate 7 random digits
    let randomDigits = '';
    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
      randomDigits += Math.floor(Math.random() * 10);
    }
    
    const transactionId = 'T' + randomDigits;
    
    // Check if already exists (very unlikely but safety check)
    let attempts = 0;
    while (checkTransactionIdExists(transactionId) && attempts < 10) {
      randomDigits = '';
      for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
        randomDigits += Math.floor(Math.random() * 10);
      }
      transactionId = 'T' + randomDigits;
      attempts++;
    }
    
    if (attempts >= 10) {
      throw new Error('Could not generate unique transaction ID');
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Generated Transaction ID: ' + transactionId);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      transactionId: transactionId
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Generate Transaction ID error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Check if transaction ID exists
 */
function checkTransactionIdExists(transactionId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Check in DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT
    const depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const depositData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 10, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < depositData.length; i++) {
        if (String(depositData[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check in LOAN MANAGEMENT
    const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 15, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
        if (String(loanData[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check in LOAN REPAY
    const repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    if (repaySheet && repaySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const repayData = repaySheet.getRange(2, 9, repaySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < repayData.length; i++) {
        if (String(repayData[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    return false;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Check transaction ID error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}


/**
 * Get branch code from operator/supervisor ID
 */
function getBranchCodeFromOperator(userId) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!userId) return { success: false, message: 'User ID required' };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // ✅ FIX: Check USER_DETAILS first, then CREDENTIALS as fallback
    // USER_DETAILS sheet
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (userSheet && userSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          const branchCode = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
          if (branchCode) {
            return {
              success:    true,
              branchCode: branchCode,
              userId:     String(data[i][0]),
              name:       String(data[i][1]),
              role:       String(data[i][2])
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // ✅ FALLBACK: CREDENTIALS sheet — Col A: userId, Col D: branchCode
    const credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
      for (let j = 0; j < credData.length; j++) {
        if (String(credData[j][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          const branchCode = String(credData[j][3] || '').trim();
          if (branchCode) {
            Logger.log('getBranchCodeFromOperator: found in CREDENTIALS for ' + userId);
            return {
              success:    true,
              branchCode: branchCode,
              userId:     String(credData[j][0]),
              role:       String(credData[j][2])
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    Logger.log('getBranchCodeFromOperator: user not found in USER_DETAILS or CREDENTIALS: ' + userId);
    return { success: false, message: 'User not found: ' + userId };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get branch code error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// 📊 ID GENERATION HELPER FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

/**
 * Get current GLOBAL counter values
 */
function getCurrentCounters() {
  try {
    const sheet = getOrCreateSerialCountersSheet();
    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, Math.max(1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1), 3).getValues();
    
    const counters = {
      memberId: 0,
      accountNo: 0,
      loanAccount: 0
    };
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const counterType = String(data[i][0]);
      const value = parseInt(data[i][1]) || 0;
      
      if (counterType === 'MEMBER_ID') counters.memberId = value;
      if (counterType === 'ACCOUNT_NO') counters.accountNo = value;
      if (counterType === 'LOAN_ACCOUNT') counters.loanAccount = value;
    }
    
    return {
      success: true,
      counters: counters,
      note: 'These are GLOBAL counters across ALL branches'
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get current counters error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Reset counter (admin only - use with EXTREME caution!)
 */
function resetCounter(counterType, newValue, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only admin can reset counters' };
    }
    
    const sheet = getOrCreateSerialCountersSheet();
    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, Math.max(1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1), 3).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]) === counterType) {
        const rowIndex = i + 2;
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 2).setValue(newValue);
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 3).setValue(new Date());
        
        logActivity(adminId, 'RESET_COUNTER', 'GLOBAL Counter - Type: ' + counterType + ', New Value: ' + newValue);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Counter reset successfully! ⚠️ This affects ALL branches!'
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Counter not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Reset counter error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Initialize all wallet and day operation sheets
 * RUN THIS ONCE after adding Step 4 code
 */
function initializeWalletSystem() {
  try {
    const results = {
      walletMaster: createWalletMasterSheet(),
      walletTransactions: createWalletTransactionsSheet(),
      dayOperations: createDayOperationsSheet()
    };
    
    Logger.log('✅ Wallet system initialized successfully!');
    Logger.log(JSON.stringify(results, null, 2));
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Wallet system initialized!',
      sheets: results
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Initialize wallet system error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Create WALLET_MASTER sheet
 */
function createWalletMasterSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
  
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('WALLET_MASTER');
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setValues([
      ['User ID', 'Role', 'Branch Code', 'Current Balance', 'Last Updated', 'Status']
    ]);
    
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#16a085')
      .setFontColor('#ffffff')
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
    
    sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 100);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 120);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 120);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(5, 150);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(6, 100);
    
    return { created: true, name: 'WALLET_MASTER' };
  }
  
  return { created: false, name: 'WALLET_MASTER', message: 'Already exists' };
}

// ============================================
// 💰 WALLET CORE FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

function getWalletBalance(userId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, balance: 0, exists: false };
    }
    
    const data = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(userId).toUpperCase()) {
        return { 
          success: true, 
          balance: Number(data[i][3]) || 0,
          exists: true,
          userId: String(data[i][0]),
          role: String(data[i][1]),
          branchCode: String(data[i][2]),
          lastUpdated: data[i][4]
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, balance: 0, exists: false };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get wallet balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString(), balance: 0 };
  }
}
function initializeWallet(userId, role, branchCode, initialBalance) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!sheet) {
      initializeWalletSystem();
      sheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    }
    
    // Check if already exists
    const existing = getWalletBalance(userId);
    if (existing.success && existing.exists) {
      return {
        success: true,
        message: 'Wallet already exists',
        balance: existing.balance
      };
    }
    
    // Create new wallet
    sheet.appendRow([
      userId.toUpperCase(),
      role || 'OPERATOR',
      branchCode || '',
      initialBalance || 0,
      new Date()
    ]);
    
    Logger.log('✅ Wallet initialized: ' + userId + ' with balance: ' + (initialBalance || 0));
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Wallet created successfully',
      balance: initialBalance || 0
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Initialize wallet error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function updateWalletBalance(userId, newBalance) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet) {
      return false;
    }
    
    const data = walletSheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? 
      walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues() : [];
    
    let found = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(userId).toUpperCase()) {
        // Update balance (column 4) and last updated (column 5)
        // ✅ FIX: Atomic write — balance + timestamp in single API call
        walletSheet.getRange(i + 2, 4, 1, 2).setValues([[newBalance, new Date()]]);
        found = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (!found) {
      Logger.log('⚠️ Wallet not found for update: ' + userId);
      return false;
    }
    
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update wallet balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Record wallet transaction
 */
function recordWalletTransaction(transId, fromUser, toUser, amount, type, remarks, branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_TRANSACTIONS');
    
    if (!sheet) return { success: false };
    
    sheet.appendRow([
      transId,
      fromUser,
      toUser,
      amount,
      type,
      new Date(),
      remarks || '',
      branchCode || ''
    ]);
    
    return { success: true };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Record wallet transaction error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Record wallet load transaction
 */
function recordWalletLoadTransaction(transId, supervisorId, amount, remarks, branchCode, oldBalance, newBalance) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let transSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_LOAD_TRANSACTIONS');
    
    // Create sheet if doesn't exist
    if (!transSheet) {
      transSheet = ss.insertSheet('WALLET_LOAD_TRANSACTIONS');
      transSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([[
        'Transaction ID', 'Date', 'Time', 'Supervisor ID', 'Branch Code', 
        'Amount', 'Old Balance', 'New Balance', 'Remarks'
      ]]);
      
      // Format header
      transSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#16a085')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    // Add transaction record
    const now = new Date();
    transSheet.appendRow([
      transId,
      Utilities.formatDate(now, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
      Utilities.formatDate(now, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'HH:mm:ss'),
      supervisorId,
      branchCode,
      amount,
      oldBalance,
      newBalance,
      remarks
    ]);
    
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Record load transaction error: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}
/**
 * Find supervisor for a branch
 */
function findSupervisorForBranch(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet || userSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return null;
    
    const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][2]).toUpperCase() === 'SUPERVISOR' &&
          String(data[i][3]) === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][7]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        return String(data[i][0]);
      }
    }
    
    return null;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Find supervisor error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}
// ============================================
// GET OPERATORS FOR BRANCH (FOR DROPDOWN)
// ============================================

function getOperatorsForBranch(supervisorId) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX: Validate input
    if (!supervisorId || supervisorId.trim() === '') {
      Logger.log('ERROR: supervisorId is missing in getOperatorsForBranch');
      return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID is required' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX: Check if user is supervisor
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: User ' + supervisorId + ' is not a supervisor');
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can view operators' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX: Properly extract branch code from object
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: Failed to get branch code for supervisor ' + supervisorId);
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found for supervisor' };
    }
    
    const branchCode = branchResult.branchCode; // ✅ Extract from object
    
    if (!branchCode || branchCode.trim() === '') {
      Logger.log('ERROR: Branch code is empty for supervisor ' + supervisorId);
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code is empty' };
    }
    
    Logger.log('✅ Getting operators for branch: ' + branchCode + ' (Supervisor: ' + supervisorId + ')');
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: USER_DETAILS sheet not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'USER_DETAILS sheet not found' };
    }
    
    if (userSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      Logger.log('INFO: No users in USER_DETAILS sheet');
      return { success: true, operators: [], branchCode: branchCode };
    }
    
    const lastRow = userSheet.getLastRow();
    const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 10).getValues();
    const operators = [];
    
    Logger.log('Scanning ' + (lastRow - 1) + ' users in USER_DETAILS...');
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const userId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      const name = String(data[i][1] || '').trim();
      const role = String(data[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const userBranch = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
      const status = String(data[i][7] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      // ✅ DEBUG: Log each operator found
      if (role === 'OPERATOR') {
        Logger.log('Found OPERATOR: ' + userId + ' | Branch: ' + userBranch + ' | Status: ' + status);
      }
      
      // ✅ Only show ACTIVE operators from SAME BRANCH
      if (role === 'OPERATOR' && userBranch === branchCode && status === 'ACTIVE') {
        operators.push({
          operatorId: userId,
          name: name || userId,
          branch: userBranch,
          status: status
        });
        Logger.log('  ✅ Added to list: ' + userId);
      }
    }
    
    // Sort by operator ID
    operators.sort((a, b) => a.operatorId.localeCompare(b.operatorId));
    
    Logger.log('✅ Found ' + operators.length + ' active operators for branch ' + branchCode);
    
    return { 
      success: true, 
      operators: operators,
      branchCode: branchCode,
      count: operators.length
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Get operators for branch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// CHECK IF DAY IS STARTED
// ============================================
// ✅ FEATURE 1 FIX: getLastDayStatus — date-independent
// Returns last open day record for branch regardless of date
// No auto-close at midnight — previous day stays open until manually closed
function isDayStarted(branchCode) {
  return getLastDayStatus(branchCode).started;
}

function getLastDayStatus(branchCode) {
  try {
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const daySheet = ss.getSheetByName('DAY_OPERATIONS');

    if (!daySheet || daySheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { started: false, status: 'CLOSED', dayDate: null, isToday: false };
    }

    const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = daySheet.getRange(2, 1, daySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

    // Search from BOTTOM — get most recent record for this branch
    for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      if (!data[i][0]) continue;
      const branch    = String(data[i][1] || '').trim();
      const operation = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const status    = String(data[i][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

      if (branch !== branchCode) continue;

      const dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const isToday = (dateStr === today);

      if (operation === 'DAY_BEGIN' && status === 'OPEN') {
        return {
          started:         true,
          status:          'OPEN',
          dayDate:         dateStr,
          dayDateDisplay:  Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
          isToday:         isToday,
          isPreviousDay:   !isToday,
          rowIndex:        i + 2,
          supervisorId:    String(data[i][2] || '')
        };
      }

       if (operation === 'DAY_BEGIN' && status === 'CLOSED') {
        // ✅ FIX: Agar aaj ka day CLOSED bhi ho chuka hai — dobara begin block karo
        if (isToday) {
          return {
            started:        false,
            status:         'DONE_TODAY',   // new status signal
            dayDate:        dateStr,
            dayDateDisplay: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
            isToday:        true,
            alreadyDoneToday: true
          };
        }
        return { started: false, status: 'CLOSED', dayDate: dateStr, isToday: false };
      }
    }

    return { started: false, status: 'CLOSED', dayDate: null, isToday: false };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getLastDayStatus error: ' + e.toString());
    return { started: false, status: 'CLOSED', dayDate: null, isToday: false };
  }
}

// ✅ FEATURE 1: getLastCounterStatus for operator — date-independent
function getLastCounterStatus(operatorId) {
  try {
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim();
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { hasOpen: false };
    }

    const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

    // From bottom — find last record for this operator
    for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      if (String(data[i][3] || '').trim() !== operatorId) continue;
      const status  = String(data[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const dateStr = data[i][0] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
      const isToday = (dateStr === today);

      if (status === 'OPEN') {
        return {
          hasOpen:       true,
          counterNo:     String(data[i][4] || ''),
          dateStr:       dateStr,
          dateDisplay:   dateStr ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy') : '',
          isToday:       isToday,
          isPreviousDay: !isToday,
          rowIndex:      i + 2
        };
      }
      if (status === 'CLOSED') {
        return { hasOpen: false, isToday: isToday };
      }
    }
    return { hasOpen: false };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getLastCounterStatus error: ' + e.toString());
    return { hasOpen: false };
  }
}

function supervisorStartDay(supervisorId, branchCode) {
  try {
    // ✅ FIX: Add validation for parameters
    if (!supervisorId || !branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Missing supervisor ID or branch code' };
    }
    
    // Verify supervisor
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can start the day' };
    }
    
    // ✅ FIX: Properly extract branch code from object
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ ' + branchResult.message };
    }
    
    const supBranch = branchResult.branchCode; // ✅ Extract branchCode from object
    
    // ✅ FIX: Now compare strings properly
    if (supBranch !== branchCode) {
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: '⛔ Branch code mismatch!\n\nYour branch: ' + supBranch + '\nRequested: ' + branchCode 
      };
    }
    
    const dayCheck = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);

    // ✅ FIX: Aaj ka day already COMPLETE ho chuka hai (Begin + End dono)
    if (dayCheck.alreadyDoneToday) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '🔒 Aaj ka Day already complete ho chuka hai!\n\n' +
                 'Day Begin aur Day End dono ho chuke hain aaj ke liye.\n' +
                 'Kal hi dobara Day Begin ho sakta hai.',
        alreadyDoneToday: true
      };
    }

    if (dayCheck.started) {
      if (dayCheck.isPreviousDay) {
        return {
          success: false,
          message: '⛔ Previous Day Still Open!\n\nDate: ' + dayCheck.dayDateDisplay +
                   '\n\nPehle Day End karo, tab hi naya Day Begin ho sakta hai.',
          isPreviousDay: true,
          openDayDate:   dayCheck.dayDateDisplay
        };
      }
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⚠️ Aaj ka Day already started hai!',
        isPreviousDay: false
      };
    }
    // Record day start
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let daySheet = ss.getSheetByName('DAY_STATUS');
    
    // ✅ FIX: Create DAY_STATUS sheet if not exists
    if (!daySheet) {
      daySheet = ss.insertSheet('DAY_STATUS');
      daySheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setValues([
        ['Branch Code', 'Date', 'Status', 'Started By', 'Ended By', 'Timestamp']
      ]);
      daySheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#28a745')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    // Add new day record
    const today = new Date();
    daySheet.appendRow([
      branchCode,           // Column A: Branch Code
      today,                // Column B: Date
      'OPEN',               // Column C: Status
      supervisorId,         // Column D: Started By
      '',                   // Column E: Ended By (empty for now)
      today                 // Column F: Timestamp
    ]);
    
    // Also log in DAY_OPERATIONS if it exists
    const dayOpsSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DAY_OPERATIONS');
    if (dayOpsSheet) {
      dayOpsSheet.appendRow([
        today,
        branchCode,
        supervisorId,
        'DAY_BEGIN',
        0, // Opening balance
        0, // Closing balance
        'OPEN',
        today
      ]);
    }
    
    logActivity(supervisorId, 'DAY_BEGIN', 
      'Day started for branch ' + branchCode + ' - Cash to be loaded separately');

    // ✅ BALANCE LOG: Save opening balance snapshot
    try { saveOpeningBalance(supervisorId, branchCode); } catch(be) {
      Logger.log('Opening balance log warning: ' + be.toString());
    }
    
    // ✅ Holiday warning on Day Begin
    var hCheck = isHolidayToday();
    return {
      success: true,
      message: hCheck.isHoliday
        ? '✅ Day started!\n\n🏖️ Note: Aaj ' + (hCheck.description || 'Holiday') + ' hai. Emergency kaam ke liye Day Begin ho gaya.'
        : '✅ Day started successfully!',
      branchCode:   branchCode,
      supervisorId: supervisorId,
      dayStatus:    'OPEN',
      isHoliday:    hCheck.isHoliday || false
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Start day error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}



/**
 * Check operator wallets for a branch
 */
function checkOperatorWallets(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { allClear: true, operators: [] };
    }
    
    const data = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    const operators = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const role = String(data[i][1]).toUpperCase();
      const branch = String(data[i][2]);
      const balance = parseFloat(data[i][3]) || 0;
      
      if (role === 'OPERATOR' && branch === branchCode && balance > 0) {
        operators.push({
          userId: data[i][0],
          balance: balance
        });
      }
    }
    
    return {
      allClear: operators.length === 0,
      operators: operators
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Check operator wallets error: ' + e.toString());
    return { allClear: false, operators: [] };
  }
}
