/**
 * Get wallet transactions for a user
 */
function getWalletTransactions(userId, days) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_TRANSACTIONS');
    
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, transactions: [] };
    }
    
    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    const transactions = [];
    
    const daysAgo = new Date();
    if (days) {
      daysAgo.setDate(daysAgo.getDate() - days);
    }
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const fromUser = String(data[i][1]).toUpperCase();
      const toUser = String(data[i][2]).toUpperCase();
      const transDate = new Date(data[i][5]);
      
      if ((fromUser === userId.toUpperCase() || toUser === userId.toUpperCase()) &&
          (!days || transDate >= daysAgo)) {
        transactions.push({
          transactionId: data[i][0],
          fromUser: fromUser,
          toUser: toUser,
          amount: data[i][3],
          type: data[i][4],
          date: formatDate(data[i][5]),
          remarks: data[i][6],
          branchCode: data[i][7]
        });
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, transactions: transactions };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get wallet transactions error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getOperatorsWithWallets(supervisorId) {
  try {
    // Verify supervisor
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can view operator wallets' };
    }
    
    // Get supervisor's branch
    const supervisorBranch = getBranchCodeFromUser(supervisorId);
    
    if (!supervisorBranch) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found' };
    }
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Get all operators from same branch
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    const operators = [];
    
    if (userSheet && userSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const userData = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < userData.length; i++) {
        const role = String(userData[i][2]).toUpperCase();
        const branchCode = String(userData[i][3]);
        const status = String(userData[i][7]).toUpperCase();
        
        // Only ACTIVE operators from SAME BRANCH
        if (role === 'OPERATOR' && branchCode === supervisorBranch && status === 'ACTIVE') {
          const userId = String(userData[i][0]);
          
          // Get wallet balance
          const walletResult = getWalletBalance(userId);
          const balance = walletResult.success ? walletResult.balance : 0;
          
          operators.push({
            userId: userId,
            name: String(userData[i][1]),
            branchCode: branchCode,
            balance: balance
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('Operators for supervisor ' + supervisorId + ': ' + operators.length);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      operators: operators,
      supervisorBranch: supervisorBranch
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get operators with wallets error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function generateDayEndReport(supervisorId, reportDate) {
  try {
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can generate reports' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX: getBranchCodeFromOperator returns object
    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found for supervisor' };
    }
    var branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();
    if (!branchCode) return { success: false, message: 'Branch code is empty' };

    var ss  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz  = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    // ✅ FIX: Parse date correctly
    var dateStr;
    try {
      dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(reportDate), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    } catch(de) {
      dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    }

    var deposits    = { count: 0, total: 0 };
    var repayments  = { count: 0, total: 0 };
    var loans       = { count: 0, total: 0 };

    // ── DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT ──
    // A=AccountNo | B=Name | C=Amount | D=Interest | E=Balance | F=Date | K=BranchCode
    var depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 11).getValues();
      for (var d = 0; d < depData.length; d++) {
        var depBranch = String(depData[d][10] || '').trim(); // Col K
        if (depBranch !== branchCode) continue;
        var depDateVal = depData[d][5]; // ✅ Col F = Date
        if (!depDateVal) continue;
        try {
          var depDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(depDateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          if (depDate === dateStr) {
            deposits.count++;
            deposits.total += (parseFloat(depData[d][2]) || 0) + (parseFloat(depData[d][3]) || 0); // ✅ Col C + D
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    }

    // ── LOAN MANAGEMENT ──
    // A=MemberID | B=LoanAC | C=Name | D=LoanType | E=ROI | F=LoanAmount | G=LoanDate | O=BranchCode
    var loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      for (var l = 0; l < loanData.length; l++) {
        var loanDateVal = loanData[l][6]; // ✅ Col G = Loan_Date
        if (!loanDateVal) continue;
        try {
          var loanDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(loanDateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          var loanBranch = String(loanData[l][14] || '').trim(); // Col O
          if (loanDate === dateStr && (!loanBranch || loanBranch === branchCode)) {
            loans.count++;
            loans.total += parseFloat(loanData[l][5]) || 0; // ✅ Col F = Loan_Amount
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    }

    // ── LOAN REPAY ──
    // A=LoanAcNo | B=PaidAmt | C=MonthFor | D=Interest | E=DefaultFee | F=BranchCode
    // ⚠️ No date column — filter by branch only
    var repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
if (repaySheet && repaySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
  var repayData = repaySheet.getRange(2, 1, repaySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues(); // ✅ 7 cols
  for (var r = 0; r < repayData.length; r++) {
    var repBranch = String(repayData[r][5] || '').trim(); // Col F
    if (repBranch !== branchCode) continue;
    
    // ✅ Ab date se filter karo
    var repDateVal = repayData[r][6]; // Col G = Date
    if (repDateVal) {
      try {
        var repDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(repDateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        if (repDateStr !== dateStr) continue; // ✅ sirf us din ki entries
      } catch(e) { continue; }
    }
    
    repayments.count++;
    repayments.total += (parseFloat(repayData[r][1]) || 0) +
                        (parseFloat(repayData[r][3]) || 0) +
                        (parseFloat(repayData[r][4]) || 0);
  }
}

    // ── DAY_OPERATIONS info ──
    var dayInfo = { openingBalance: 0, closingBalance: 0, status: 'NOT STARTED' };
    var daySheet = ss.getSheetByName('DAY_OPERATIONS');
    if (daySheet && daySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var dayData = daySheet.getRange(2, 1, daySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (var i = dayData.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (!dayData[i][0]) continue;
        var dBranch = String(dayData[i][1] || '').trim();
        var dOp     = String(dayData[i][3] || '').toUpperCase();
        var dDate   = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(dayData[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        if (dBranch === branchCode && dDate === dateStr && dOp === 'DAY_BEGIN') {
          dayInfo.openingBalance = parseFloat(dayData[i][4]) || 0;
          dayInfo.closingBalance = parseFloat(dayData[i][5]) || 0;
          dayInfo.status         = String(dayData[i][6] || '');
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    var netCollection = deposits.total + repayments.total - loans.total;

    return {
      success: true,
      report: {
        date:             dateStr,
        branchCode:       branchCode,
        totalDeposits:    deposits.total,
        depositCount:     deposits.count,
        totalRepayments:  repayments.total,
        repaymentCount:   repayments.count,
        totalDisbursements: loans.total,
        disbursementCount:  loans.count,
        netCollection:    netCollection,
        openingBalance:   dayInfo.openingBalance,
        closingBalance:   dayInfo.closingBalance,
        dayStatus:        dayInfo.status
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('generateDayEndReport error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Generate complete passbook for an account
 */
// PURANA function (line 8877-8959) replace karo with:
function generatePassbook(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    if (!accountNo) return { success: false, message: 'Account number required' };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // ✅ FIX 1: ACCOUNT OPEN — correct column mapping
    // A=MemberID | B=Name | C=AccountNo | D=OpenDate | E=AccountType
    // F=Nominee | G=Relation | H=Status | I=Email | J=UserId | K=Photo | L=DOB | M=Branch
    const accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSheet || accountSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }

    const accountData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    let account = null;

    for (let i = 0; i < accountData.length; i++) {
      // ✅ FIX: Col C (index 2) = ACCOUNT NO
      if (String(accountData[i][2]).trim() === accountNo) {
        account = {
          memberId:    String(accountData[i][0] || ''),
          name:        String(accountData[i][1] || ''),
          accountNo:   String(accountData[i][2] || ''),
          openDate:    accountData[i][3] ? formatDate(accountData[i][3]) : '',
          accountType: String(accountData[i][4] || ''),
          status:      String(accountData[i][7] || '')
        };
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!account) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account not found: ' + accountNo };
    }

    // ✅ FIX 2: Current balance — DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT se lo (last entry)
    // A=Account_Number | B=Name | C=Amount | D=Interest | E=Current_Balance | F=Date
    let currentBalance = 0;
    const depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    const transactions = [];

    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const depositData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();

      for (let i = 0; i < depositData.length; i++) {
        // ✅ FIX: Col A (index 0) = Account_Number
        if (String(depositData[i][0]).trim() === accountNo) {
          currentBalance = parseFloat(depositData[i][4]) || 0; // Col E = Current_Balance

          transactions.push({
            date:          depositData[i][5] ? formatDate(depositData[i][5]) : '', // Col F
            transactionId: 'DEP-' + (i + 2),         // row number as ID
            amount:        parseFloat(depositData[i][2]) || 0, // Col C = Amount
            interest:      parseFloat(depositData[i][3]) || 0, // Col D = Interest
            monthFor:      String(depositData[i][6] || ''),    // Col G
            type:          'DEPOSIT',
            balance:       parseFloat(depositData[i][4]) || 0  // Col E = Running balance
          });
        }
      }
    }
    // Sort by date (oldest first)
    transactions.sort(function(a, b) {
      var da = a.date ? new Date(a.date.split('/').reverse().join('-')) : new Date(0);
      var db = b.date ? new Date(b.date.split('/').reverse().join('-')) : new Date(0);
      return da - db;
    });

    return {
      success:           true,
      account:           account,
      currentBalance:    currentBalance,
      transactions:      transactions,
      totalTransactions: transactions.length
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('generatePassbook error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Generate transaction receipt
 */
function generateTransactionReceipt(transactionId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Check in deposits
    const depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT_DETAILS');
    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const data = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return {
            success: true,
            transaction: {
              id: data[i][0],
              accountNo: data[i][1],
              date: data[i][2],
              amount: data[i][3],
              type: 'DEPOSIT',
              remarks: data[i][4] || ''
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check in loan disbursements
    const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN_DETAILS');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const data = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return {
            success: true,
            transaction: {
              id: data[i][0],
              accountNo: data[i][1],
              date: data[i][3],
              amount: data[i][4],
              type: 'LOAN DISBURSEMENT',
              remarks: ''
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Check in repayments
    const repaymentSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN_REPAYMENT');
    if (repaymentSheet && repaymentSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const data = repaymentSheet.getRange(2, 1, repaymentSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]) === transactionId) {
          return {
            success: true,
            transaction: {
              id: data[i][0],
              accountNo: data[i][1],
              date: data[i][2],
              amount: data[i][3],
              type: 'LOAN REPAYMENT',
              remarks: data[i][4] || ''
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Transaction not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Generate receipt error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 🧾 TRANSACTION RECEIPT GENERATION
// ============================================

/**
 * Generate Receipt for a transaction
 */
function generateReceipt(transactionId, userId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Search in deposits
    const depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const depositData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < depositData.length; i++) {
        if (String(depositData[i][9]) === String(transactionId)) { // Column J - Transaction ID
          return {
            success: true,
            receipt: {
              type: 'DEPOSIT',
              transactionId: depositData[i][9],
              accountNo: depositData[i][0],
              customerName: depositData[i][1],
              amount: depositData[i][2],
              date: formatDate(depositData[i][5]),
              operatorId: depositData[i][8],
              remarks: depositData[i][7] || '',
              branchCode: depositData[i][depositSheet.getLastColumn() - 1]
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Search in loans
    const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 20).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
        if (String(loanData[i][14]) === String(transactionId)) { // Column O - Transaction ID
          return {
            success: true,
            receipt: {
              type: 'LOAN',
              transactionId: loanData[i][14],
              loanAccount: loanData[i][1],
              customerName: loanData[i][2],
              amount: loanData[i][5],
              date: formatDate(loanData[i][6]),
              loanType: loanData[i][3],
              roi: loanData[i][4],
              operatorId: loanData[i][13],
              remarks: loanData[i][12] || '',
              branchCode: loanData[i][loanSheet.getLastColumn() - 1]
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Search in repayments
    const repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    if (repaySheet && repaySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const repayData = repaySheet.getRange(2, 1, repaySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < repayData.length; i++) {
        if (String(repayData[i][8]) === String(transactionId)) { // Column I - Transaction ID
          return {
            success: true,
            receipt: {
              type: 'REPAYMENT',
              transactionId: repayData[i][8],
              loanAccount: repayData[i][0],
              customerName: repayData[i][2],
              amount: repayData[i][3],
              date: formatDate(repayData[i][4]),
              operatorId: repayData[i][6],
              remarks: repayData[i][5] || '',
              branchCode: repayData[i][repaySheet.getLastColumn() - 1]
            }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Transaction not found: ' + transactionId };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Generate receipt error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 📈 PAYMENT SUMMARY REPORT
// ============================================

/**
 * Generate Payment Summary Report
 * Date-wise, category-wise breakdown
 */
function generatePaymentSummary(supervisorId, fromDate, toDate) {
  try {
    // Verify supervisor
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can generate reports' };
    }
    
    const branchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    
    if (!branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found' };
    }
    
    fromDate = fromDate || new Date();
    toDate = toDate || new Date();
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const depositSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    const repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    
    const summary = {
      fromDate: formatDate(new Date(fromDate)),
      toDate: formatDate(new Date(toDate)),
      branchCode: branchCode,
      
      deposits: [],
      loans: [],
      repayments: [],
      
      totals: {
        deposits: 0,
        loans: 0,
        repayments: 0,
        net: 0
      }
    };
    
    // Process deposits
    if (depositSheet && depositSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const depositData = depositSheet.getRange(2, 1, depositSheet.getLastRow() - 1, depositSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < depositData.length; i++) {
        const transDate = new Date(depositData[i][5]);
        const transBranch = String(depositData[i][depositSheet.getLastColumn() - 1] || '');
        
        if (transDate >= new Date(fromDate) && transDate <= new Date(toDate) && transBranch === branchCode) {
          summary.deposits.push({
            date: formatDate(depositData[i][5]),
            accountNo: depositData[i][0],
            name: depositData[i][1],
            amount: depositData[i][2],
            transactionId: depositData[i][9]
          });
          summary.totals.deposits += parseFloat(depositData[i][2]) || 0;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Process loans
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, loanSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < loanData.length; i++) {
        const transDate = new Date(loanData[i][6]);
        const transBranch = String(loanData[i][loanSheet.getLastColumn() - 1] || '');
        
        if (transDate >= new Date(fromDate) && transDate <= new Date(toDate) && transBranch === branchCode) {
          summary.loans.push({
            date: formatDate(loanData[i][6]),
            loanAccount: loanData[i][1],
            name: loanData[i][2],
            amount: loanData[i][5],
            transactionId: loanData[i][14]
          });
          summary.totals.loans += parseFloat(loanData[i][5]) || 0;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Process repayments
    if (repaySheet && repaySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const repayData = repaySheet.getRange(2, 1, repaySheet.getLastRow() - 1, repaySheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
      
      for (let i = 0; i < repayData.length; i++) {
        const transDate = new Date(repayData[i][4]);
        const transBranch = String(repayData[i][repaySheet.getLastColumn() - 1] || '');
        
        if (transDate >= new Date(fromDate) && transDate <= new Date(toDate) && transBranch === branchCode) {
          summary.repayments.push({
            date: formatDate(repayData[i][4]),
            loanAccount: repayData[i][0],
            name: repayData[i][2],
            amount: repayData[i][3],
            transactionId: repayData[i][8]
          });
          summary.totals.repayments += parseFloat(repayData[i][3]) || 0;
        }
      }
    }
    
    summary.totals.net = summary.totals.deposits + summary.totals.repayments - summary.totals.loans;
    
    return {
      success: true,
      summary: summary
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Generate payment summary error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// 👤 CUSTOMER STATEMENT
// ============================================

/**
 * Generate Customer Statement
 * Complete account history + outstanding loans
 */
function generateCustomerStatement(accountNo, supervisorId) {
  try {
    accountNo    = String(accountNo    || '').trim();
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();

    if (!accountNo) return { success: false, message: 'Account number required' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    // ── Get account details from ACCOUNT OPEN ──
    // A=MemberID | B=Name | C=AccountNo | D=OpenDate | E=AccountType | H=Status | M=BranchCode
    var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSheet || accountSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }

    var accData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accountInfo = null;

    for (var a = 0; a < accData.length; a++) {
      if (String(accData[a][2]).trim() === accountNo) { // Col C = AccountNo
        accountInfo = {
          memberId:    String(accData[a][0] || ''),
          name:        String(accData[a][1] || ''),
          accountNo:   String(accData[a][2] || ''),
          openDate:    accData[a][3] ? formatDate(accData[a][3]) : '',
          accountType: String(accData[a][4] || ''),
          status:      String(accData[a][7] || ''),
          branchCode:  String(accData[a][12] || '')
        };
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!accountInfo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account not found: ' + accountNo };
    }

    // ── Get all deposits for this account ──
    var transactions = [];
    var currentBalance = 0;
    var depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
      for (var d = 0; d < depData.length; d++) {
        if (String(depData[d][0]).trim() !== accountNo) continue;
        var depAmt  = parseFloat(depData[d][2]) || 0;
        var depInt  = parseFloat(depData[d][3]) || 0;
        var depBal  = parseFloat(depData[d][4]) || 0;
        var depDate = depData[d][5] ? formatDate(depData[d][5]) : '';
        currentBalance = depBal;
        transactions.push({
          date:      depDate,
          type:      'DEPOSIT',
          amount:    depAmt,
          interest:  depInt,
          monthFor:  String(depData[d][6] || ''),
          balance:   depBal
        });
      }
    }

    // ── Get loans for this member ──
    var loans = [];
    var loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 11).getValues();
      for (var l = 0; l < loanData.length; l++) {
        if (String(loanData[l][0]).trim() !== accountInfo.memberId) continue; // Col A = MemberID
        loans.push({
          loanAcNo:   String(loanData[l][1] || ''),
          loanType:   String(loanData[l][3] || ''),
          amount:     parseFloat(loanData[l][5]) || 0,
          loanDate:   loanData[l][6] ? formatDate(loanData[l][6]) : '',
          totalPaid:  parseFloat(loanData[l][8]) || 0,
          remaining:  parseFloat(loanData[l][9]) || 0,
          status:     String(loanData[l][10] || '')
        });
      }
    }

    return {
      success: true,
      statement: {
        accountInfo:    accountInfo,
        currentBalance: currentBalance,
        transactions:   transactions,
        loans:          loans,
        generatedBy:    supervisorId,
        generatedOn:    formatDate(new Date())
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('generateCustomerStatement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Format currency
 */
function formatCurrency(amount) {
  try {
    return '₹' + parseFloat(amount).toFixed(2);
  } catch (e) {
    return '₹0.00';
  }

// ============================================
// 🔧 FIX 2: GET OPERATOR/SUPERVISOR DETAILS WITH BRANCH
// ============================================

/**
 * Get operator details including branch info
 * For operator dashboard display
 */
function getOperatorDetails(userId) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!userId) return { success: false, message: 'User ID required' };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // ✅ Step 1: Check USER_DETAILS sheet
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    if (userSheet && userSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          const branchCode = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
          const role       = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
          if (branchCode) {
            // Init wallet if needed
            if (role.toUpperCase() === 'OPERATOR') {
              try {
                const w = getWalletBalance(userId);
                if (!w.exists) initializeWallet(userId, 'OPERATOR', branchCode, 0);
              } catch(_) {}
            }
            return {
              success:    true,
              userId:     String(data[i][0]),
              name:       String(data[i][1]),
              role:       role,
              branchCode: branchCode,
              branchName: branchCode
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // ✅ Step 2: CREDENTIALS fallback — Col A: userId, Col C: role, Col D: branchCode
    const credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
      for (let j = 0; j < credData.length; j++) {
        if (String(credData[j][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === userId) {
          const branchCode = String(credData[j][3] || '').trim();
          const role       = String(credData[j][2] || '').trim();
          if (branchCode) {
            Logger.log('getOperatorDetails: found in CREDENTIALS for ' + userId);
            if (role.toUpperCase() === 'OPERATOR') {
              try {
                const w = getWalletBalance(userId);
                if (!w.exists) initializeWallet(userId, 'OPERATOR', branchCode, 0);
              } catch(_) {}
            }
            return {
              success:    true,
              userId:     userId,
              name:       userId,
              role:       role,
              branchCode: branchCode,
              branchName: branchCode
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    Logger.log('getOperatorDetails: not found: ' + userId);
    return { success: false, message: 'Operator not found: ' + userId };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getOperatorDetails error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Get supervisor details including branch info
 * For supervisor dashboard display
 */
function getSupervisorDetails(supervisorId) {
  try {
    const details = getOperatorDetails(supervisorId);
    
    if (details.success) {
      // Initialize wallet if not exists
      const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
      
      if (!walletInfo.exists) {
        // Create wallet with ₹0 balance for supervisor
        initializeWallet(supervisorId, 'SUPERVISOR', details.branchCode, 0);
      }
      
      // Return details with wallet info
      return {
        success: true,
        userId: details.userId,
        name: details.name,
        role: details.role,
        branchCode: details.branchCode,
        branchName: details.branchName,
        walletBalance: walletInfo.balance || 0
      };
    }
    
    return details;
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// ENSURE SUPERVISOR WALLET EXISTS
// ============================================
function ensureSupervisorWallet(supervisorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('=== Ensuring wallet for: ' + supervisorId);
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: USER_DETAILS not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'USER_DETAILS not found' };
    }
    
    // Get user details
    const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    let branchCode = '';
    let role = '';
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(supervisorId).toUpperCase()) {
        branchCode = String(data[i][3]);
        role = String(data[i][2]);
        Logger.log('Found user - Branch: ' + branchCode + ', Role: ' + role);
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (!branchCode) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: Branch code not found');
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found' };
    }
    
    // Check if wallet exists
    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    Logger.log('Wallet check result:', JSON.stringify(walletInfo));
    
    if (!walletInfo.exists) {
      Logger.log('Creating new wallet...');
      // Create wallet
      const initResult = initializeWallet(supervisorId, role, branchCode, 0);
      Logger.log('Init result:', JSON.stringify(initResult));
      
      // Verify creation
      const verifyWallet = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
      Logger.log('Verification:', JSON.stringify(verifyWallet));
      
      return {
        success: true,
        message: 'Wallet created',
        balance: 0,
        created: true
      };
    }
    
    Logger.log('Wallet already exists with balance: ' + walletInfo.balance);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Wallet exists',
      balance: walletInfo.balance,
      created: false
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

      return {

    };

    Logger.log('ERROR getting supervisor wallet balance: ' + e.toString());
    return {
      success: false,
      balance: 0,
      message: e.toString()
    };
  }
}
function submitPendingEntry(entryData) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!sh) {
      // Create sheet with branch code column
      sh = ss.insertSheet('PENDING_ENTRIES');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([
        ['Entry ID', 'Type', 'Data JSON', 'Submitted By', 'Submitted On', 'Status', 'Notes', 'Branch Code']
      ]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#667eea')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    // Generate Entry ID
    const entryId = 'ENT-' + Date.now();
    
    // AUTO: Get operator's branch code
    const operatorId = entryData.operatorId || entryData.submittedBy || entryData.userId;
    const branchCode = getBranchCodeFromUser(operatorId);
    
    if (!branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found for operator' };
    }
    
    Logger.log('Submitting entry - Operator: ' + operatorId + ', Branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    // Append with AUTO branch code
    sh.appendRow([
      entryId,
      entryData.type || '',
      JSON.stringify(entryData.data || {}),
      operatorId,
      new Date(),
      'PENDING',
      '',
      branchCode // Column H - AUTO branch code
    ]);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Entry submitted for approval',
      entryId: entryId,
      branchCode: branchCode
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Submit pending entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


/**
 * UPDATED: Approve pending entry with branch validation
 * This REPLACES any existing approvePendingEntry function
 */
function approvePendingEntry(rowIndex, supervisorId) {
  try {
    // Verify supervisor
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can approve entries' };
    }
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!pendingSheet || rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > pendingSheet.getLastRow()) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid entry' };
    }
    
    // Get supervisor's branch
    const supervisorBranch = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    
    // Get entry details
    const rowData = pendingSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 1, 1, 15).getValues()[0];
    const entryBranch = String(rowData[14]); // Column O - Branch Code
    
    // VALIDATE: Supervisor can only approve entries from their branch
    if (supervisorBranch !== entryBranch) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⛔ Cannot approve!\n\nThis entry is from branch: ' + entryBranch + 
                 '\nYour branch: ' + supervisorBranch + 
                 '\n\nYou can only approve entries from your own branch.'
      };
    }
    
    const entryType = String(rowData[0]);
    
    // Process based on entry type
    let saveResult = { success: false };
    
    if (entryType === 'ACCOUNT_OPEN') {
      saveResult = saveAccountOpen({
        memberId: rowData[1],
        name: rowData[2],
        accountType: rowData[4],
        userId: supervisorId,
        operatorId: rowData[9],
        branchCode: entryBranch // Pass branch code
      });
    } else if (entryType === 'LOAN') {
      saveResult = saveLoanEntry({
        memberId: rowData[1],
        name: rowData[2],
        loanType: rowData[5],
        loanAmount: rowData[6],
        roi: rowData[7],
        monthlyEmi: rowData[8],
        userId: supervisorId,
        operatorId: rowData[9],
        branchCode: entryBranch // Pass branch code
      });
    } else if (entryType === 'ACCOUNT_CLOSE') {
      // Handle account close
      saveResult = { success: true, message: 'Account close approved' };
    }
    
    if (saveResult.success) {
      // Update status
      pendingSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 13).setValue('APPROVED');
      pendingSheet.getRange(rowIndex, 14).setValue(supervisorId);
      
      logActivity(supervisorId, 'APPROVE_ENTRY', 
        'Approved ' + entryType + ' (Row: ' + rowIndex + ', Branch: ' + entryBranch + ')');
      
      return {
        success: true,
        message: 'Entry approved successfully!',
        branchCode: entryBranch
      };
    } else {
      return saveResult;
    }
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Approve pending entry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// DIRECT OPERATOR WALLET FETCH FROM SHEET
// ============================================
function getOperatorWalletBalanceDirect(operatorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('=== Direct fetch operator wallet: ' + operatorId);
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      Logger.log('WALLET_MASTER sheet empty or not found');
      return { success: true, balance: 0 };
    }
    
    const data = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const userId = String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase();
      
      if (userId === String(operatorId).toUpperCase()) {
        const balance = Number(data[i][3]) || 0; // Column D (Current Balance)
        
        Logger.log('✅ Found operator wallet: ' + userId + ' = ₹' + balance);
        
        return {
          success: true,
          balance: balance,
          userId: userId,
          role: String(data[i][1]),
          branch: String(data[i][2])
        };
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('⚠️ Operator not found in WALLET_MASTER');
    return { success: true, balance: 0, note: 'User not found in WALLET_MASTER' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Direct operator wallet fetch: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, balance: 0, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// GET OPERATOR COUNTER STATUS
// ============================================
function getOperatorCounterStatus(operatorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('=== Checking counter status for: ' + operatorId);

    const ss         = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');

    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, allocated: false, message: 'No counter allocated. Please contact supervisor.' };
    }

    const tz    = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data  = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();

    // ✅ FIX 7: Get the branch's open day date — not just today
    // If day started for a previous date and not yet ended, counter from that date must also be visible
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    let checkDate = today;
    if (branchResult && branchResult.success) {
      const openDayInfo = getLastDayStatus(branchResult.branchCode);
      if (openDayInfo && openDayInfo.started && openDayInfo.dayDate) {
        checkDate = openDayInfo.dayDate; // could be yesterday or earlier
      }
    }

    Logger.log('Checking allocations for date: ' + checkDate + ' (today: ' + today + ')');

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (!data[i][0]) continue;
      const allocDate     = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const allocOperator = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const counterNo     = String(data[i][4] || '').trim();
      const status        = String(data[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

      // ✅ Check both open-day date AND today (covers both normal and carry-forward case)
      const dateMatch = (allocDate === checkDate || allocDate === today);

      if (dateMatch && allocOperator === operatorId.toUpperCase() && status === 'OPEN') {
        Logger.log('✅ Active counter found: ' + counterNo + ' from date: ' + allocDate);
        return {
          success:    true,
          allocated:  true,
          counterNo:  counterNo,
          status:     'OPEN',
          allocDate:  allocDate,
          isPrevDay:  allocDate !== today,
          message:    'Counter ' + counterNo + ' allocated' + (allocDate !== today ? ' (previous day — please close)' : '')
        };
      }
    }

    Logger.log('⛔ No active counter found');
    return {
      success:   true,
      allocated: false,
      message:   'No counter allocated. Please contact supervisor.'
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getOperatorCounterStatus ERROR: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, allocated: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 🔧 HELPER: Get Branch Name
// ============================================

/**
 * Get branch name from branch code
 */
function getBranchName(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const branchSheet = ss.getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER');
    
    if (!branchSheet || branchSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return branchCode;
    }
    
    const branchData = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, branchSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < branchData.length; i++) {
      if (String(branchData[i][0]) === branchCode) {
        return String(branchData[i][1]);
      }
    }
    
    return branchCode;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get branch name error: ' + e.toString());
    return branchCode;
  }
}

/**
 * NEW: Validate if day is open for transactions
 */
function validateDayOpen(branchCode) {
  try {
    const dayStarted = isDayStarted(branchCode);
    
    if (!dayStarted) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Day Not Started! Ask supervisor to start the day before making transactions.'
      };
    }
    
    return { success: true };
    
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error checking day status' };
  }
}

/**
 * NEW: Check if user is supervisor
 */
function allocateCounter(supervisorId, operatorId, counterNo, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can allocate counters' };
    }
    
    const supBranch = getBranchCodeFromUser(supervisorId);
    const opBranch = getBranchCodeFromUser(operatorId);
    
    if (supBranch !== opBranch) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Operator not in your branch' };
    }
    
    const dayStarted = isDayStarted(supBranch);
    if (!dayStarted) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Day must be started first' };
    }
    
    let allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    if (!allocSheet) {
      allocSheet = ss.insertSheet('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
      allocSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 9).setValues([[
        'Date', 'Branch Code', 'Supervisor', 'Operator', 'Counter No', 
        'Status', 'Allocated At', 'Closed At'
      ]]);
    }
    
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = allocSheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? 
      allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues() : [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const allocDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      if (allocDate === today && String(data[i][3]) === operatorId && String(data[i][5]) === 'OPEN') {
        return { success: false, message: 'Operator already allocated to Counter ' + data[i][4] };
      }
    }
    allocSheet.appendRow([new Date(), supBranch, supervisorId, operatorId, counterNo,'OPEN', new Date(), '']);
    
    logActivity(supervisorId, 'COUNTER_ALLOCATION', 'Allocated Counter ' + counterNo + ' to ' + operatorId);
    
    return { success: true, message: 'Counter allocated successfully', counterNo: counterNo, operator: operatorId };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Allocate counter error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getCounterAllocations(supervisorId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, allocations: [] };
    
    const branch = getBranchCodeFromUser(supervisorId);
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    const allocations = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const allocDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      if (allocDate === today && String(data[i][1]) === branch) {
        allocations.push({
          operator: String(data[i][3]),
          counterNo: String(data[i][4]),
          cashAmount: Number(data[i][5]),
          status: String(data[i][6]),
          allocatedAt: formatDate(data[i][7])
        });
      }
    }
    return { success: true, allocations: allocations };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function hasActiveCounter(operatorId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return false;
    
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const allocDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      if (allocDate === today && String(data[i][3]) === operatorId && String(data[i][6]) === 'OPEN') {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  } catch (e) {
    return false;
  }
}
function getMemberBranchInfo(userId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (userSheet && userSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === String(userId).toUpperCase()) {
          const branchCode = String(data[i][3]);
          return { success: true, branchCode: branchCode, branchName: branchCode };
        }
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Branch info not found' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function checkWalletBalance(userId, requiredAmount) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, balance: 0, sufficient: false };
    }
    
    const data = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]) === String(userId)) {
        const balance = Number(data[i][1]) || 0;
        const sufficient = balance >= requiredAmount;
        
        return {
          success: true,
          balance: balance,
          required: requiredAmount,
          sufficient: sufficient,
          shortage: sufficient ? 0 : (requiredAmount - balance)
        };
      }
    }
    
    // User not found in wallet
    return {
      success: false,
      balance: 0,
      required: requiredAmount,
      sufficient: false,
      shortage: requiredAmount
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Check wallet balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, balance: 0, sufficient: false };
  }
}
/**
 * Close operator counter and return cash to supervisor
 * @param {string} operatorId - Operator ID
 * @param {number} returnAmount - Amount in operator wallet to return
 */
/**
 * Close operator counter
 * Works with ANY balance - zero or positive
 */
function closeOperatorCounter(operatorId, returnAmount) {
  try {
    Logger.log('=== CLOSE COUNTER START ===');
    Logger.log('Operator: ' + operatorId);
    Logger.log('Return amount: ₹' + returnAmount);
    
    // ✅ Convert to number and handle zero/null/undefined
    returnAmount = parseFloat(returnAmount) || 0;
    
    // Get operator branch code
    const branchInfo = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    if (!branchInfo || !branchInfo.success) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: Could not get branch code');
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'Could not get operator branch information. Contact admin.' 
      };
    }
    
    const branchCode = branchInfo.branchCode;
    Logger.log('Branch: ' + branchCode);
    
    // Get supervisor for this branch
    const supervisorId = getSupervisorForBranch(branchCode);
    if (!supervisorId) {
      Logger.log('ERROR: No supervisor found for branch: ' + branchCode);
      return { 
        success: false, 
        message: 'No supervisor found for your branch. Contact admin.' 
      };
    }
    
    Logger.log('Supervisor: ' + supervisorId);
    
    // ✅ ONLY transfer cash if amount > 0
    if (returnAmount > 0) {
      Logger.log('💰 Transferring ₹' + returnAmount + ' from operator to supervisor...');
      
      // Get wallet balances
      const opWallet = getWalletBalance(operatorId);
      const supWallet = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
      
      if (!opWallet.success || !supWallet.success) {
        Logger.log('ERROR: Could not get wallet balances');
        return { 
          success: false, 
          message: 'Wallet error. Cannot retrieve balances.' 
        };
      }
      
      // Validate operator has enough balance
      const opBalance = parseFloat(opWallet.balance) || 0;
      if (opBalance < returnAmount) {
        Logger.log('ERROR: Insufficient balance. Has: ₹' + opBalance + ', Needs: ₹' + returnAmount);
        return { 
          success: false, 
          message: 'Insufficient wallet balance. Available: ₹' + opBalance 
        };
      }
      
      // Deduct from operator
      const newOpBalance = opBalance - returnAmount;
      updateWalletBalance(operatorId, newOpBalance);
      Logger.log('Operator new balance: ₹' + newOpBalance);
      
      // Add to supervisor
      const supBalance = parseFloat(supWallet.balance) || 0;
      const newSupBalance = supBalance + returnAmount;
      updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newSupBalance);
      Logger.log('Supervisor new balance: ₹' + newSupBalance);
      
      // Record transaction
      const transId = 'WT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
      recordWalletTransaction(
        transId,
        operatorId,
        supervisorId,
        returnAmount,
        'CASH_RETURN',
        'Counter closure - cash return',
        branchCode
      );
      
      Logger.log('Transaction recorded: ' + transId);
    } else {
      Logger.log('ℹ️ No cash to transfer (balance is zero)');
    }
    
    // ✅ Mark counter as CLOSED in COUNTER_ALLOCATION sheet
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    
    if (!allocSheet) {
      Logger.log('WARNING: COUNTER_ALLOCATION sheet not found');
      // Don't fail - just log warning and continue
    } else {
      const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
      const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

      // ✅ FIX: Also check previous open day date in case this is a previous-day close
      const branchForCounter = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      const openDayInfo = (branchForCounter && branchForCounter.success)
        ? getLastDayStatus(branchForCounter.branchCode)
        : { started: false };
      const checkDate = (openDayInfo.started && openDayInfo.dayDate)
        ? openDayInfo.dayDate
        : today;

      const lastRow = allocSheet.getLastRow();

      if (lastRow > 1) {
        const data = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 9).getValues();

        let counterClosed = false;

        for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
          if (!data[i][0]) continue;
          const allocDate     = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          const allocOperator = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          const allocStatus   = String(data[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

          // ✅ FIX: Match against checkDate (open day date) instead of only today
          if ((allocDate === checkDate || allocDate === today) && allocOperator === operatorId.toUpperCase() && allocStatus === 'OPEN') {
            // Update counter status to CLOSED
            allocSheet.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('CLOSED');  // Column F - Status
            allocSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date()); // Column H - Closed At
            
            Logger.log('✅ Counter allocation marked as CLOSED (Row ' + (i + 2) + ')');
            counterClosed = true;
            break;
          }
        }
        
        if (!counterClosed) {
          Logger.log('WARNING: No OPEN counter found for operator ' + operatorId + ' today');
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Log activity
    const activityMsg = returnAmount > 0 
      ? 'Counter closed, returned ₹' + returnAmount + ' to ' + supervisorId
      : 'Counter closed (no cash to return)';
    
    logActivity(operatorId, 'CLOSE_COUNTER', activityMsg);
    
    Logger.log('✅ CLOSE COUNTER SUCCESS');
    Logger.log('=== CLOSE COUNTER END ===');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Counter closed successfully',
      cashReturned: returnAmount,
      returnedTo: supervisorId,
      operatorBalance: 0
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ ERROR closing counter: ' + e.toString());
    Logger.log('Stack: ' + e.stack);
    return { 
      success: false, 
      message: 'System error: ' + e.toString() 
    };
  }
}
/**
 * Get all operators with cash in wallet (for day end validation)
 */
function getOperatorWalletsWithBalance(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    const credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    
    if (!walletSheet || !credSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return [];
    }
    
    const walletData = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
    const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
    
    const operatorsWithCash = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < walletData.length; i++) {
      const userId = String(walletData[i][0]);
      const balance = Number(walletData[i][1]) || 0;
      
      if (balance > 0) {
        // Check if user is operator from same branch
        for (let j = 0; j < credData.length; j++) {
          if (String(credData[j][0]) === userId && 
              String(credData[j][2]).toUpperCase() === 'OPERATOR' &&
              String(credData[j][3]) === branchCode) {
            operatorsWithCash.push({
              operatorId: userId,
              balance: balance
            });
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    return operatorsWithCash;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get operators with balance error: ' + e.toString());
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Get count of open counters for a branch
 */
function getOpenCounters(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    
    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return [];
    }
    
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const data = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
    
    const openCounters = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const allocDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      
      if (allocDate === today && 
          String(data[i][1]) === branchCode && 
          String(data[i][6]) === 'OPEN') {
        openCounters.push({
          operator: String(data[i][3]),
          counter: String(data[i][4])
        });
      }
    }
    
    return openCounters;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get open counters error: ' + e.toString());
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Get count of pending entries for a branch
 */
function getPendingEntriesCount(branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!pendingSheet || pendingSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return 0;
    }
    
    const data = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    let count = 0;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const status = String(data[i][5]).toUpperCase(); // Column F - Status
      const entryBranch = String(data[i][7]); // Column H - Branch Code
      
      if (status === 'PENDING' && entryBranch === branchCode) {
        count++;
      }
    }
    
    return count;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get pending entries count error: ' + e.toString());
    return 0;
  }
}
// ============================================
// GET OPERATOR WALLETS (FOR SUPERVISOR)
// ============================================
function getOperatorWallets(supervisorId) {
  try {
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Only supervisors can view operator wallets' };
    }
    
    const branchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found' };
    }
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    
    if (!walletSheet || walletSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, operators: [] };
    }
    
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    const data = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    const operators = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const userId = String(data[i][0]);
      const role = String(data[i][1]).toUpperCase();
      const branch = String(data[i][2]);
      const balance = Number(data[i][3]) || 0;
      
      // Only show operators from same branch
      if (role === 'OPERATOR' && branch === branchCode) {
        // Get operator name from USER_DETAILS
        let operatorName = userId;
        if (userSheet && userSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
          const userData = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
          for (let j = 0; j < userData.length; j++) {
            if (String(userData[j][0]).toUpperCase() === userId.toUpperCase()) {
              operatorName = String(userData[j][1]) || userId;
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        
        operators.push({
          operatorId: userId,
          name: operatorName,
          balance: balance,
          branch: branch
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Sort by operator ID
    operators.sort((a, b) => a.operatorId.localeCompare(b.operatorId));
    
    return { success: true, operators: operators };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get operator wallets error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function generateSchemeWiseReport(branchCode, scheme) {
  try {
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    scheme     = String(scheme     || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // ✅ FIX: Sahi sheet naam — 'ACCOUNT OPEN' (na ki 'ACCOUNT_DETAILS')
    // A=MemberID | B=Name | C=AccountNo | D=OpenDate | E=AccountType | H=Status | M=BranchCode
    var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSheet || accountSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No accounts found in ACCOUNT OPEN sheet' };
    }

    var data = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accounts   = [];
    var totalBalance  = 0;
    var activeCount   = 0;
    var inactiveCount = 0;

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var accBranch = String(data[i][12] || '').trim(); // Col M = Branch Code
      if (branchCode && accBranch !== branchCode) continue;

      var accountType = String(data[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); // Col E
      if (scheme && accountType !== scheme) continue;

      var status     = String(data[i][7] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); // Col H
      var accountNo  = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();               // Col C
      var memberId   = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();               // Col A
      var name       = String(data[i][1] || '').trim();               // Col B

      // Get current balance from DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT — last entry for this account
      var balance = 0;
      var depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
      if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        var depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
        for (var d = depData.length - 1; d >= 0; d--) {
          if (String(depData[d][0]).trim() === accountNo) {
            balance = parseFloat(depData[d][4]) || 0; // Col E = Current_Balance
            break;
          }
        }
      }

      accounts.push({
        accountNo:   accountNo,
        memberId:    memberId,
        name:        name,
        accountType: accountType,
        openDate:    data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : '',
        status:      status || 'ACTIVE',
        balance:     balance
      });

      totalBalance += balance;
      if (status === 'ACTIVE' || status === '') activeCount++;
      else inactiveCount++;
    }

    return {
      success:          true,
      scheme:           scheme || 'ALL',
      branchCode:       branchCode,
      totalAccounts:    accounts.length,
      activeAccounts:   activeCount,
      inactiveAccounts: inactiveCount,
      totalBalance:     totalBalance,
      accounts:         accounts
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('generateSchemeWiseReport error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// BACKUP CREATION
// ============================================
function createDatabaseBackup(adminId, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(adminId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const backupId = 'BACKUP_' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss');
    
    // Create backup in a new spreadsheet
    const backupSS = SpreadsheetApp.create(backupId);
    const sourceSheets = ss.getSheets();
    
    // Copy all sheets
    for (let i = 0; i < sourceSheets.length; i++) {
      sourceSheets[i].copyTo(backupSS);
    }
    
    // Delete default sheet
    const defaultSheet = backupSS.getSheetByName('Sheet1');
    if (defaultSheet) {
      backupSS.deleteSheet(defaultSheet);
    }
    
    logActivity(userId, 'CREATE_BACKUP', 'Database backup created: ' + backupId);
    
    return {
      success: true,
      backupId: backupId,
      timestamp: new Date().toString(),
      fileUrl: backupSS.getUrl()
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Backup error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function exportBranchData(userId, exportType) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const branchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(userId);
    const fileName = 'EXPORT_' + (exportType === 'ALL' ? 'ALL' : branchCode) + '_' + 
                     Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss');
    
    // Create new spreadsheet for export
    const exportSS = SpreadsheetApp.create(fileName);
    
    // Export logic based on type
    if (exportType === 'ALL') {
      // Copy all sheets
      const sheets = ss.getSheets();
      for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
        sheets[i].copyTo(exportSS);
      }
    } else {
      // Copy only branch-specific data
      // Implementation would filter data by branch code
    }
    
    // Delete default sheet
    const defaultSheet = exportSS.getSheetByName('Sheet1');
    if (defaultSheet) {
      exportSS.deleteSheet(defaultSheet);
    }
    
    logActivity(userId, 'EXPORT_DATA', 'Exported ' + exportType + ' data');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      fileName: fileName,
      fileUrl: exportSS.getUrl()
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// OPERATOR FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function operatorReceiveCashFromSupervisor(operatorId, amount) {
  try {
    const branchCode = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const supervisorId = getSupervisorForBranch(branchCode);
    
    if (!supervisorId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor not found for your branch' };
    }
    
    // Transfer cash from supervisor to operator
    const result = transferCashToOperator(supervisorId, operatorId, amount, 'Cash received by operator');
    
    if (result.success) {
      logActivity(operatorId, 'RECEIVE_CASH', 'Received ₹' + amount + ' from supervisor');
    }
    
    return result;
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getRejectedEntries(operatorId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    
    if (!pendingSheet || pendingSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, entries: [] };
    }
    
    const data = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    const entries = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][3]) === operatorId && String(data[i][5]) === 'REJECTED') {
        entries.push({
          rowIndex: i + 2,
          entryId: String(data[i][0]),
          type: String(data[i][1]),
          dataJSON: String(data[i][2]),
          operator: String(data[i][3]),
          submitted: formatDate(data[i][4]),
          status: String(data[i][5]),
          notes: String(data[i][6])
        });
      }
    }
    
    return { success: true, entries: entries };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
