// ============================================
function getSupervisorDayStatus(branchCode) {
  // ✅ FEATURE 1: Wrapper around getLastDayStatus
  try {
    const info = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
    return {
      success:       true,
      dayStatus:     info.started ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSED',
      dayDate:       info.dayDate || '',
      dayDateDisplay: info.dayDateDisplay || '',
      isToday:       info.isToday || false,
      isPreviousDay: info.isPreviousDay || false,
      branchCode:    branchCode
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: true, dayStatus: 'CLOSED' };
  }
}
// ============================================
// CASH ACKNOWLEDGEMENT SYSTEM
// ============================================

/**
 * Get pending cash acknowledgements for operator
 */
function getPendingCashAcknowledgements(operatorId) {
  try {
    Logger.log('=== Getting pending cash acknowledgements for: ' + operatorId);
    
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
    
    // Create sheet if doesn't exist
    if (!ackSheet) {
      ackSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
        'Transaction ID', 'Date', 'Supervisor ID', 'Operator ID', 'Amount', 
        'Remarks', 'Status', 'Acknowledged At', 'Branch Code', 'Timestamp'
      ]]);
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#27ae60')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    if (ackSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, transfers: [], count: 0 };
    }
    
    const data = ackSheet.getRange(2, 1, ackSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    const transfers = [];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const operator = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
      const status = String(data[i][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      
      if (operator.toUpperCase() === operatorId.toUpperCase() && status === 'PENDING') {
        transfers.push({
          transactionId: String(data[i][0]),
          date: formatDate(data[i][1]),
          supervisorId: String(data[i][2]),
          operatorId: String(data[i][3]),
          amount: Number(data[i][4]) || 0,
          remarks: String(data[i][5] || ''),
          status: status,
          rowIndex: i + 2
        });
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log('Found ' + transfers.length + ' pending transfers');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      transfers: transfers,
      count: transfers.length
    };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Get pending acknowledgements: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString(), transfers: [], count: 0 };
  }
}

/**
 * Acknowledge cash transfer
 */
function acknowledgeCashTransfer(operatorId, transactionId) {
  // ✅ FIX C-1: LockService — race condition rokta hai (concurrent acknowledgements prevent karta hai)
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }

  try {
    Logger.log('=== Acknowledging cash transfer: ' + transactionId);

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');

    if (!ackSheet || ackSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No pending transfers found' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX C-1: Fresh read INSIDE lock — stale data se bacho
    const data = ackSheet.getRange(2, 1, ackSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const txnId    = String(data[i][0]).trim();
      const operator = String(data[i][3]).trim();
      const amount   = Number(data[i][4]) || 0;
      const status   = String(data[i][6]).trim().toUpperCase();
      const branchCode = String(data[i][8]);

      if (txnId === transactionId && operator.toUpperCase() === operatorId.toUpperCase() && status === 'PENDING') {

        // ✅ FIX C-1: Status ACKNOWLEDGED mein set karo PEHLE wallet update se — double-ack block
        ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue('ACKNOWLEDGED');
        ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date());

        // Ab wallet update karo (lock ke andar — safe read-modify-write)
        const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(operatorId);
        if (!walletInfo.success) {
          // Rollback status
          ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue('PENDING');
          ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue('');
          return { success: false, message: 'Failed to get wallet balance' };
        }

        const newBalance = (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) + amount;
        updateWalletBalance(operatorId, newBalance);

        recordWalletTransaction(
          'ACK' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8),
          'SUPERVISOR', operatorId, amount,
          'CASH_TRANSFER_ACKNOWLEDGED',
          'Cash acknowledged TxnID: ' + transactionId,
          branchCode
        );

        logActivity(operatorId, 'CASH_ACKNOWLEDGED',
          'Acknowledged ₹' + amount + ' from ' + data[i][2] + ' (ID: ' + transactionId + ')');

        Logger.log('✅ Cash acknowledged: ₹' + amount + ', New balance: ₹' + newBalance);

        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Cash acknowledged successfully',
          amount: amount,
          newBalance: newBalance,
          transactionId: transactionId
        };
      }
    }

    return { success: false, message: 'Transfer not found or already acknowledged' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Acknowledge cash: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  } finally {
    // ✅ FIX C-1: Lock hamesha release karo
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}
/**
 * Create cash acknowledgement entry
 */
function createCashAcknowledgement(transactionId, supervisorId, operatorId, amount, remarks, branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
    
    // Create sheet if doesn't exist
    if (!ackSheet) {
      ackSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
        'Transaction ID', 'Date', 'Supervisor ID', 'Operator ID', 'Amount', 
        'Remarks', 'Status', 'Acknowledged At', 'Branch Code', 'Timestamp'
      ]]);
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#27ae60')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    // Add pending acknowledgement
    ackSheet.appendRow([
      transactionId,
      new Date(),
      supervisorId,
      operatorId,
      amount,
      remarks || 'Cash transfer',
      'PENDING',
      '',
      branchCode,
      new Date()
    ]);
    
    Logger.log('✅ Cash acknowledgement created: ' + transactionId);
    return true;
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Create acknowledgement: ' + e.toString());
    return false;
  }
}
// ============================================
// 📖 PASSBOOK PRINT SYSTEM
// ============================================

/**
 * Get account transactions for passbook print
 * Returns only unprinted transactions or all transactions based on printType
 */
function getPassbookTransactions(accountNumber, printType) {
  try {
    accountNumber = String(accountNumber || '').trim();
    if (!accountNumber) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account number required' };
    }

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    // ── Account info from ACCOUNT OPEN ──
    var accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSheet || accountSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }

    var accountData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accountInfo = null;

    for (var a = 0; a < accountData.length; a++) {
      if (String(accountData[a][2]).trim() === accountNumber) {
        accountInfo = {
          accountNumber:  String(accountData[a][2]),
          memberName:     String(accountData[a][1] || ''),
          schemeName:     String(accountData[a][4] || ''),
          openingDate:    accountData[a][3] ? formatDate(accountData[a][3]) : '',
          currentBalance: 0
        };
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!accountInfo) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account not found: ' + accountNumber };
    }

    // ── DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT ──
    // A=AccountNo | B=Name | C=Amount | D=Interest | E=CurrentBalance | F=Date | G=MonthFor
    var depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    var transactions = [];
    var latestBalance = 0;

    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var depLastCol = depSheet.getLastColumn(); // actual columns only
      var depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, depLastCol).getValues();

      for (var i = 0; i < depData.length; i++) {
        if (String(depData[i][0]).trim() !== accountNumber) continue;

        var amount   = parseFloat(depData[i][2]) || 0;   // Col C
        var interest = parseFloat(depData[i][3]) || 0;   // Col D
        var balance  = parseFloat(depData[i][4]) || 0;   // Col E
        var monthFor = String(depData[i][6] || '');       // Col G

        // ✅ FIX: Date — Col F — could be Date object OR string
        var rawDate  = depData[i][5] || null;             // Col F
        var dateStr  = '';
        var dateObj  = null;
        if (rawDate) {
          if (rawDate instanceof Date) {
            dateObj = rawDate;
            dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(rawDate, tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
          } else {
            // String date like "2026-02-22" — parse safely
            try {
              dateObj = new Date(String(rawDate));
              if (!isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
                dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
              } else {
                dateStr = String(rawDate); // keep as-is
                dateObj = null;
              }
            } catch(de) {
              dateStr = String(rawDate);
              dateObj = null;
            }
          }
        }

        // Col L (index 11) = Printed flag — may not exist
        var isPrinted = (depLastCol > 11)
                        ? String(depData[i][11] || '').toUpperCase() === 'YES'
                        : false;

        latestBalance = balance;

        if (printType === 'NEW' || (printType === 'SUBSEQUENT' && !isPrinted)) {
          transactions.push({
            rowIndex:  i + 2,
            txnId:     String(depData[i][0]) + '_' + (i + 2),
            date:      dateStr,
            dateObj:   dateObj ? dateObj.getTime() : 0, // ✅ timestamp for sorting
            type:      'DEPOSIT' + (monthFor ? ' (' + monthFor + ')' : ''),
            amount:    amount,
            interest:  interest,
            balance:   balance,
            printed:   isPrinted
          });
        }
      }
    }

    accountInfo.currentBalance = latestBalance;

    // ✅ FIX: Sort by timestamp — not by formatted string
    transactions.sort(function(a, b) {
      return (a.dateObj || 0) - (b.dateObj || 0);
    });

    if (transactions.length === 0) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: printType === 'SUBSEQUENT'
          ? 'No new unprinted transactions. All already printed.'
          : 'No transactions found for account: ' + accountNumber
      };
    }

    Logger.log('✅ getPassbookTransactions: ' + transactions.length + ' txns for ' + accountNumber);

  // ✅ Count already-printed transactions for Sr. No. continuation
    var printedCount = 0;
    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var depLastCol2 = depSheet.getLastColumn();
      if (depLastCol2 > 11) {
        var depData2 = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 12).getValues();
        for (var pc = 0; pc < depData2.length; pc++) {
          if (String(depData2[pc][0]).trim() !== accountNumber) continue;
          if (String(depData2[pc][11] || '').toUpperCase() === 'YES') printedCount++;
        }
      }
    }

    Logger.log('✅ getPassbookTransactions: ' + transactions.length + ' new, ' + printedCount + ' already printed for ' + accountNumber);

    return {
      success:           true,
      accountInfo:       accountInfo,
      transactions:      transactions,
      totalTransactions: transactions.length,
      printedCount:      printedCount
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getPassbookTransactions error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
/**
 * Mark transactions as printed
 */
function markTransactionsAsPrinted(accountNumber, txnIds, printedBy) {
  try {
    accountNumber = String(accountNumber || '').trim();
    if (!accountNumber || !txnIds || txnIds.length === 0) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid parameters' };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    // ✅ FIX: Use 'DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT' sheet
    // Printed flag → Col L (12), PrintDate → Col M (13), PrintedBy → Col N (14)
    const depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');

    if (!depSheet || depSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT sheet not found' };
    }

    const depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues(); // only col A needed
    const printDate = new Date();
    let markedCount = 0;

    for (let i = 0; i < depData.length; i++) {
      const accNum   = String(depData[i][0]).trim();
      const rowTxnId = accNum + '_' + (i + 2);

      if (accNum === accountNumber && txnIds.indexOf(rowTxnId) !== -1) {
        const rowNum = i + 2;
        depSheet.getRange(rowNum, 12).setValue('YES');      // L: Printed
        depSheet.getRange(rowNum, 13).setValue(printDate);  // M: PrintDate
        depSheet.getRange(rowNum, 14).setValue(printedBy);  // N: PrintedBy
        markedCount++;
      }
    }

    logActivity(printedBy, 'PASSBOOK_PRINT',
      'Passbook printed for A/C ' + accountNumber + ' (' + markedCount + ' transactions)');

    Logger.log('✅ markTransactionsAsPrinted: ' + markedCount + ' marked for ' + accountNumber);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: markedCount + ' transactions marked as printed',
      markedCount: markedCount
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Error in markTransactionsAsPrinted: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Search account by account number or member name
 */
function searchAccountForPassbook(searchTerm) {
  try {
    if (!searchTerm) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Search term required' };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    // ✅ FIX: Correct sheet name 'ACCOUNTS' → 'ACCOUNT OPEN'
    const accountSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');

    if (!accountSheet || accountSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };
    }

    // ACCOUNT OPEN columns:
    // A(0)=MemberId | B(1)=Name | C(2)=AccountNo | D(3)=OpenDate |
    // E(4)=AccountType | F(5)=NomineeName | G(6)=Relationship | H(7)=Status |
    // I(8)=Email | J(9)=UserId | K(10)=PhotoUrl | L(11)=DOB | M(12)=BranchCode
    const accountData = accountSheet.getRange(2, 1, accountSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    const results = [];

    searchTerm = String(searchTerm).trim().toUpperCase();

    for (let i = 0; i < accountData.length; i++) {
      const accountNo  = String(accountData[i][2] || '');   // C: Account No
      const memberName = String(accountData[i][1] || '').toUpperCase(); // B: Name
      const status     = String(accountData[i][7] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase(); // H: Status

      const memberId = String(accountData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase(); // A: MemberId
      if (status === 'ACTIVE' &&
          (accountNo.toUpperCase().indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1 ||
           memberName.indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1 ||
           memberId.indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1)) {

        // ✅ Get current balance from DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT (last entry for this account)
        let currentBalance = 0;
        try {
          const balResult = getCurrentBalanceFromDeposit(accountNo);
          currentBalance = balResult.success ? balResult.balance : 0;
        } catch(be) {}

        results.push({
          accountNumber: accountNo,
          memberId:      String(accountData[i][0] || ''),   // A: MemberId
          memberName:    String(accountData[i][1] || ''),   // B: Name
          schemeName:    String(accountData[i][4] || ''),   // E: Account Type (scheme)
          nomineeName:   String(accountData[i][5] || ''),   // F: Nominee Name
          relationship:  String(accountData[i][6] || ''),   // G: Relationship
          openDate:      accountData[i][3] ? formatDate(accountData[i][3]) : '',
          dob:           accountData[i][11] ? formatDate(accountData[i][11]) : '', // L: DOB
          branchCode:    String(accountData[i][12] || ''),  // M: BranchCode
          email:         String(accountData[i][8] || ''),   // I: Email
          balance:       currentBalance
        });
      }

      if (results.length >= 10) break;
    }

    return { success: true, results: results };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Error in searchAccountForPassbook: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ Helper: get latest balance for account from DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT
function getCurrentBalanceFromDeposit(accountNo) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (!depSheet || depSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, balance: 0 };

    const data = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    let latestBalance = 0;
    let found = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === String(accountNo).trim()) {
        latestBalance = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0; // E: Current_Balance
        found = true;
      }
    }
    return { success: true, balance: latestBalance };
  } catch(e) {
    return { success: true, balance: 0 };
  }
}
// ============================================
// CREATE ANNOUNCEMENT (ADMIN)
// ============================================
function createAnnouncementAdmin(data) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([
        ['ID', 'Title', 'Message', 'Date', 'Status', 'Target', 'Branch Code', 'Created By']
      ]);
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#667eea')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    
    // Generate unique ID
    const id = 'ANN_' + new Date().getTime();
    
    // Validate target
    const validTargets = ['ALL', 'ALL_STAFF', 'ALL_OPERATORS', 'ALL_SUPERVISORS', 
                          'BRANCH_SPECIFIC', 'BRANCH_STAFF', 'BRANCH_MEMBERS'];
    const target = validTargets.includes(data.target) ? data.target : 'ALL';
    
    // Add new row
    sheet.appendRow([
      id,
      data.title || 'Untitled',
      data.message || '',
      new Date(),
      'ACTIVE',
      target,
      data.branchCode || '',
      data.createdBy || 'ADMIN'
    ]);
    
    Logger.log('✅ Announcement created: ' + id + ' | Target: ' + target);
    
    return { success: true, announcementId: id };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Create announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// UPDATE ANNOUNCEMENT (ADMIN)
// ============================================
function updateAnnouncementAdmin(announcementId, data) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No announcements found' };
    }
    
    const dataRange = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < dataRange.length; i++) {
      if (String(dataRange[i][0]) === String(announcementId)) {
        const rowNum = i + 2;
        
        // Update fields
        sheet.getRange(rowNum, 2).setValue(data.title || 'Untitled'); // B: Title
        sheet.getRange(rowNum, 3).setValue(data.message || ''); // C: Message
        sheet.getRange(rowNum, 6).setValue(data.target || 'ALL'); // F: Target
        sheet.getRange(rowNum, 7).setValue(data.branchCode || ''); // G: Branch Code
        
        Logger.log('✅ Announcement updated: ' + announcementId);
        
        return { success: true };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Announcement not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Update announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// DELETE ANNOUNCEMENT (ADMIN)
// ============================================
function deleteAnnouncementAdmin(announcementId) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('ANNOUNCEMENTS');
    
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No announcements found' };
    }
    
    const dataRange = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < dataRange.length; i++) {
      if (String(dataRange[i][0]) === String(announcementId)) {
        const rowNum = i + 2;
        sheet.deleteRow(rowNum);
        
        Logger.log('✅ Announcement deleted: ' + announcementId);
        
        return { success: true };
      }
    }
    
    return { success: false, message: 'Announcement not found' };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Delete announcement error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ============================================
// GET ALL BRANCHES
// ============================================
function getAllBranches() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName('USER_DETAILS');
    
    if (!userSheet || userSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, branches: [] };
    }
    
    const data = userSheet.getRange(2, 1, userSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
    const branchesMap = {};
    
    // Collect unique branches
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const branchCode = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
      if (branchCode && !branchesMap[branchCode]) {
        branchesMap[branchCode] = {
          code: branchCode,
          name: branchCode // Can be enhanced with actual branch names
        };
      }
    }
    
    // Convert to array and sort
    const branches = Object.values(branchesMap).sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code));
    
    return { success: true, branches: branches };
    
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Get all branches error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function rejectEntry(entryId, supervisorId, reason, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    // ✅ FIX: Input sanitization
    entryId      = String(entryId      || '').trim();
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    reason       = String(reason       || 'Not specified').trim();

    Logger.log('rejectEntry called → entryId: "' + entryId + '" | supervisor: "' + supervisorId + '"');

    if (!entryId || !supervisorId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Entry ID and Supervisor ID are required' };
    }

    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only supervisors can reject entries' };
    }

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');

    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No pending entries found' };
    }

    // ✅ Read 8 columns (A-H)
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

    // ✅ DUAL-MODE: accept numeric rowIndex OR string entryId (PE...)
    var isNumeric = /^\d+$/.test(entryId);

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var rowEntryId = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      var rowMatch = isNumeric ? ((i + 2) === parseInt(entryId)) : (rowEntryId === entryId);

      if (rowMatch) {
        var status = String(data[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

        if (status !== 'PENDING') {
          return { success: false, message: 'Entry already ' + status + '. Cannot reject again.' };
        }

        var type = String(data[i][1] || '');

        // ✅ FIX: Write to Col F (6) = Status, Col G (7) = Notes (was writing to col 5 = Submitted!)
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('REJECTED');
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue('Rejected by ' + supervisorId + ': ' + reason);

        logActivity(supervisorId, 'REJECT_ENTRY', type + ' rejected — Entry: ' + entryId + ' | Reason: ' + reason);

        Logger.log('✅ Rejected: ' + entryId);

        return {
          success: true,
          message: '❌ Entry rejected.',
          entryId: entryId
        };
      }
    }

    Logger.log('❌ Entry not found for reject: "' + entryId + '"');
    return { success: false, message: 'Entry not found: ' + entryId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('rejectEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================================
// FIX 18: getMemberDetailsByMemberId — was placeholder/empty
// ============================================================
function getMemberDetailsByMemberId(memberId) {
  try {
    memberId = String(memberId || '').trim();
    if (!memberId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member ID required' };
    }

    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No members found' };
    }

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === memberId) {
        return {
          success: true,
          member: {
            memberId:   String(data[i][0]),
            name:       String(data[i][1]),
            contact:    String(data[i][2]),
            userId:     String(data[i][3]),
            email:      String(data[i][4]),
            branchCode: String(data[i][5] || '')
          }
        };
      }
    }

    return { success: false, message: 'Member not found: ' + memberId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getMemberDetailsByMemberId error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================================
// FIX 20: logActivity — safe helper (used throughout)
// ============================================================
function logActivity(userId, action, details) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ACTIVITY_LOG');

    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('ACTIVITY_LOG');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Timestamp', 'User ID', 'Action', 'Details']]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4)
        .setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#2c3e50').setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }

    sh.appendRow([new Date(), userId, action, details || '']);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('logActivity error: ' + e.toString());
  }
}

// ================================================================
// UPDATED: transferCashToOperator — Auto-create acknowledgement
// ================================================================
// ================================================================
// FEATURE 1: Wallet + Counter + Pending (30-sec refresh APIs)
// ================================================================
function getOperatorLiveDashboard(operatorId) {
  try {
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim();
    if (!operatorId) return { success: false, balance: 0, counterOpen: false, pendingCount: 0, cashPendingCount: 0 };

    // Wallet
    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(operatorId);
    const balance = walletInfo.success ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;

    // Counter status
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    let counterOpen = false;
    let counterNo = '';

    if (allocSheet && allocSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const allocData = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

      for (let i = 0; i < allocData.length; i++) {
        // Columns: Date | Branch Code | Supervisor | Operator | Counter No | Status | Allocated At | Closed At
        const rowDate = allocData[i][0] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(allocData[i][0]), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
        const rowOp   = String(allocData[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();  // Column D: Operator
        const rowStatus = String(allocData[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();  // Column F: Status

        if (rowDate === today && rowOp === operatorId.toUpperCase() && rowStatus === 'OPEN') {
          counterOpen = true;
          counterNo = String(allocData[i][4] || '');  // Column E: Counter No
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Pending entries count
    const pendingCount = getOperatorPendingCount(operatorId);

    // Pending cash acknowledgements count
    const cashPending = getPendingCashAcknowledgements(operatorId);
    const cashPendingCount = cashPending.success ? cashPending.count : 0;

    // ── Active day info: branch day date + form state signals ────
    let dayStarted           = false;
    let activeDayDateDisplay = '';
    let counterIsPrevDay     = false;
    const brRes = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    const opBc  = (brRes && brRes.success) ? String(brRes.branchCode || '').trim() : '';
    if (opBc) {
      const di = getLastDayStatus(opBc);
      dayStarted           = !!(di && di.started);
      activeDayDateDisplay = (di && di.dayDateDisplay) ? di.dayDateDisplay : '';
      if (counterOpen && di && di.dayDate) {
        const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        counterIsPrevDay = (di.dayDate !== todayStr);
      }
    }

    // BUG FIX: If branch day is from previous day and counter open, restrict operator menu
    const branchDayInfo = opBc ? getLastDayStatus(opBc) : { started: false };
    const branchPrevDay = !!(branchDayInfo.started && branchDayInfo.isPreviousDay);
    const operatorMustClose = (counterOpen && counterIsPrevDay) || branchPrevDay;

    const operatorAllowedActions = operatorMustClose
      ? ['cash_return', 'counter_close', 'logout']
      : null; // null = all actions allowed

    return {
      success: true,
      balance: balance,
      counterOpen: counterOpen,
      counterNo: counterNo,
      pendingCount: pendingCount,
      cashPendingCount: cashPendingCount,
      dayStarted:           dayStarted,
      activeDayDateDisplay: activeDayDateDisplay,
      counterIsPrevDay:     counterIsPrevDay,
      branchPreviousDay:    branchPrevDay,
      mustCloseFirst:       operatorMustClose,
      openDayDate:          (branchDayInfo.dayDateDisplay || ''),
      allowedActions:       operatorAllowedActions
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getOperatorLiveDashboard error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, balance: 0, counterOpen: false, pendingCount: 0, cashPendingCount: 0 };
  }
}

function getSupervisorLiveDashboard(supervisorId) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!supervisorId) return { success: false };

    // Wallet
    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    const balance = walletInfo.success ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;

    // Branch
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    const branchCode = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';

    // Operator wallets
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    const operators = [];

    if (walletSheet && walletSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const wData = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < wData.length; i++) {
        const role   = String(wData[i][1] || '').toUpperCase();
        const branch = String(wData[i][2] || '');
        if (role === 'OPERATOR' && branch === branchCode) {
          operators.push({
            operatorId: String(wData[i][0]),
            balance: parseFloat(wData[i][3]) || 0
          });
        }
      }
    }

    // Open counters
    const openCounters = branchCode ? getOpenCounters(branchCode) : [];

    // Pending approvals
    let pendingCount = 0;
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    if (pendingSheet && pendingSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const pData = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < pData.length; i++) {
        const status = String(pData[i][4] || pData[i][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        const entryBranch = String(pData[i][7] || '');
        if (status === 'PENDING' && (!branchCode || entryBranch === branchCode || entryBranch === '')) {
          pendingCount++;
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Active day info for supervisor dashboard card ─────────────
    const supDayInfo = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
    const supDayDateDisplay = (supDayInfo && supDayInfo.dayDateDisplay) ? supDayInfo.dayDateDisplay : '';
    const supDayStarted     = !!(supDayInfo && supDayInfo.started);

    // BUG FIX: isPreviousDay check - restricted menu
    const isPreviousDay = !!(supDayInfo && supDayInfo.started && supDayInfo.isPreviousDay);
    const allowedActions = isPreviousDay
      ? ['cash_return', 'reports', 'daily_account_report', 'day_end', 'logout']
      : null; // null = all actions allowed

    return {
      success: true,
      balance: balance,
      branchCode: branchCode,
      operators: operators,
      openCounterCount: openCounters.length,
      openCounters: openCounters,
      pendingCount: pendingCount,
        activeDayDateDisplay: supDayDateDisplay,
  activeDayDate: (supDayInfo && supDayInfo.dayDate) ? supDayInfo.dayDate : '', 
      dayStarted:           supDayStarted,
      isPreviousDay:        isPreviousDay,
      openDayDate:          supDayDateDisplay,
      allowedActions:       allowedActions,
      mustCloseFirst:       isPreviousDay
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSupervisorLiveDashboard error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, balance: 0, operators: [], openCounterCount: 0, pendingCount: 0 };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// FEATURE 2: Operator Self-Close Counter
// ================================================================
function canOperatorSelfClose(operatorId) {
  try {
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim();
    if (!operatorId) return { canClose: false, reason: 'Operator ID missing' };

    // 1. Check wallet
    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(operatorId);
    const balance = walletInfo.success ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : -1;

    if (balance > 0) {
      return {
        canClose: false,
        reason: '₹' + balance.toFixed(2) + ' cash baaki hai. Pehle supervisor ko return karo.',
        balance: balance,
        pendingCount: 0
      };
    }

    // 2. Check pending entries
    const pendingCount = getOperatorPendingCount(operatorId);
    if (pendingCount > 0) {
      return {
        canClose: false,
        reason: pendingCount + ' pending entries hain. Supervisor se approve/reject karwao.',
        balance: balance,
        pendingCount: pendingCount
      };
    }

    // 3. Check if counter is open (today OR previous unclosed day)
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { canClose: false, reason: 'Koi counter allocate nahi hai.' };
    }

    const tz    = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    // ✅ FIX 7: Use open-day date, not just today
    let checkDate = today;
    const branchInfo = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    if (branchInfo && branchInfo.success) {
      const openDay = getLastDayStatus(branchInfo.branchCode);
      if (openDay && openDay.started && openDay.dayDate) {
        checkDate = openDay.dayDate;
      }
    }

    const allocData  = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    let counterFound = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < allocData.length; i++) {
      const rowDate   = allocData[i][0] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(allocData[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
      const rowOp     = String(allocData[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const rowStatus = String(allocData[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

      if ((rowDate === checkDate || rowDate === today) && rowOp === operatorId.toUpperCase() && rowStatus === 'OPEN') {
        counterFound = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!counterFound) {
      return { canClose: false, reason: 'Counter already closed hai ya allocate nahi hai.' };
    }

    return { canClose: true, reason: '', balance: 0, pendingCount: 0 };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('canOperatorSelfClose error: ' + e.toString());
    return { canClose: false, reason: 'System error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSelfCloseCounter(operatorId) {
  try {
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim();
    if (!operatorId) return { success: false, message: 'Operator ID missing' };

    const check = canOperatorSelfClose(operatorId);
    if (!check.canClose) {
      return { success: false, message: '❌ ' + check.reason };
    }

   // ✅ FIX 7: Mark CLOSED — check open-day date, not just today
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');
    const tz    = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    // Get the branch's open day date
    let checkDate = today;
    const brInfo  = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    if (brInfo && brInfo.success) {
      const dayInfo = getLastDayStatus(brInfo.branchCode);
      if (dayInfo && dayInfo.started && dayInfo.dayDate) {
        checkDate = dayInfo.dayDate;
      }
    }

    const allocData = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    let closed = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < allocData.length; i++) {
      const rowDate   = allocData[i][0] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(allocData[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
      const rowOp     = String(allocData[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const rowStatus = String(allocData[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

      if ((rowDate === checkDate || rowDate === today) && rowOp === operatorId.toUpperCase() && rowStatus === 'OPEN') {
        allocSheet.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('CLOSED');
        allocSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date());
        closed = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!closed) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Counter close karte waqt error. Admin se contact karo.' };
    }

    logActivity(operatorId, 'SELF_CLOSE_COUNTER', 'Operator self-closed counter (zero balance, no pending)');
    Logger.log('✅ Operator self-closed: ' + operatorId);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ Counter successfully close ho gaya!\n\nSupervisor ko request nahi bheji gayi.\nAb logout kar sakte ho.'
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSelfCloseCounter error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function getOperatorPendingCount(operatorId) {
  try {
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    if (!pendingSheet || pendingSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return 0;

    const data = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    let count = 0;

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const rowOp     = String(data[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();  // Column C: operatorId
      const statusA   = String(data[i][4] || '').toUpperCase();
      const statusB   = String(data[i][5] || '').toUpperCase();
      const status    = statusA === 'PENDING' ? 'PENDING' : statusB;

      if (rowOp === operatorId && status === 'PENDING') count++;
    }
    return count;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getOperatorPendingCount error: ' + e.toString());
    return 0;
  }
}


// ================================================================
// FEATURE 3: Supervisor Day-End Counter Check
// ================================================================
function getBranchCounterStatus(supervisorId) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors allowed' };
    }

    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found' };
    }
    const branchCode = branchResult.branchCode;

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const allocSheet = ss.getSheetByName('COUNTER_ALLOCATION');

    if (!allocSheet || allocSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, allClosed: true, counters: [], branchCode: branchCode };
    }

    // ✅ FIX: Use the OPEN day's actual date, not hardcoded today.
    // This handles previous-day day-end correctly.
    const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const lastDayInfo = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
    const checkDate = lastDayInfo.started && lastDayInfo.dayDate
      ? lastDayInfo.dayDate   // e.g. '2026-02-28' (previous day if not closed)
      : Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');  // fallback to today

    Logger.log('getBranchCounterStatus: checking date = ' + checkDate + ' (branch: ' + branchCode + ')');

    const allocData = allocSheet.getRange(2, 1, allocSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

    const counters = [];
    let allClosed = true;

    for (let i = 0; i < allocData.length; i++) {
      if (!allocData[i][0]) continue;
      const rowDate    = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(allocData[i][0]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      const rowBranch  = String(allocData[i][1] || '').trim();  // Column B: Branch Code
      const rowOp      = String(allocData[i][3] || '').trim();  // Column D: Operator
      const rowCounter = String(allocData[i][4] || '').trim();  // Column E: Counter No
      const rowStatus  = String(allocData[i][5] || '').trim().toUpperCase();  // Column F: Status

      if (rowDate === checkDate && rowBranch === branchCode) {
        const isOpen = rowStatus === 'OPEN';
        if (isOpen) allClosed = false;

        const walletInfo   = getWalletBalance(rowOp);
        const walletBalance = walletInfo.success ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;
        const pendingCount  = getOperatorPendingCount(rowOp);

        counters.push({
          operatorId:   rowOp,
          counterNo:    rowCounter,
          status:       rowStatus,
          isOpen:       isOpen,
          walletBalance: walletBalance,
          pendingCount:  pendingCount
        });
      }
    }

    return {
      success:     true,
      allClosed:   allClosed,
      counters:    counters,
      branchCode:  branchCode,
      checkDate:   checkDate,  // ✅ returned so UI can display which date was checked
      totalOpen:   counters.filter(c => c.isOpen).length,
      totalClosed: counters.filter(c => !c.isOpen).length
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getBranchCounterStatus error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function endDay(supervisorId, branchCode, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    if (!supervisorId || !branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Missing supervisor ID or branch code' };
    }

    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can end day' };
    }

    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ ' + branchResult.message };
    }

    const supBranch = branchResult.branchCode;
    if (supBranch !== branchCode) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⛔ Branch mismatch!\nTumhara: ' + supBranch + '\nRequest: ' + branchCode
      };
    }

    const dayCheck = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);

    // ✅ FIX: Aaj already complete ho chuka hai
    if (dayCheck.alreadyDoneToday) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '🔒 Aaj ka Day already end ho chuka hai!\n\nDobara Day End nahi ho sakta.'
      };
    }

    if (!dayCheck.started) {
      return { success: false, message: '⚠️ Day start nahi hua, pehle Day Begin karo.' };
    }

    // ── Check counters ──────────────────────────────────────────
    const counterStatus = getBranchCounterStatus(supervisorId);

    if (!counterStatus.allClosed) {
      const openList = counterStatus.counters
        .filter(c => c.isOpen)
        .map(c => {
          let detail = '• ' + c.operatorId + ' (Counter ' + c.counterNo + ')';
          if (c.walletBalance > 0) detail += ' — ₹' + c.walletBalance.toFixed(2) + ' wallet';
          if (c.pendingCount  > 0) detail += ' — ' + c.pendingCount + ' pending';
          return detail;
        })
        .join('\n');

      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⛔ Day end block!\n\n' +
                 counterStatus.totalOpen + ' counter(s) OPEN:\n' + openList +
                 '\n\n✅ Sabhi counters band karo pehle.',
        openCounters: counterStatus.counters.filter(c => c.isOpen)
      };
    }

    // ── Update DAY_OPERATIONS ───────────────────────────────────
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const daySheet = ss.getSheetByName('DAY_OPERATIONS');

    if (!daySheet) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ DAY_OPERATIONS sheet not found' };
    }

    // ✅ FEATURE 1: Use getLastDayStatus — works for today OR previous day
    const lastDayInfo = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);

    if (!lastDayInfo.started) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Koi open day nahi mila' };
    }

    const closingDate    = lastDayInfo.dayDate;
    const closingDisplay = lastDayInfo.dayDateDisplay;
    const openRowIndex   = lastDayInfo.rowIndex;

    // Update the OPEN row → CLOSED
    if (openRowIndex && openRowIndex >= 2) {
      daySheet.getRange(openRowIndex, 7).setValue('CLOSED');
      daySheet.getRange(openRowIndex, 8).setValue(new Date());
      Logger.log('✅ Closed DAY_BEGIN row at index ' + openRowIndex);
    }

    // Append DAY_END record
    daySheet.appendRow([
      new Date(),    // A: Date (actual close time)
      branchCode,    // B: Branch Code
      supervisorId,  // C: Supervisor ID
      'DAY_END',     // D: Operation
      0,             // E: Opening Balance
      0,             // F: Closing Balance
      'CLOSED',      // G: Status
      new Date()     // H: Timestamp
    ]);

    logActivity(supervisorId, 'DAY_END', 'Day ended for branch ' + branchCode);

    logActivity(supervisorId, 'DAY_END', 'Day ended for branch ' + branchCode + ' (original date: ' + closingDisplay + ')');

    // ✅ BALANCE LOG: Save closing balance snapshot
    try { saveClosingBalance(supervisorId, branchCode); } catch(ce) {
      Logger.log('Closing balance log warning: ' + ce.toString());
    }

    return {
      success:   true,
      message:   '✅ Day successfully closed!\nBranch: ' + branchCode + '\nDay Date: ' + closingDisplay,
      branchCode: branchCode,
      date:       closingDate,
      dayStatus: 'CLOSED'
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('endDay error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
function getSupervisorPendingReturns(supervisorId) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!supervisorId) {
      return { success: false, returns: [], count: 0 };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');

    if (!ackSheet || ackSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, returns: [], count: 0 };
    }

    // Read all 10 columns
    const data = ackSheet.getRange(2, 1, ackSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    const returns = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      // ✅ FIXED: Col C(index 2) = SupervisorId (receiver), Col G(index 6) = Status
      const toSup  = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();   // C: SupervisorId
      const status = String(data[i][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); // G: Status

      if (toSup.toUpperCase() === supervisorId.toUpperCase() && status === 'RETURN_PENDING') {
        returns.push({
          transactionId: String(data[i][0] || ''),          // A: TxnId
          date:          data[i][1] ? formatDate(data[i][1]) : '', // B: Date
          toSupervisor:  String(data[i][2] || ''),          // C: SupervisorId
          fromOperator:  String(data[i][3] || ''),          // D: OperatorId
          amount:        parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0,       // E: Amount
          remarks:       String(data[i][5] || ''),          // F: Remarks
          status:        status,                             // G: Status
          branchCode:    String(data[i][8] || ''),          // I: BranchCode
          rowIndex:      i + 2
        });
      }
    }

    return { success: true, returns: returns, count: returns.length };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSupervisorPendingReturns error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, returns: [], count: 0, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// ================================================================
function supervisorAcknowledgeReturn(supervisorId, transactionId) {
  // ✅ FIX C-1: LockService — concurrent return acknowledgements se race condition rokta hai
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }

  try {
    supervisorId  = String(supervisorId  || '').trim();
    transactionId = String(transactionId || '').trim();

    if (!supervisorId || !transactionId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Missing supervisor ID or transaction ID' };
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');

    if (!ackSheet || ackSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No pending returns found' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX C-1: Fresh read INSIDE lock
    const data = ackSheet.getRange(2, 1, ackSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      const txnId  = String(data[i][0] || '').trim();
      const toSup  = String(data[i][2] || '').trim();
      const fromOp = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();
      const amount = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0;
      const status = String(data[i][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase();

      if (txnId === transactionId &&
          toSup.toUpperCase() === supervisorId.toUpperCase() &&
          status === 'RETURN_PENDING') {

        // ✅ FIX C-1: Status update PEHLE — double-ack block karo
        ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue('RETURN_ACKNOWLEDGED');
        ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date());

        // Ab wallet credit karo (lock ke andar — safe)
        const supWallet = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
        if (!supWallet.success) {
          // Rollback
          ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue('RETURN_PENDING');
          ackSheet.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue('');
          return { success: false, message: 'Could not get supervisor wallet' };
        }

        const newSupBalance = (parseFloat(supWallet.balance) || 0) + amount;
        updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newSupBalance);

        // Update WALLET_TRANSACTIONS status
        const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_TRANSACTIONS');
        if (txnSheet && txnSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
          const txnData = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
          for (let j = 0; j < txnData.length; j++) {
            if (String(txnData[j][0]) === transactionId) {
              txnSheet.getRange(j + 2, 5).setValue('CASH_RETURN_ACKNOWLEDGED');
              txnSheet.getRange(j + 2, 7).setValue('Supervisor acknowledged cash return');
              break;
            }
          }
        }

        logActivity(supervisorId, 'CASH_RETURN_ACKNOWLEDGED',
          'Acknowledged ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + ' return from ' + fromOp + ' (TxnID: ' + transactionId + ')');

        Logger.log('✅ Cash return acknowledged: ₹' + amount + ' | New balance: ₹' + newSupBalance);

        return {
          success:       true,
          message:       '✅ Cash return acknowledged!\n\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nNew Balance: ₹' + newSupBalance.toFixed(2),
          amount:        amount,
          newBalance:    newSupBalance,
          transactionId: transactionId,
          fromOperator:  fromOp
        };
      }
    }

    return { success: false, message: 'Return not found or already acknowledged' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('supervisorAcknowledgeReturn error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    // ✅ FIX C-1: Lock hamesha release karo
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ================================================================
// ✅ FEATURE 2: CASH OFFICE SYSTEM
// Cash Office = Master office that handles excess cash for mapped branches
// Sheets:
//   CASH_OFFICE         → office_id | name | address | contact | status
//   CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES → office_id | branch_code | mapped_date | status
//   CASH_OFFICE_TXN     → txn_id | date | office_id | branch_code | direction | amount | remarks | processed_by | status
// ================================================================

// ── Setup Cash Office sheets ──────────────────────────────────
function setupCashOfficeSheets() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    // 1. CASH_OFFICE
    let coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!coSheet) {
      coSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_OFFICE');
      coSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setValues([[
        'Office ID', 'Office Name', 'Address', 'Contact', 'Status', 'Created Date'
      ]]);
      coSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a237e').setFontColor('white');
      Logger.log('✅ CASH_OFFICE sheet created');
    }

    // 2. CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES
    let cobSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!cobSheet) {
      cobSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
      cobSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setValues([[
        'Office ID', 'Branch Code', 'Branch Name', 'Mapped Date', 'Status'
      ]]);
      cobSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a237e').setFontColor('white');
      Logger.log('✅ CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES sheet created');
    }

    // 3. CASH_OFFICE_TXN
    let cotSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!cotSheet) {
      cotSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
      cotSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
        'Txn ID', 'Date', 'Office ID', 'Branch Code', 'Direction',
        'Amount', 'Remarks', 'Processed By', 'Status', 'Timestamp'
      ]]);
      cotSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a237e').setFontColor('white');
      Logger.log('✅ CASH_OFFICE_TXN sheet created');
    }

    return { success: true, message: 'Cash Office sheets ready' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Create / Get Cash Office ──────────────────────────────────
function createCashOffice(officeId, officeName, address, contact, adminId) {
  try {
    officeId   = String(officeId   || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    officeName = String(officeName || '').trim();
    if (!officeId || !officeName) return { success: false, message: 'Office ID and Name required' };

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss     = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet  = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    const data   = sheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues() : [];

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === officeId) {
        return { success: false, message: 'Office ID already exists: ' + officeId };
      }
    }

    sheet.appendRow([officeId, officeName, address || '', contact || '', 'ACTIVE', new Date()]);
    logActivity(adminId, 'CASH_OFFICE_CREATE', 'Created office: ' + officeId + ' - ' + officeName);
    return { success: true, message: 'Cash Office created: ' + officeName, officeId: officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ✅ FIX P4: Cash Office management functions
function updateCashOfficeStatus(officeId, newStatus, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only admin can update cash office' };
    officeId  = String(officeId  || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    newStatus = String(newStatus || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!['ACTIVE', 'INACTIVE'].includes(newStatus)) return { success: false, message: 'Invalid status' };

    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, message: 'CASH_OFFICE sheet not found' };

    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === officeId) {
        sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue(newStatus); // Col F = Status
        logActivity(adminId, 'UPDATE_CASH_OFFICE', 'Office ' + officeId + ' → ' + newStatus);
        return { success: true, message: 'Cash office status updated to ' + newStatus };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Cash office not found: ' + officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function editCashOffice(officeId, updatedData, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only admin can edit cash office' };
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, message: 'CASH_OFFICE sheet not found' };

    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === officeId) {
        const row = i + 2;
        if (updatedData.officeName) sh.getRange(row, 2).setValue(updatedData.officeName);
        if (updatedData.address)    sh.getRange(row, 3).setValue(updatedData.address);
        if (updatedData.contact)    sh.getRange(row, 4).setValue(updatedData.contact);
        if (updatedData.email)      sh.getRange(row, 5).setValue(updatedData.email);
        logActivity(adminId, 'EDIT_CASH_OFFICE', 'Office edited: ' + officeId);
        return { success: true, message: 'Cash office updated successfully' };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Cash office not found: ' + officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function deleteCashOffice(officeId, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only admin can delete cash office' };
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, message: 'CASH_OFFICE sheet not found' };

    const data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === officeId) {
        const hasTreasurer = String(data[i][6] || '').trim(); // Col G = treasurerId
        if (hasTreasurer) {
          return { success: false, message: '⚠️ Cannot delete office with assigned treasurer. Remove treasurer first.' };
        }
        sh.deleteRow(i + 2);
        logActivity(adminId, 'DELETE_CASH_OFFICE', 'Office deleted: ' + officeId);
        return { success: true, message: 'Cash office deleted successfully' };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Cash office not found: ' + officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ── Map Branch to Cash Office ─────────────────────────────────
function mapBranchToCashOffice(officeId, branchCode, adminId) {
  try {
    officeId   = String(officeId   || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    adminId    = String(adminId    || '').trim();
    // BUG FIX: Admin role check - sirf admin map kar sakta hai, supervisor nahi
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only Admin can map branches to Cash Office' };
    if (!officeId || !branchCode) return { success: false, message: 'Office ID and Branch Code required' };

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet   = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    const data    = sheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues() : [];

    // Check duplicate active mapping
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === officeId &&
          String(data[i][1]).trim() === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][4]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        return { success: false, message: 'Branch ' + branchCode + ' already mapped to ' + officeId };
      }
    }

    // Get branch name
    const branchSheet = ss.getSheetByName('BRANCHES');
    let branchName = branchCode;
    if (branchSheet && branchSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const bd = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, branchSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < bd.length; i++) {
        if (String(bd[i][0]).trim() === branchCode) { branchName = String(bd[i][1] || branchCode); break; }
      }
    }

    sheet.appendRow([officeId, branchCode, branchName, new Date(), 'ACTIVE']);
    logActivity(adminId, 'CASH_OFFICE_MAP', 'Mapped branch ' + branchCode + ' to office ' + officeId);
    return { success: true, message: 'Branch ' + branchCode + ' mapped to office ' + officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Unmap Branch from Cash Office ───────────────────────────
function unmapBranchFromCashOffice(officeId, branchCode, adminId) {
  try {
    officeId   = String(officeId   || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    adminId    = String(adminId    || '').trim();

    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only Admin can remove branch mapping' };
    if (!officeId || !branchCode) return { success: false, message: 'Office ID and Branch Code required' };

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'No branch mappings found' };
    }

    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    let found = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === officeId &&
          String(data[i][1]).trim() === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][4]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        // Status col E (col index 5) ko INACTIVE kar do
        sheet.getRange(i + 2, 5).setValue('INACTIVE');
        found = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!found) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Active mapping not found for branch ' + branchCode + ' in office ' + officeId };
    }

    logActivity(adminId, 'CASH_OFFICE_UNMAP', 'Removed branch ' + branchCode + ' from office ' + officeId);
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Branch ' + branchCode + ' removed from office ' + officeId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('unmapBranchFromCashOffice error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Get All Branch Mappings for an Office (active + inactive) ────────
function getCashOfficeBranchesAll(officeId, adminId) {
  try {
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    adminId  = String(adminId  || '').trim();

    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only Admin can view all branch mappings' };
    if (!officeId) return { success: false, message: 'Office ID required' };

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, branches: [], officeId: officeId };
    }

    const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    const branches = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() !== officeId) continue;
      const brCode = String(data[i][1] || '').trim();
      if (!brCode) continue;
      branches.push({
        branchCode: brCode,
        branchName: String(data[i][2] || brCode),
        mappedDate: data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : '',
        status:     String(data[i][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase(),
        rowIndex:   i + 2
      });
    }

    return { success: true, branches: branches, officeId: officeId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getCashOfficeBranchesAll error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Cash Transfer: Branch → Office (excess cash send) ────────
function branchSendCashToOffice(officeId, branchCode, amount, remarks, processedBy) {
  try {
    officeId   = String(officeId   || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    amount     = parseFloat(amount) || 0;
    if (!officeId || !branchCode || amount <= 0) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Office ID, Branch Code, and valid Amount required' };
    }

    // Verify mapping
    const mapCheck = isBranchMappedToOffice(officeId, branchCode);
    if (!mapCheck) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch ' + branchCode + ' is not mapped to office ' + officeId };
    }

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    const txnId = 'COT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);

    sheet.appendRow([
      txnId,
      new Date(),
      officeId,
      branchCode,
      'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE',   // Branch ne Office ko bheja (excess deposit)
      amount,
      remarks || '',
      processedBy,
      'COMPLETED',
      new Date()
    ]);

    logActivity(processedBy, 'CASH_OFFICE_TXN',
      'Branch ' + branchCode + ' sent ₹' + amount + ' to office ' + officeId);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ ₹' + amount.toLocaleString('en-IN') + ' sent to Cash Office ' + officeId,
      txnId: txnId
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Cash Transfer: Office → Branch (send cash to branch) ─────
function officeSendCashToBranch(officeId, branchCode, amount, remarks, processedBy) {
  try {
    officeId   = String(officeId   || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode = String(branchCode || '').trim();
    amount     = parseFloat(amount) || 0;
    if (!officeId || !branchCode || amount <= 0) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Office ID, Branch Code, and valid Amount required' };
    }

    const mapCheck = isBranchMappedToOffice(officeId, branchCode);
    if (!mapCheck) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch ' + branchCode + ' is not mapped to office ' + officeId };
    }

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    const txnId = 'COT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);

    sheet.appendRow([
      txnId,
      new Date(),
      officeId,
      branchCode,
      'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH',   // Office ne Branch ko bheja (cash supply)
      amount,
      remarks || '',
      processedBy,
      'COMPLETED',
      new Date()
    ]);

    logActivity(processedBy, 'CASH_OFFICE_TXN',
      'Office ' + officeId + ' sent ₹' + amount + ' to branch ' + branchCode);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ ₹' + amount.toLocaleString('en-IN') + ' sent to Branch ' + branchCode,
      txnId: txnId
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Helper: Check branch-office mapping ──────────────────────
function isBranchMappedToOffice(officeId, branchCode) {
  try {
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return false;
    const data  = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === officeId &&
          String(data[i][1]).trim() === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][4]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') return true;
    }
    return false;
  } catch (e) { return false; }
}

// ── Get Mapped Branches for an Office ────────────────────────
function getCashOfficeBranches(officeId) {
  try {
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss     = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet  = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, branches: [] };
    const data   = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    const branches = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase() === officeId &&
          String(data[i][4]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        branches.push({
          branchCode: String(data[i][1]),
          branchName: String(data[i][2]),
          mappedDate: data[i][3] ? formatDate(data[i][3]) : ''
        });
      }
    }
    return { success: true, branches: branches, officeId: officeId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Daily Report for Cash Office ─────────────────────────────
function getCashOfficeReport(officeId, reportDate) {
  try {
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    setupCashOfficeSheets();

    const ss  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const tz  = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    // Parse date — format: 'yyyy-MM-dd' or Date object
    let targetDate;
    if (!reportDate) {
      targetDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    } else if (typeof reportDate === 'string' && reportDate.length === 10) {
      targetDate = reportDate;
    } else {
      targetDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(reportDate), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    }

    const targetDisplay = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(targetDate), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');

    // Get all mapped branches for this office
    const branchResult = getCashOfficeBranches(officeId);
    const mappedBranches = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branches : [];

    // Get transactions for this date
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    const branchTotals = {};

    // Initialize all mapped branches
    mappedBranches.forEach(function(b) {
      branchTotals[b.branchCode] = {
        branchCode:    b.branchCode,
        branchName:    b.branchName,
        sentToOffice:  0,   // Branch → Office (excess cash received by office)
        receivedFromOffice: 0, // Office → Branch (cash sent to branch)
        netFlow:       0,
        txnCount:      0,
        transactions:  []
      };
    });

    let totalReceived = 0; // Office received from all branches
    let totalSent     = 0; // Office sent to all branches

    if (txnSheet && txnSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const txnData = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < txnData.length; i++) {
        const txnDate   = txnData[i][1] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(txnData[i][1]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
        const tOfficeId = String(txnData[i][2] || '').toUpperCase();
        const branch    = String(txnData[i][3] || '').trim();
        const direction = String(txnData[i][4] || '').trim();
        const amount    = parseFloat(txnData[i][5]) || 0;
        const status    = String(txnData[i][8] || '').toUpperCase();

        if (txnDate !== targetDate || tOfficeId !== officeId || status !== 'COMPLETED') continue;

        if (!branchTotals[branch]) {
          branchTotals[branch] = {
            branchCode: branch, branchName: branch,
            sentToOffice: 0, receivedFromOffice: 0, netFlow: 0, txnCount: 0, transactions: []
          };
        }

        branchTotals[branch].transactions.push({
          txnId:     String(txnData[i][0]),
          direction: direction,
          amount:    amount,
          remarks:   String(txnData[i][6] || ''),
          by:        String(txnData[i][7] || '')
        });
        branchTotals[branch].txnCount++;

        if (direction === 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE') {
          branchTotals[branch].sentToOffice += amount;
          totalReceived += amount;
        } else if (direction === 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH') {
          branchTotals[branch].receivedFromOffice += amount;
          totalSent += amount;
        }
        branchTotals[branch].netFlow = branchTotals[branch].sentToOffice - branchTotals[branch].receivedFromOffice;
      }
    }

    const branchReport = Object.values(branchTotals);

    return {
      success:        true,
      officeId:       officeId,
      reportDate:     targetDate,
      reportDateDisplay: targetDisplay,
      totalBranches:  mappedBranches.length,
      totalReceived:  totalReceived,  // Total cash office received from branches
      totalSent:      totalSent,       // Total cash office sent to branches
      netPosition:    totalReceived - totalSent,
      branches:       branchReport
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getCashOfficeReport error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
function getAllCashOffices() {
  try {
    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, offices: [] };
    // ✅ FIX: Read 7 columns to include col G = treasurerId
    const data  = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
    const offices = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][4] || '').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        offices.push({
          officeId:    String(data[i][0] || ''),
          officeName:  String(data[i][1] || ''),
          address:     String(data[i][2] || ''),
          contact:     String(data[i][3] || ''),
          createdDate: data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : '',
          treasurerId: String(data[i][6] || '')   // ✅ col G
        });
      }
    }
    return { success: true, offices: offices };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ── Assign / Change Treasurer for a Cash Office ──────────────
function assignTreasurerToOffice(officeId, treasurerId, adminId) {
  try {
    officeId    = String(officeId    || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    adminId     = String(adminId     || '').trim();

    if (!officeId || !treasurerId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Office ID and Treasurer ID required' };
    }

    // ✅ Verify admin
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };

    const credData = credSheet.getLastRow() > 1
      ? credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues()
      : [];

    // Validate treasurer exists and has TREASURER role
    let treasurerFound = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
      if (String(credData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
          String(credData[i][2] || '').toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER' &&
          String(credData[i][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
        treasurerFound = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    if (!treasurerFound) {
      return { success: false, message: '❌ Treasurer ID not found or not active: ' + treasurerId };
    }

    // ✅ Find the office row and update col G (treasurerId)
    const officeSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!officeSheet || officeSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Cash Office not found' };
    }

    const offData = officeSheet.getRange(2, 1, officeSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
    let rowFound = -1;
    let oldTreasurer = '';

    for (let i = 0; i < offData.length; i++) {
      if (String(offData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === officeId) {
        rowFound = i + 2; // 1-based sheet row
        oldTreasurer = String(offData[i][6] || '').trim();
        break;
      }
    }

    if (rowFound === -1) {
      return { success: false, message: '❌ Office not found: ' + officeId };
    }

    // ✅ Update col G with new treasurerId
    officeSheet.getRange(rowFound, 7).setValue(treasurerId);

    // ✅ Also initialize treasurer wallet if not already done
    try {
      initializeWallet(treasurerId, 'TREASURER', officeId, 0);
    } catch (we) {
      Logger.log('Wallet init warning for treasurer: ' + we.toString());
    }

    logActivity(adminId, 'ASSIGN_TREASURER',
      'Office: ' + officeId + ' | New: ' + treasurerId +
      (oldTreasurer ? ' | Old: ' + oldTreasurer : ''));

    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ Treasurer ' + treasurerId + ' assigned to ' + officeId + ' successfully!' +
               (oldTreasurer && oldTreasurer !== treasurerId
                 ? '\n\n(Previous treasurer: ' + oldTreasurer + ' replaced)'
                 : '')
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('assignTreasurerToOffice error: ' + e.toString());
