    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ── Get Cash Offices mapped to Supervisor's branch ────────────
function getMappedCashOfficesForSupervisor(supervisorId) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!supervisorId) return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID required' };
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors allowed' };

    // Get supervisor's branch
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch not found for supervisor' };
    }
    const branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // Step 1: Find all officeIds where this branchCode is ACTIVE
    const cobSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
    if (!cobSheet || cobSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, offices: [], branchCode: branchCode };
    }

    const cobData = cobSheet.getRange(2, 1, cobSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    const mappedOfficeIds = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < cobData.length; i++) {
      const oId    = String(cobData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const bCode  = String(cobData[i][1] || '').trim();
      const status = String(cobData[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (bCode === branchCode && status === 'ACTIVE' && oId) {
        if (!mappedOfficeIds.includes(oId)) mappedOfficeIds.push(oId);
      }
    }

    if (mappedOfficeIds.length === 0) {
      return { success: true, offices: [], branchCode: branchCode,
               message: 'Aapki branch (' + branchCode + ') kisi Cash Office se mapped nahi hai.' };
    }

    // Step 2: Get full office details from CASH_OFFICE sheet
    const coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (!coSheet || coSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, offices: [], branchCode: branchCode };
    }

    const coData  = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
    const offices = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < coData.length; i++) {
      const officeId = String(coData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      const status   = String(coData[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;
      if (!mappedOfficeIds.includes(officeId)) continue;
      offices.push({
        officeId:    officeId,
        officeName:  String(coData[i][1] || ''),
        address:     String(coData[i][2] || ''),
        contact:     String(coData[i][3] || ''),
        treasurerId: String(coData[i][6] || '')
      });
    }

    return { success: true, offices: offices, branchCode: branchCode };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getMappedCashOfficesForSupervisor error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ── Get Cash Office Transaction History ──────────────────────
function getCashOfficeTxnHistory(officeId, branchCode, days) {
  try {
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    days     = parseInt(days) || 30;
    setupCashOfficeSheets();

    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet   = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, transactions: [] };

    const tz      = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    const cutoff  = new Date();
    cutoff.setDate(cutoff.getDate() - days);
    const cutoffStr = Utilities.formatDate(cutoff, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    const data   = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    const txns   = [];

    for (let i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      const txnDate   = data[i][1] ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][1]), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : '';
      const tOfficeId = String(data[i][2] || '').toUpperCase();
      const branch    = String(data[i][3] || '').trim();

      if (txnDate < cutoffStr) continue;
      if (tOfficeId !== officeId) continue;
      if (branchCode && branch !== branchCode) continue;

      txns.push({
        txnId:     String(data[i][0]),
        date:      txnDate ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(data[i][1]), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy') : '',
        officeId:  tOfficeId,
        branch:    branch,
        direction: String(data[i][4]),
        amount:    parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0,
        remarks:   String(data[i][6] || ''),
        by:        String(data[i][7] || ''),
        status:    String(data[i][8] || '')
      });
      if (txns.length >= 200) break;
    }

    return { success: true, transactions: txns };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
function transferCashToOperator(supervisorId, operatorId, amount, remarks, token) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    if (!amount || amount === '' || amount === null || amount === undefined) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Please enter an amount' };
    }
    amount = parseFloat(amount);
    if (isNaN(amount) || amount <= 0) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid amount. Please enter a positive number' };
    }

    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can transfer cash' };
    }

    const supBranchObj = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    const opBranchObj  = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);

    if (!supBranchObj || !supBranchObj.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not find supervisor branch information' };
    }
    if (!opBranchObj || !opBranchObj.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not find operator branch information' };
    }

    const supBranch = String(supBranchObj.branchCode || '').trim();
    const opBranch  = String(opBranchObj.branchCode  || '').trim();

    if (!supBranch) return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor branch code is missing' };
    if (!opBranch)  return { success: false, message: 'Operator branch code is missing' };

    if (supBranch !== opBranch) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⛔ Cannot transfer to different branch!\n\nYour Branch: ' + supBranch + '\nOperator Branch: ' + opBranch
      };
    }

    initializeWallet(supervisorId, 'SUPERVISOR', supBranch, 0);
    initializeWallet(operatorId,   'OPERATOR',   opBranch,  0);

    const supWallet = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    if (!supWallet || !supWallet.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not retrieve supervisor wallet' };
    }

    const supBalance = parseFloat(supWallet.balance) || 0;
    if (supBalance < amount) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ Insufficient wallet balance!\n\nRequired: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) +
                 '\nAvailable: ₹' + supBalance.toFixed(2) +
                 '\nShortfall: ₹' + (amount - supBalance).toFixed(2)
      };
    }

    // ✅ FIX #9: Deduct from supervisor NOW
    const newSupBalance = supBalance - amount;
    updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newSupBalance);

    // ✅ FIX #9: Create PENDING acknowledgement — operator wallet NOT credited yet
    const transId = 'WT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    createCashAcknowledgement(transId, supervisorId, operatorId, amount, remarks || 'Cash allocation', supBranch);

    recordWalletTransaction(transId, supervisorId, operatorId, amount, 'CASH_TRANSFER_PENDING', remarks || 'Cash allocation', supBranch);
    logActivity(supervisorId, 'WALLET_TRANSFER', 'Transfer PENDING ₹' + amount + ' to ' + operatorId + ' | TxnID: ' + transId);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ Cash transfer initiated!\n\nTransaction ID: ' + transId +
               '\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) +
               '\nYour New Balance: ₹' + newSupBalance.toFixed(2) +
               '\n\n⚠️ Operator must acknowledge to receive cash.',
      transactionId:     transId,
      supervisorBalance: newSupBalance,
      amount:            amount
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ Transfer cash error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'System error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}


// ================================================================
function returnCashToSupervisor(operatorId, amount, remarks) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try {
    lock.waitLock(15000);
  } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }
  try {
    amount = parseFloat(amount);
    if (!amount || amount <= 0) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid amount' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX #10: Returns object {success, branchCode, ...} — not a string
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Operator branch not found' };
    }
    const opBranch = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    // ✅ FIX #10: Use findSupervisorForBranch (correct helper)
    const supervisorId = findSupervisorForBranch(opBranch);
    if (!supervisorId) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor not found for branch: ' + opBranch + '. Contact admin.' };
    }

    const opWallet = getWalletBalance(operatorId);
    const opBalance = parseFloat(opWallet && opWallet.success ? opWallet.balance : 0) || 0;

    if (opBalance < amount) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ Insufficient wallet!\n\nRequired: ₹' + amount + '\nAvailable: ₹' + opBalance
      };
    }

    // Deduct from operator
    const newOpBal = opBalance - amount;
    updateWalletBalance(operatorId, newOpBal);

    // Create RETURN_PENDING ack — supervisor ke paas acknowledgement aayegi
    const transId = 'WT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let ackSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
    if (!ackSheet) {
      ackSheet = ss.insertSheet('CASH_ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS');
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
        'Transaction ID', 'Date', 'Supervisor ID', 'Operator ID', 'Amount',
        'Remarks', 'Status', 'Acknowledged At', 'Branch Code', 'Timestamp'
      ]]);
      ackSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#27ae60').setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }
    // RETURN_PENDING: Col A=TxnId, B=Date, C=SupervisorId, D=OperatorId, E=Amount, F=Remarks, G=Status, H=AckAt, I=Branch, J=Timestamp
    ackSheet.appendRow([
      transId, new Date(), supervisorId, operatorId, amount,
      remarks || 'Day close return', 'RETURN_PENDING', '', opBranch, new Date()
    ]);

    recordWalletTransaction(transId, operatorId, supervisorId, amount, 'CASH_RETURN_PENDING', remarks || 'Day close return', opBranch);
    logActivity(operatorId, 'WALLET_RETURN', 'Return PENDING ₹' + amount + ' to ' + supervisorId);

    return {
      success:         true,
      message:         '✅ Cash return initiated!\n\nTxn ID: ' + transId + '\nSupervisor will acknowledge to confirm.',
      transactionId:   transId,
      operatorBalance: newOpBal,
      amount:          amount
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Return cash error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}


// ================================================================
// ================================================================
function operatorReturnCash(operatorId, amount) {
  try {
    return returnCashToSupervisor(operatorId, parseFloat(amount), 'Cash return to supervisor');
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// ✅ FIX: Admin can now create TREASURER role
// ================================================================
function createUser(userData, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access Denied: Only admin can create users' };
    }

    if (!userData.userId || !userData.name || !userData.role) {
      return { success: false, message: 'User ID, Name, and Role are required' };
    }

    const role   = userData.role.toUpperCase();
    const userId = userData.userId.trim().toUpperCase();

    // ✅ FIX #5: TREASURER allowed (no branch needed)
    if (!['SUPERVISOR', 'OPERATOR', 'TREASURER'].includes(role)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Role must be SUPERVISOR, OPERATOR, or TREASURER' };
    }

    if (role !== 'TREASURER' && !userData.branchCode) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch Code is required for ' + role };
    }

  const existingUser = checkUserIdExists(userId);
    if (existingUser.exists) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ User ID already exists!\n\nUser: ' + existingUser.name + '\nRole: ' + existingUser.role
      };
    }

    // ✅ FIX P5: One supervisor per branch, one treasurer per cash office
    if (role === 'SUPERVISOR' && userData.branchCode) {
      const credSheet2 = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
      if (credSheet2 && credSheet2.getLastRow() > 1) {
        const credData = credSheet2.getRange(2, 1, credSheet2.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
        for (let ci = 0; ci < credData.length; ci++) {
          const cRole   = String(credData[ci][2] || '').toUpperCase();
          const cBranch = String(credData[ci][3] || '').trim();
          const cStatus = String(credData[ci][4] || '').toUpperCase();
          if (cRole === 'SUPERVISOR' && cBranch === userData.branchCode && cStatus === 'ACTIVE') {
            return {
              success: false,
              message: '⛔ Branch ' + userData.branchCode + ' mein already ek SUPERVISOR hai (' + String(credData[ci][0]) + ').\n\nPehle purane supervisor ko inactive karo.'
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (role === 'TREASURER' && userData.officeId) {
      const offSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
      if (offSheet && offSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        const offData = offSheet.getRange(2, 1, offSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
        for (let oi = 0; oi < offData.length; oi++) {
          const oId  = String(offData[oi][0] || '').toUpperCase();
          const oTrs = String(offData[oi][6] || '').trim(); // Col G = existing treasurer
          if (oId === userData.officeId.toUpperCase() && oTrs) {
            return {
              success: false,
              message: '⛔ Office ' + userData.officeId + ' mein already ek TREASURER hai (' + oTrs + ').\n\nPehle purane treasurer ko remove karo.'
            };
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (role !== 'TREASURER') {
      const branchCheck = validateBranchExists(userData.branchCode);
      if (!branchCheck.exists) {
        return { success: false, message: 'Branch code not found: ' + userData.branchCode };
      }
    }

    const defaultPassword = DEFAULT_USER_PASSWORD; // ✅ FIX 14: central constant
    const hashedPassword  = hashPassword(defaultPassword, userId); // ✅ FIX: salted

    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet) return { success: false, message: 'CREDENTIALS sheet not found' };

    credSheet.appendRow([userId, hashedPassword, role, userData.branchCode || '', 'ACTIVE']);

    const lastRow = credSheet.getLastRow();
    credSheet.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 5).setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
    credSheet.getRange(lastRow, 5).setBackground('#d4edda').setFontColor('#155724').setFontWeight('bold');

    const userDetailsSheet = getOrCreateUserDetailsSheet();
    userDetailsSheet.appendRow([
      userId, userData.name.trim(), role, userData.branchCode || '',
      userData.contact || '', userData.email || '', new Date(), 'ACTIVE', adminId
    ]);

    if (role === 'SUPERVISOR') {
      updateBranchSupervisor(userData.branchCode, userId);
    }

    // ✅ FIX #5: If TREASURER + officeId given, link in CASH_OFFICE sheet col G
    if (role === 'TREASURER' && userData.officeId) {
      try {
        const officeSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
        if (officeSheet && officeSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
          const offData = officeSheet.getRange(2, 1, officeSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
          for (let i = 0; i < offData.length; i++) {
            if (String(offData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === userData.officeId.toUpperCase()) {
              officeSheet.getRange(i + 2, 7).setValue(userId);
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (oe) {
        Logger.log('Treasurer-office link warning: ' + oe.toString());
      }
    }

    logActivity(adminId, 'CREATE_USER', 'User: ' + userId + ' (' + role + ')' + (userData.branchCode ? ' Branch: ' + userData.branchCode : ''));

    return {
      success:         true,
      message:         '✅ User created successfully!\n\nDefault Password: ' + defaultPassword,
      userId:          userId,
      defaultPassword: defaultPassword,
      role:            role,
      branchCode:      userData.branchCode || 'N/A',
      branchName:      userData.branchCode || 'N/A'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Create user error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ================================================================
// NEW FUNCTIONS — ADD AT BOTTOM OF gs.txt
// ================================================================

// ✅ FIX #1: Supervisor → Cash Office transfer (supervisor initiates)
function supervisorSendCashToOffice(supervisorId, officeId, amount, remarks, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(supervisorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };
    amount   = parseFloat(amount) || 0;
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();

    // BUG FIX: Amount string se float properly parse karo
    if (typeof amount === 'string') amount = parseFloat(amount.replace(/,/g, '')) || 0;

    // BUG FIX: officeId blank ho toh auto-lookup karo branch mapping se
    if (!officeId && supervisorId) {
      try {
        var brRes = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
        var bc = brRes && brRes.success ? String(brRes.branchCode || '').trim() : '';
        if (bc) {
          var cobSh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_BRANCHES');
          if (cobSh && cobSh.getLastRow() > 1) {
            var cobD = cobSh.getRange(2, 1, cobSh.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
            for (var ci = 0; ci < cobD.length; ci++) {
              if (String(cobD[ci][1] || '').trim() === bc &&
                  String(cobD[ci][4] || '').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
                officeId = String(cobD[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
                break;
              }
            }
          }
        }
      } catch(oe) { Logger.log('officeId auto-lookup error: ' + oe.toString()); }
    }

    if (!supervisorId) return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID required' };
    if (!officeId)     return { success: false, message: 'Office ID not found. Please contact Admin.' };
    if (amount <= 0)   return { success: false, message: 'Valid amount required (must be greater than 0)' };
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can send cash to office' };
    }

    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not determine supervisor branch' };
    }
    const branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    if (!isBranchMappedToOffice(officeId, branchCode)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Your branch (' + branchCode + ') is not mapped to office ' + officeId };
    }

    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    if (!walletInfo || !walletInfo.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not retrieve supervisor wallet' };
    }
    const supBalance = parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0;
    if (supBalance < amount) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ Insufficient wallet!\nRequired: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nAvailable: ₹' + supBalance.toFixed(2)
      };
    }

    const newSupBal = supBalance - amount;
    updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newSupBal);

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    const txnId   = 'COT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);

    txnSheet.appendRow([
      txnId, new Date(), officeId, branchCode,
      'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE', amount, remarks || '',
      supervisorId, 'PENDING_ACK', new Date()
    ]);

    logActivity(supervisorId, 'CASH_TO_OFFICE', 'Sent ₹' + amount + ' to office ' + officeId + ' (PENDING ACK)');

    return {
      success:           true,
      message:           '✅ Cash sent!\n\nTxn ID: ' + txnId + '\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nNew Balance: ₹' + newSupBal.toFixed(2) + '\n\n⚠️ Cash Office will acknowledge.',
      txnId:             txnId,
      supervisorBalance: newSupBal,
      amount:            amount
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('supervisorSendCashToOffice error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #1: Cash Office acknowledges receipt from branch
function officeAcknowledgeCashFromBranch(treasurerId, txnId) {
  try {
    txnId       = String(txnId       || '').trim();
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!txnId || !treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Txn ID and Treasurer ID required' };

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss       = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!txnSheet || txnSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No transactions found' };

    const data = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === txnId &&
          String(data[i][8]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'PENDING_ACK' &&
          String(data[i][4]).trim() === 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE') {

        const amount   = parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0;
        const branchCd = String(data[i][3] || '');

        // ✅ FIX: Credit treasurer wallet when cash received from branch
        let newWalletBalance = 0;
        try {
          initializeWallet(treasurerId, 'TREASURER', '', 0); // ensure wallet exists
          const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
          const oldBal     = (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;
          newWalletBalance = oldBal + amount;
          updateWalletBalance(treasurerId, newWalletBalance);
          Logger.log('✅ Treasurer wallet credited: ' + treasurerId + ' +₹' + amount + ' → ₹' + newWalletBalance);
        } catch (we) {
          Logger.log('Treasurer wallet credit warning: ' + we.toString());
        }

        txnSheet.getRange(i + 2, 9).setValue('COMPLETED');
        txnSheet.getRange(i + 2, 10).setValue(new Date());
logActivity(treasurerId, 'CASH_OFFICE_ACK', 'Acknowledged ₹' + amount + ' from branch ' + branchCd);

        // BUG FIX: Duplicate FIX P2 block removed - double credit bug fixed
        // Treasurer wallet already credited above (newWalletBalance variable)

        return {
          success: true,
          message: '\xe2\x9c\x85 Cash acknowledged!\nAmount: \xe2\x82\xb9' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nBranch: ' + branchCd + ' | New Balance: \xe2\x82\xb9' + newWalletBalance.toFixed(2),
          txnId: txnId, amount: amount, newWalletBalance: newWalletBalance
        };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Transaction not found or already acknowledged' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('officeAcknowledgeCashFromBranch error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #1: Office → Branch (treasurer dispatches, supervisor acknowledges)
function officeSendCashToBranchPending(treasurerId, officeId, branchCode, amount, remarks) {
  try {
    amount      = parseFloat(amount) || 0;
    officeId    = String(officeId    || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    branchCode  = String(branchCode  || '').trim();
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    // BUG FIX: Agar officeId blank hai toh CASH_OFFICE sheet se auto-lookup karo
    if (!officeId && treasurerId) {
      try {
        var coSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
        if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
          var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
          for (var ci = 0; ci < coData.length; ci++) {
            if (String(coData[ci][6] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
                String(coData[ci][4] || 'ACTIVE').trim().toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
              officeId = String(coData[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (oe) { Logger.log('officeId auto-lookup error: ' + oe.toString()); }
    }

    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };
    if (!officeId)    return { success: false, message: 'Office ID not found. Please contact Admin.' };
    if (!branchCode)  return { success: false, message: 'Branch Code required' };
    if (amount <= 0)  return { success: false, message: 'Valid Amount required' };

    if (!isBranchMappedToOffice(officeId, branchCode)) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch ' + branchCode + ' is not mapped to office ' + officeId };
    }

    // ✅ FIX: Check treasurer wallet balance before sending
    initializeWallet(treasurerId, 'TREASURER', '', 0); // ensure exists
    const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
    const oldBal     = (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;

    if (oldBal < amount) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '❌ Treasurer wallet mein insufficient balance!\nRequired: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nAvailable: ₹' + oldBal.toFixed(2)
      };
    }

    // ✅ Debit treasurer wallet immediately on dispatch
    const newWalletBalance = oldBal - amount;
    updateWalletBalance(treasurerId, newWalletBalance);

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss       = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    const txnId    = 'COT' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);

    txnSheet.appendRow([
      txnId, new Date(), officeId, branchCode,
      'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH', amount, remarks || '',
      treasurerId, 'PENDING_ACK', new Date()
    ]);

    logActivity(treasurerId, 'CASH_FROM_OFFICE',
      'Dispatched ₹' + amount + ' to branch ' + branchCode +
      ' | Wallet: ₹' + oldBal + ' → ₹' + newWalletBalance);

    return {
      success:          true,
      message:          '✅ Cash dispatched!\n\nTxn ID: ' + txnId + '\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) +
                        '\nBranch: ' + branchCode + '\n💰 Wallet: ₹' + newWalletBalance.toFixed(2) +
                        '\n\n⚠️ Supervisor must acknowledge.',
      txnId:            txnId,
      amount:           amount,
      newWalletBalance: newWalletBalance
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('officeSendCashToBranchPending error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #1: Supervisor acknowledges cash received from Cash Office
function supervisorAcknowledgeCashFromOffice(supervisorId, txnId) {
  try {
    txnId       = String(txnId       || '').trim();
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!txnId || !supervisorId) return { success: false, message: 'Txn ID and Supervisor ID required' };
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can acknowledge' };

    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) return { success: false, message: 'Could not get supervisor branch' };
    const branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!txnSheet || txnSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No transactions found' };

    const data = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === txnId &&
          String(data[i][3]).trim() === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][8]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'PENDING_ACK' &&
          String(data[i][4]).trim() === 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH') {
        const amount = parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0;

        // ✅ Credit supervisor wallet only after acknowledge
        const walletInfo = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
        const oldBal  = walletInfo.success ? (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) : 0;
        const newBal  = oldBal + amount;
        updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newBal);

        txnSheet.getRange(i + 2, 9).setValue('COMPLETED');
        txnSheet.getRange(i + 2, 10).setValue(new Date());

        logActivity(supervisorId, 'CASH_FROM_OFFICE_ACK', 'Acknowledged ₹' + amount + ' from Cash Office');

        return {
          success: true,
          message: '✅ Cash acknowledged!\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nNew Balance: ₹' + newBal.toFixed(2),
          txnId: txnId, amount: amount, newBalance: newBal
        };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, message: 'Transaction not found or already processed' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('supervisorAcknowledgeCashFromOffice error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #1: Get pending BRANCH_TO_OFFICE transactions for treasurer
function getPendingBranchToOfficeTxns(officeId) {
  try {
    officeId = String(officeId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!officeId) return { success: false, transactions: [] };
    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!txnSheet || txnSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, transactions: [], count: 0 };

    const data = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    const txns = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][2]).trim().toUpperCase() === officeId &&
          String(data[i][8]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'PENDING_ACK' &&
          String(data[i][4]).trim() === 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE') {
        txns.push({
          txnId:     String(data[i][0]),
          date:      data[i][1] ? formatDate(data[i][1]) : '',
          officeId:  String(data[i][2] || ''),
          branchCode: String(data[i][3] || ''),
          amount:    parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0,
          remarks:   String(data[i][6] || ''),
          by:        String(data[i][7] || ''),
          rowIndex:  i + 2
        });
      }
    }
    return { success: true, transactions: txns, count: txns.length };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, transactions: [], count: 0, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #1: Get pending OFFICE_TO_BRANCH for supervisor's branch
function getPendingOfficeTobranchTxns(supervisorId) {
  try {
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) return { success: false, transactions: [] };
    const branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) return { success: false, transactions: [] };
    const branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    setupCashOfficeSheets();
    const ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (!txnSheet || txnSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, transactions: [], count: 0 };

    const data = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    const txns = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][3]).trim() === branchCode &&
          String(data[i][8]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'PENDING_ACK' &&
          String(data[i][4]).trim() === 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH') {
        txns.push({
          txnId:     String(data[i][0]),
          date:      data[i][1] ? formatDate(data[i][1]) : '',
          officeId:  String(data[i][2] || ''),
          branchCode: branchCode,
          amount:    parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0,
          remarks:   String(data[i][6] || ''),
          by:        String(data[i][7] || ''),
          rowIndex:  i + 2
        });
      }
    }
    return { success: true, transactions: txns, count: txns.length };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, transactions: [], count: 0, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ✅ FIX #6: Treasurer — All branches report
function getTreasurerAllBranchesReport(treasurerId) {
  try {
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (!credSheet) return { success: false, message: 'System error' };
    const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    let ok = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
      if (String(credData[i][0]).toUpperCase() === treasurerId.toUpperCase() &&
          String(credData[i][2]).toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER' &&
          String(credData[i][4]).toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') { ok = true; break; }
    }
    if (!ok) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Treasurer access only' };

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const branchSheet = ss.getSheetByName('BRANCH_MASTER') || ss.getSheetByName('BRANCHES');
    const branches = [];
    if (branchSheet && branchSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const bd = branchSheet.getRange(2, 1, branchSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 4).getValues();
      bd.forEach(function(r) { if (String(r[0]||'').trim()) branches.push({branchCode:String(r[0]),branchName:String(r[1]||r[0])}); });
    }

    const depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    const branchDeposits = {};
    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const dd = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow()-1, 11).getValues();
      dd.forEach(function(r) { const bc=String(r[10]||'').trim(); if(bc) branchDeposits[bc]=(branchDeposits[bc]||0)+(parseFloat(r[2])||0); });
    }
    const loanSheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    const branchLoans = {};
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const ld = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow()-1, 15).getValues();
      ld.forEach(function(r) { const bc=String(r[14]||'').trim(); if(bc) branchLoans[bc]=(branchLoans[bc]||0)+(parseFloat(r[5])||0); });
    }
    const walletSheet = ss.getSheetByName('WALLET_MASTER');
    const branchWallet = {};
    if (walletSheet && walletSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const wd = walletSheet.getRange(2, 1, walletSheet.getLastRow()-1, 5).getValues();
      wd.forEach(function(r) { if(String(r[2]||'').toUpperCase()==='SUPERVISOR'&&String(r[3]||'').trim()) branchWallet[String(r[3]).trim()]=(branchWallet[String(r[3]).trim()]||0)+(parseFloat(r[1])||0); });
    }

    const report = branches.map(function(b) {
      return {
        branchCode:       b.branchCode,
        branchName:       b.branchName,
        totalDeposits:    branchDeposits[b.branchCode]  || 0,
        totalLoans:       branchLoans[b.branchCode]     || 0,
        supervisorWallet: branchWallet[b.branchCode]    || 0
      };
    });
    return { success: true, report: report };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerAllBranchesReport error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// DAILY BALANCE LOG SYSTEM
// Sheet: DAILY_BALANCE_LOG
// Columns: A=Date(yyyy-MM-dd) | B=BranchCode | C=SupervisorId
//          D=OpeningBalance | E=ClosingBalance | F=DayStatus
//          G=OpenTimestamp | H=CloseTimestamp
// ================================================================

function _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss) {
  var sh = ss.getSheetByName('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
  if (!sh) {
    sh = ss.insertSheet('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8).setValues([[
      'Date', 'Branch Code', 'Supervisor ID',
      'Opening Balance', 'Closing Balance',
      'Day Status', 'Open Timestamp', 'Close Timestamp'
    ]]);
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 8)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#1a237e')
      .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    sh.setColumnWidth(1, 110);
    sh.setColumnWidth(2, 110);
    sh.setColumnWidth(4, 130);
    sh.setColumnWidth(5, 130);
  }
  return sh;
}

function saveOpeningBalance(supervisorId, branchCode) {
  try {
    var ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz      = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var sh      = _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss);
    var now     = new Date();
    var dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    // BUG FIX: Opening balance = previous day's closing balance (not current wallet)
    // Search DAILY_BALANCE_LOG for most recent CLOSED entry for this branch
    var openBal = 0;
    var foundPrevClose = false;
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var allRows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

      // Check if today already saved
      var tzSave = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
      for (var i = 0; i < allRows.length; i++) {
        var savedDate = allRows[i][0] instanceof Date
          ? Utilities.formatDate(allRows[i][0], tzSave, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
          : String(allRows[i][0] || '').trim();
        if (savedDate === dateStr &&
            String(allRows[i][1] || '').trim() === branchCode &&
            String(allRows[i][5] || '').toUpperCase() === 'OPEN') {
          Logger.log('Balance log already exists for today: ' + branchCode + ' ' + dateStr);
          return { success: true, message: 'Already exists', openingBalance: parseFloat(allRows[i][3]) || 0 };
        }
      }

      // Find most recent CLOSED entry for this branch (previous day closing)
      for (var j = allRows.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
        var prevDate = allRows[j][0] instanceof Date
          ? Utilities.formatDate(allRows[j][0], tzSave, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
          : String(allRows[j][0] || '').trim();
        if (String(allRows[j][1] || '').trim() === branchCode &&
            String(allRows[j][5] || '').toUpperCase() === 'CLOSED' &&
            prevDate !== dateStr) {
          openBal = parseFloat(allRows[j][4]) || 0; // Col E = closing balance
          foundPrevClose = true;
          Logger.log('Previous day closing found: ' + allRows[j][0] + ' Rs.' + openBal);
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Fallback: use current wallet balance if no previous record
    if (!foundPrevClose) {
  openBal = 0; // ✅ Fresh start — no previous history
  Logger.log('No previous closing found for branch ' + branchCode + ' — starting from 0');
}

    sh.appendRow([
      dateStr, branchCode, supervisorId,
      openBal, 0, 'OPEN', now, ''
    ]);

    Logger.log('Opening balance saved: Branch=' + branchCode + ' Date=' + dateStr + ' Bal=Rs.' + openBal);
    return { success: true, openingBalance: openBal };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveOpeningBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function saveClosingBalance(supervisorId, branchCode) {
  try {
    var ss      = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz      = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var sh      = _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss);
    var now     = new Date();
    var today   = Utilities.formatDate(now, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    var lastDayInfo   = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);
    var targetDateStr = lastDayInfo.dayDate
      ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(lastDayInfo.dayDate), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
      : today;

    var walletRes = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    var closeBal  = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;

    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      var tzClose = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
      for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
        var rDate   = rows[i][0] instanceof Date
          ? Utilities.formatDate(rows[i][0], tzClose, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
          : String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
        var rBranch = String(rows[i][1] || '').trim();
        var rStatus = String(rows[i][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        if ((rDate === targetDateStr || rDate === today) && rBranch === branchCode && rStatus === 'OPEN') {
          var rowNum = i + 2;
          sh.getRange(rowNum, 5).setValue(closeBal);
          sh.getRange(rowNum, 6).setValue('CLOSED');
          sh.getRange(rowNum, 8).setValue(now);
          Logger.log('Closing balance saved: Branch=' + branchCode + ' Date=' + rDate + ' Bal=Rs.' + closeBal);
          return { success: true, closingBalance: closeBal };
        }
      }
    }

    sh.appendRow([
      targetDateStr, branchCode, supervisorId,
      0, closeBal, 'CLOSED', '', now
    ]);
    Logger.log('Closing balance appended (no open record): ' + branchCode + ' Rs.' + closeBal);
    return { success: true, closingBalance: closeBal };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveClosingBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// gs.txt mein getSavedDayBalance function replace karo:
function getSavedDayBalance(branchCode, dateStr) {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { found: false, openingBalance: 0, closingBalance: 0, status: 'NOT_FOUND' };
    }
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    
    // STEP 1: Pehle exact date match dhundh (original logic)
    var best = null;
    var tz2 = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      // ✅ FIX: Handle both Date objects and strings from Sheets
      var rowDate = rows[i][0] instanceof Date
        ? Utilities.formatDate(rows[i][0], tz2, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
        : String(rows[i][0] || '').trim();
      if (rowDate === dateStr &&
          String(rows[i][1] || '').trim() === branchCode) {
        best = {
          found:          true,
          openingBalance: parseFloat(rows[i][3]) || 0,
          closingBalance: parseFloat(rows[i][4]) || 0,
          status:         String(rows[i][5] || '').toUpperCase()
        };
      }
    }
    if (best) return best;

    // ✅ FIX P3: Exact date nahi mili — last working day ka CB = aaj ka OB
    // Reverse mein scan karo: is date se pehle ka last CLOSED entry dhundh
    var lastClosing = 0;
    var lastClosingDate = '';
    for (var j = rows.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
      var rDate   = rows[j][0] instanceof Date
        ? Utilities.formatDate(rows[j][0], tz2, 'yyyy-MM-dd')
        : String(rows[j][0] || '').trim();
      var rBranch = String(rows[j][1] || '').trim();
      var rStatus = String(rows[j][5] || '').toUpperCase();
      // Sirf is branch ki, is date se PEHLE ki CLOSED entries lo
      if (rBranch === branchCode && rStatus === 'CLOSED' && rDate < dateStr) {
        lastClosing     = parseFloat(rows[j][4]) || 0; // Col E = closing balance
        lastClosingDate = rDate;
        Logger.log('getSavedDayBalance: Previous closing found for ' + dateStr + 
                   ' → using ' + lastClosingDate + ' CB = Rs.' + lastClosing);
        break;
      }
    }

    // lastClosing = 0 bhi ho sakta hai agar genuinely 0 tha — yeh correct hai
    // lekin agar koi record hi nahi mila, foundPrevClose = false
    return {
      found:          false,
      openingBalance: lastClosing,  // ✅ Last working day ka CB
      closingBalance: 0,
      status:         'NOT_FOUND',
      prevClosingDate: lastClosingDate
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSavedDayBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { found: false, openingBalance: 0, closingBalance: 0, status: 'ERROR' };
  }
}

// ================================================================
// FRESH DAILY REPORT — TOTAL + SCHEME-WISE + OPERATOR-WISE
// ================================================================
function getBranchDailyReport(supervisorId, reportDate) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!supervisorId) return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID required' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Branch not found for supervisor' };
    }
    var branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    // ── Parse date ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    var targetDate;
    if (reportDate && String(reportDate).trim()) {
      var parts = String(reportDate).trim().split('/');
      if (parts.length === 3) {
        targetDate = new Date(parseInt(parts[2]), parseInt(parts[1]) - 1, parseInt(parts[0]));
      } else {
        targetDate = new Date();
      }
    } else {
      targetDate = new Date();
    }
    targetDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var targetDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var targetDisplay = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');

    // ── Opening & Closing Balance from DAILY_BALANCE_LOG ────────
    var savedBal         = getSavedDayBalance(branchCode, targetDateStr);
    var openingBalance   = savedBal.openingBalance;
    var closingBalSaved  = savedBal.closingBalance;
    var dayStatus        = savedBal.status; // OPEN / CLOSED / NOT_FOUND

    var isToday   = (targetDateStr === Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
    var walletRes = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    var currentWallet = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;

    // ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    function matchDate(dateVal) {
      if (!dateVal) return false;
      try { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(dateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd') === targetDateStr; } catch(e) { return false; }
    }
    function fmtDateDisplay(dateVal) {
      if (!dateVal) return '';
      try { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(dateVal), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy'); } catch(e) { return ''; }
    }

    // ── Build account → scheme map ───────────────────────────────
    var acctSchemeMap = {};
    var acctSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (acctSheet && acctSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var acctData = acctSheet.getRange(2, 1, acctSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
      for (var ai = 0; ai < acctData.length; ai++) {
        var an = String(acctData[ai][2] || '').trim();
        var at = String(acctData[ai][4] || 'General').trim();
        if (an) acctSchemeMap[an] = at || 'General';
      }
    }

    // ── Load PENDING_ENTRIES once (for operator mapping) ─────────
    var pendData = [];
    var pendSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');
    if (pendSheet && pendSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      pendData = pendSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    }

    // Helper: find operator from approved pending entry
    function findOperator(entryType, matchFn) {
      for (var pi = 0; pi < pendData.length; pi++) {
        if (String(pendData[pi][5] || '').toUpperCase() !== 'APPROVED') continue;
        if (String(pendData[pi][1] || '').toUpperCase() !== entryType) continue;
        try {
          var pj = JSON.parse(String(pendData[pi][2] || '{}'));
          if (matchFn(pj)) return String(pendData[pi][3] || '').trim();
        } catch(pe) {}
      }
      return 'UNKNOWN';
    }

    // ================================================================
    // DEPOSITS
    // ================================================================
    var depositByScheme   = {};
    var depositByOperator = {};
    var totalDeposit      = 0;
    var depositDetails    = [];

    var depSheet = ss.getSheetByName('DEPOSIT MANAGEMENT');
    if (depSheet && depSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var depData = depSheet.getRange(2, 1, depSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 11).getValues();
      for (var di = 0; di < depData.length; di++) {
        if (String(depData[di][10] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
        if (!matchDate(depData[di][5])) continue;
        var dAcct   = String(depData[di][0] || '').trim();
        var dName   = String(depData[di][1] || '');
        var dAmt    = parseFloat(depData[di][2]) || 0;
        var dInt    = parseFloat(depData[di][3]) || 0;
        var dMonFor = String(depData[di][6] || '');
        var dUserId = String(depData[di][8] || '');
        var dTotal  = dAmt + dInt;
        var scheme  = acctSchemeMap[dAcct] || 'General';
        var opId    = findOperator('DEPOSIT', function(pj){ return String(pj.accountNo||'').trim() === dAcct; });
        if (opId === 'UNKNOWN' && dUserId) opId = dUserId;

        totalDeposit += dTotal;

        if (!depositByScheme[scheme])   depositByScheme[scheme]   = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };
        if (!depositByOperator[opId])   depositByOperator[opId]   = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };

        depositByScheme[scheme].total   += dTotal;
        depositByScheme[scheme].count++;
        depositByScheme[scheme].details.push({ accountNo:dAcct, name:dName, amount:dAmt, interest:dInt, monthFor:dMonFor });

        depositByOperator[opId].total   += dTotal;
        depositByOperator[opId].count++;
        depositByOperator[opId].details.push({ accountNo:dAcct, name:dName, amount:dAmt, interest:dInt, scheme:scheme });

        depositDetails.push({ accountNo:dAcct, name:dName, amount:dAmt, interest:dInt, scheme:scheme, monthFor:dMonFor, operator:opId });
      }
    }

    // ================================================================
    // LOAN REPAYMENTS
    // ================================================================
    var loanTypeMap     = {};
    var loanSheet       = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN MANAGEMENT');
    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var lmData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      for (var lmi = 0; lmi < lmData.length; lmi++) {
        var lacno = String(lmData[lmi][1] || '').trim();
        var ltype = String(lmData[lmi][3] || 'General').trim();
        if (lacno) loanTypeMap[lacno] = ltype || 'General';
      }
    }

    var repayByScheme   = {};
    var repayByOperator = {};
    var totalRepayment  = 0;
    var repayDetails    = [];

    var repaySheet = ss.getSheetByName('LOAN REPAY & DEFULT FEE COLLECTION');
    if (repaySheet && repaySheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var repayData = repaySheet.getRange(2, 1, repaySheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var ri = 0; ri < repayData.length; ri++) {
        if (String(repayData[ri][5] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
        if (!matchDate(repayData[ri][6])) continue;
        var rLoan  = String(repayData[ri][0] || '').trim();
        var rPaid  = parseFloat(repayData[ri][1]) || 0;
        var rMon   = String(repayData[ri][2] || '');
        var rInt   = parseFloat(repayData[ri][3]) || 0;
        var rFee   = parseFloat(repayData[ri][4]) || 0;
        var rTotal = rPaid + rInt + rFee;
        var lScheme = loanTypeMap[rLoan] || 'General';
        var rOpId   = findOperator('LOAN_REPAYMENT', function(pj){ return String(pj.loanAcNo||'').trim() === rLoan; });

        totalRepayment += rTotal;

        if (!repayByScheme[lScheme])   repayByScheme[lScheme]   = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };
        if (!repayByOperator[rOpId])   repayByOperator[rOpId]   = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };

        repayByScheme[lScheme].total   += rTotal;
        repayByScheme[lScheme].count++;
        repayByScheme[lScheme].details.push({ loanAcNo:rLoan, paid:rPaid, interest:rInt, fee:rFee, monthFor:rMon });

        repayByOperator[rOpId].total   += rTotal;
        repayByOperator[rOpId].count++;
        repayByOperator[rOpId].details.push({ loanAcNo:rLoan, paid:rPaid, interest:rInt, fee:rFee, scheme:lScheme });

        repayDetails.push({ loanAcNo:rLoan, paid:rPaid, interest:rInt, fee:rFee, scheme:lScheme, monthFor:rMon, operator:rOpId });
      }
    }

    // ================================================================
    // CASH FROM OFFICE + OTHER RECEIPTS
    // ================================================================
    var totalCashFromOffice = 0;
    var officeInDetails     = [];
    var coData              = [];
    var coTxnSheet          = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    if (coTxnSheet && coTxnSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      coData = coTxnSheet.getRange(2, 1, coTxnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < coData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(coData[ci][3] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
        if (!matchDate(coData[ci][1])) continue;
        if (String(coData[ci][4] || '').toUpperCase() !== 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH') continue;
        var coAmt = parseFloat(coData[ci][5]) || 0;
        totalCashFromOffice += coAmt;
        officeInDetails.push({ txnId:String(coData[ci][0]||''), amount:coAmt, remarks:String(coData[ci][6]||''), status:String(coData[ci][8]||'') });
      }
    }

    var totalOtherReceipt   = 0;
    var otherReceiptDetails = [];
    var otherData           = [];
    var otherSheet          = ss.getSheetByName('OTHER_ENTRIES');
    if (otherSheet && otherSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      otherData = otherSheet.getRange(2, 1, otherSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var oti = 0; oti < otherData.length; oti++) {
        if (String(otherData[oti][5] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
        if (String(otherData[oti][0] || '').toUpperCase() !== 'RECEIPT') continue;
        if (!matchDate(otherData[oti][4])) continue;
        var otAmt = parseFloat(otherData[oti][2]) || 0;
        totalOtherReceipt += otAmt;
        otherReceiptDetails.push({ head:String(otherData[oti][1]||''), amount:otAmt, remarks:String(otherData[oti][3]||'') });
      }
    }

    var totalReceipts = totalDeposit + totalRepayment + totalCashFromOffice + totalOtherReceipt;

    // ================================================================
    // LOAN DISBURSEMENTS
    // ================================================================
    var disburseByScheme   = {};
    var disburseByOperator = {};
    var totalLoanDisburse  = 0;
    var loanDisburseDetails= [];

    if (loanSheet && loanSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var loanData = loanSheet.getRange(2, 1, loanSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 15).getValues();
      for (var li = 0; li < loanData.length; li++) {
        if (!matchDate(loanData[li][6])) continue;
        var lBranch = String(loanData[li][14] || '').trim();
        if (lBranch && lBranch !== branchCode) continue;
        var lAcNo  = String(loanData[li][1] || '').trim();
        var lName  = String(loanData[li][2] || '');
        var lType  = String(loanData[li][3] || 'General').trim() || 'General';
        var lAmt   = parseFloat(loanData[li][5]) || 0;
        var lOpId  = findOperator('LOAN', function(pj){ return String(pj.loanAcNo||'').trim() === lAcNo; });

        totalLoanDisburse += lAmt;

        if (!disburseByScheme[lType])   disburseByScheme[lType]   = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };
        if (!disburseByOperator[lOpId]) disburseByOperator[lOpId] = { total:0, count:0, details:[] };

        disburseByScheme[lType].total   += lAmt;
        disburseByScheme[lType].count++;
        disburseByScheme[lType].details.push({ loanAcNo:lAcNo, name:lName, amount:lAmt });

        disburseByOperator[lOpId].total += lAmt;
        disburseByOperator[lOpId].count++;
        disburseByOperator[lOpId].details.push({ loanAcNo:lAcNo, name:lName, amount:lAmt, scheme:lType });

        loanDisburseDetails.push({ loanAcNo:lAcNo, name:lName, amount:lAmt, scheme:lType, operator:lOpId });
      }
    }

    // ================================================================
    // ACCOUNT CLOSE SETTLEMENTS
    // ================================================================
    var totalSettlement  = 0;
    var settlementDetails= [];
    var settleByOperator = {};
    var closeSheet       = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT CLOSE');
    if (closeSheet && closeSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var closeData = closeSheet.getRange(2, 1, closeSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (var cli = 0; cli < closeData.length; cli++) {
        if (String(closeData[cli][4] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
        if (!matchDate(closeData[cli][3])) continue;
        var clAmt  = parseFloat(closeData[cli][2]) || 0;
        var clAcct = String(closeData[cli][0] || '').trim();
        var clName = String(closeData[cli][1] || '');
        var clOpId = findOperator('ACCOUNT_CLOSE', function(pj){ return String(pj.accountNo||'').trim() === clAcct; });
        totalSettlement += clAmt;
        settlementDetails.push({ accountNo:clAcct, name:clName, amount:clAmt, operator:clOpId });
        if (!settleByOperator[clOpId]) settleByOperator[clOpId] = { total:0, count:0 };
        settleByOperator[clOpId].total += clAmt;
        settleByOperator[clOpId].count++;
      }
    }

    // ================================================================
    // CASH TO OFFICE + OTHER PAYMENTS
    // ================================================================
    var totalCashToOffice  = 0;
    var officeOutDetails   = [];
    for (var co2i = 0; co2i < coData.length; co2i++) {
      if (String(coData[co2i][3] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
      if (!matchDate(coData[co2i][1])) continue;
      if (String(coData[co2i][4] || '').toUpperCase() !== 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE') continue;
      var co2Amt = parseFloat(coData[co2i][5]) || 0;
      totalCashToOffice += co2Amt;
      officeOutDetails.push({ txnId:String(coData[co2i][0]||''), amount:co2Amt, remarks:String(coData[co2i][6]||''), status:String(coData[co2i][8]||'') });
    }

    var totalOtherPayment   = 0;
    var otherPaymentDetails = [];
    for (var ot2i = 0; ot2i < otherData.length; ot2i++) {
      if (String(otherData[ot2i][5] || '').trim() !== branchCode) continue;
      if (String(otherData[ot2i][0] || '').toUpperCase() !== 'PAYMENT') continue;
      if (!matchDate(otherData[ot2i][4])) continue;
      var ot2Amt = parseFloat(otherData[ot2i][2]) || 0;
      totalOtherPayment += ot2Amt;
      otherPaymentDetails.push({ head:String(otherData[ot2i][1]||''), amount:ot2Amt, remarks:String(otherData[ot2i][3]||'') });
    }

    var totalPayments    = totalLoanDisburse + totalSettlement + totalCashToOffice + totalOtherPayment;
    var computedClosing  = openingBalance + totalReceipts - totalPayments;

    // ── Final closing balance ────────────────────────────────────
    var finalClosing;
    var balanceSource;
    if (dayStatus === 'CLOSED' && savedBal.found) {
      finalClosing   = closingBalSaved;
      balanceSource  = 'SAVED';
    } else if (isToday) {
      finalClosing   = computedClosing;
      balanceSource  = (dayStatus === 'OPEN') ? 'LIVE' : 'COMPUTED';
    } else {
      finalClosing   = computedClosing;
      balanceSource  = 'COMPUTED';
    }

    // ================================================================
    // OPERATOR SUMMARY
    // ================================================================
    var allOpIds = {};
    function _addOp(id) { if (id) allOpIds[id] = true; }
    Object.keys(depositByOperator).forEach(_addOp);
    Object.keys(repayByOperator).forEach(_addOp);
    Object.keys(disburseByOperator).forEach(_addOp);
    Object.keys(settleByOperator).forEach(_addOp);

    var operatorSummary = [];
    Object.keys(allOpIds).forEach(function(opId) {
      var depT = depositByOperator[opId]  ? depositByOperator[opId].total  : 0;
      var repT = repayByOperator[opId]    ? repayByOperator[opId].total    : 0;
      var disT = disburseByOperator[opId] ? disburseByOperator[opId].total : 0;
      var setT = settleByOperator[opId]   ? settleByOperator[opId].total   : 0;
      operatorSummary.push({
        operatorId:  opId,
        deposits:    depT,  depCount:  depositByOperator[opId]  ? depositByOperator[opId].count  : 0,
        repayments:  repT,  repCount:  repayByOperator[opId]    ? repayByOperator[opId].count    : 0,
        disburse:    disT,  disCount:  disburseByOperator[opId] ? disburseByOperator[opId].count : 0,
        settlements: setT,  setCount:  settleByOperator[opId]   ? settleByOperator[opId].count   : 0,
        totalIn:     depT + repT,
        totalOut:    disT + setT,
        net:         (depT + repT) - (disT + setT)
      });
    });
    operatorSummary.sort(function(a,b){ return b.totalIn - a.totalIn; });

    // ================================================================
    // SCHEME SUMMARY
    // ================================================================
    var allSchemes = {};
    function _addSch(id) { if (id) allSchemes[id] = true; }
    Object.keys(depositByScheme).forEach(_addSch);
    Object.keys(repayByScheme).forEach(_addSch);
    Object.keys(disburseByScheme).forEach(_addSch);

    var schemeSummary = [];
    Object.keys(allSchemes).forEach(function(sch) {
      var depT = depositByScheme[sch]  ? depositByScheme[sch].total  : 0;
      var repT = repayByScheme[sch]    ? repayByScheme[sch].total    : 0;
      var disT = disburseByScheme[sch] ? disburseByScheme[sch].total : 0;
      schemeSummary.push({
        scheme:     sch,
        deposits:   depT, depCount: depositByScheme[sch]  ? depositByScheme[sch].count  : 0,
        repayments: repT, repCount: repayByScheme[sch]    ? repayByScheme[sch].count    : 0,
        disburse:   disT, disCount: disburseByScheme[sch] ? disburseByScheme[sch].count : 0,
        totalIn:    depT + repT,
        totalOut:   disT
      });
    });
    schemeSummary.sort(function(a,b){ return b.totalIn - a.totalIn; });

    return {
      success:        true,
      branchCode:     branchCode,
      reportDate:     targetDisplay,
      targetDateStr:  targetDateStr,
      dayStatus:      dayStatus,
      balanceSource:  balanceSource,
      openingBalance: openingBalance,
      closingBalance: finalClosing,
      computedClosing:computedClosing,
      walletBalance:  currentWallet,
      balanceMatch:   (dayStatus === 'CLOSED') ? (Math.abs(finalClosing - computedClosing) < 1) : (Math.abs(finalClosing - currentWallet) < 1),
      difference:     (dayStatus === 'CLOSED') ? Math.abs(finalClosing - computedClosing) : Math.abs(finalClosing - currentWallet),
      receipts: {
        deposits:       { total: totalDeposit,       details: depositDetails },
        repayments:     { total: totalRepayment,      details: repayDetails },
        cashFromOffice: { total: totalCashFromOffice, details: officeInDetails },
        other:          { total: totalOtherReceipt,   details: otherReceiptDetails },
        grandTotal:     totalReceipts
      },
      payments: {
        loanDisburse:  { total: totalLoanDisburse,  details: loanDisburseDetails },
        settlements:   { total: totalSettlement,    details: settlementDetails },
        cashToOffice:  { total: totalCashToOffice,  details: officeOutDetails },
        other:         { total: totalOtherPayment,  details: otherPaymentDetails },
        grandTotal:    totalPayments
      },
      schemeSummary:    schemeSummary,
      depositByScheme:  depositByScheme,
      repayByScheme:    repayByScheme,
      disburseByScheme: disburseByScheme,
      operatorSummary:    operatorSummary,
      depositByOperator:  depositByOperator,
      repayByOperator:    repayByOperator,
      disburseByOperator: disburseByOperator
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getBranchDailyReport error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// OTHER ENTRIES — Supervisor can add misc receipts / payments
// Sheet: OTHER_ENTRIES
// Columns: A=type(RECEIPT/PAYMENT) | B=head | C=amount | D=remarks
//          E=date | F=branchCode | G=supervisorId
// ================================================================
function saveOtherEntry(supervisorId, entryData) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim();
    if (!supervisorId) return { success: false, message: 'Supervisor ID required' };
    if (!isSupervisor(supervisorId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only supervisors can add entries' };

    var type    = String(entryData.type   || '').toUpperCase().trim(); // RECEIPT or PAYMENT
    var head    = String(entryData.head   || '').trim();
    var amount  = parseFloat(entryData.amount) || 0;
    var remarks = String(entryData.remarks || '').trim();
    var date    = entryData.date ? new Date(entryData.date) : new Date();
    // ✅ FIX: Sirf day begin date allow karo
var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
var dayInfo   = getLastDayStatus(branchCode);  // branchCode neeche fetch hota hai — move this up
var entryDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(date, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
if (dayInfo && dayInfo.started && dayInfo.dayDate) {
  if (entryDateStr !== dayInfo.dayDate) {
    return { 
      success: false, 
      message: '❌ Sirf Day Begin date (' + dayInfo.dayDateDisplay + ') ki entry allowed hai.\nBack date entry nahi ho sakti.' 
    };
  }
}

    if (!type || (type !== 'RECEIPT' && type !== 'PAYMENT')) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Type must be RECEIPT or PAYMENT' };
    }
    if (!head) return { success: false, message: 'Head/category is required' };
    if (amount <= 0) return { success: false, message: 'Amount must be greater than 0' };

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(supervisorId);
    if (!branchResult || !branchResult.success) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Could not determine branch' };
    }
    var branchCode = String(branchResult.branchCode || '').trim();

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName('OTHER_ENTRIES');
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet('OTHER_ENTRIES');
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 7).setValues([[
        'Type', 'Head', 'Amount', 'Remarks', 'Date', 'Branch Code', 'Supervisor ID'
      ]]);
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 7).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#2E4057').setFontColor('#FFFFFF');
    }

    sheet.appendRow([type, head, amount, remarks, date, branchCode, supervisorId]);

    // ✅ Update supervisor wallet: RECEIPT → credit, PAYMENT → debit
    var walletResult = getWalletBalance(supervisorId);
    if (walletResult && walletResult.success) {
      var currentBal = parseFloat(walletResult.balance) || 0;
      var newBal = type === 'RECEIPT' ? currentBal + amount : currentBal - amount;
      if (type === 'PAYMENT' && newBal < 0) {
        return { success: false, message: '❌ Insufficient wallet balance for this payment.\nAvailable: ₹' + currentBal.toFixed(2) };
      }
      updateWalletBalance(supervisorId, newBal);
      logActivity(supervisorId, 'OTHER_' + type, head + ' | ₹' + amount + ' | Branch: ' + branchCode);
      return {
        success:    true,
        message:    '✅ ' + type + ' entry saved!\nHead: ' + head + '\nAmount: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + '\nNew Wallet: ₹' + newBal.toFixed(2),
        newBalance: newBal
      };
    }

    logActivity(supervisorId, 'OTHER_' + type, head + ' | ₹' + amount);
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Entry saved!' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveOtherEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// Predefined heads list
function getOtherEntryHeads() {
  return {
    success: true,
    receiptHeads: [
      'Opening Cash',
      'Interest Income',
      'Membership Fee',
      'Fine / Penalty Received',
      'Donation Received',
      'Miscellaneous Receipt',
      'Other Income'
    ],
    paymentHeads: [
      'Salary / Staff Payment',
      'Office Rent',
      'Electricity Bill',
      'Stationary / Printing',
      'Travel / Conveyance',
      'Maintenance',
      'Bank Charges',
      'Miscellaneous Expense',
      'Other Payment'
    ]
  };
}
function cleanupReservedNumbers() {
  try {
    var ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var pendingSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PENDING_ENTRIES');

    // Abhi bhi PENDING mein jo hain unhe rakhna hai
    var stillPendingAccounts = [];
    var stillPendingLoans    = [];
    var stillPendingMembers  = [];

    if (pendingSheet && pendingSheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var pData = pendingSheet.getRange(2, 1, pendingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      for (var p = 0; p < pData.length; p++) {
        var pStatus = String(pData[p][5] || '').toUpperCase();
        if (pStatus !== 'PENDING') continue; // Sirf PENDING wale rakhna hai

        var pType = String(pData[p][1] || '').toUpperCase();
        try {
          var pJson = JSON.parse(String(pData[p][2] || '{}'));
          if (pType === 'ACCOUNT_OPEN') {
            var n = parseInt(String(pJson.accountNo || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(n)) stillPendingAccounts.push(n);
          } else if (pType === 'LOAN') {
            var l = parseInt(String(pJson.loanAcNo || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(l)) stillPendingLoans.push(l);
          } else if (pType === 'MEMBER_ENTRY') {
            var m = parseInt(String(pJson.memberId || '').replace(/\D/g, ''));
            if (!isNaN(m)) stillPendingMembers.push(m);
          }
        } catch (je) {}
      }
    }

    // Update PropertiesService
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_ACCOUNT_NOS', JSON.stringify(stillPendingAccounts));
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_LOAN_NOS',    JSON.stringify(stillPendingLoans));
    props.setProperty('RESERVED_MEMBER_IDS',  JSON.stringify(stillPendingMembers));

    Logger.log('✅ cleanupReservedNumbers complete');
    Logger.log('   Accounts still pending: ' + stillPendingAccounts.length);
    Logger.log('   Loans still pending:    ' + stillPendingLoans.length);
    Logger.log('   Members still pending:  ' + stillPendingMembers.length);

    return { success: true, message: 'Cleanup complete' };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('cleanupReservedNumbers error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// MEMBER REQUEST SYSTEM — FRESH COMPLETE BACKEND
// ================================================================
// MEMBER_REQUESTS Sheet Columns (10):
//   A: Request ID | B: User ID  | C: Type    | D: Details
//   E: Amount     | F: Scheme   | G: Date    | H: Status+Comment
//   I: Branch Code| J: Updated On
// ================================================================


// ================================================================
// ✅ AUTO CLEANUP TRIGGER SETUP
// SIRF EK BAAR run karo: GAS Editor → Run → setupCleanupTrigger
// Yeh har raat 2 baje cleanupReservedNumbers() automatically chalata hai
// ================================================================
function setupCleanupTrigger() {
  try {
    // Pehle existing cleanup triggers delete karo (duplicate prevent)
    var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
    triggers.forEach(function(t) {
      if (t.getHandlerFunction() === 'cleanupReservedNumbers') {
        ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t);
        Logger.log('🗑️ Old cleanup trigger deleted');
      }
    });

    // Naya daily trigger banao — har raat 2-3 baje
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('cleanupReservedNumbers')
      .timeBased()
      .everyDays(1)
      .atHour(2)
      .create();

    Logger.log('✅ cleanupReservedNumbers trigger set — runs daily at 2 AM');
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Auto-cleanup trigger set! Runs every night at 2 AM.' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ setupCleanupTrigger error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ================================================================
// ✅ AUTO BIRTHDAY TRIGGER SETUP
// SIRF EK BAAR run karo: GAS Editor → Run → setupBirthdayTrigger
// Yeh har subah 8 baje sendBirthdayWishes() chalata hai
// ================================================================
function setupBirthdayTrigger() {
  try {
    var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
    triggers.forEach(function(t) {
      if (t.getHandlerFunction() === 'sendBirthdayWishes') {
        ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t);
      }
    });

    ScriptApp.newTrigger('sendBirthdayWishes')
      .timeBased()
      .everyDays(1)
      .atHour(8)
      .create();

    Logger.log('✅ Birthday trigger set — runs daily at 8 AM');
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Birthday trigger set! Runs every morning at 8 AM.' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('❌ setupBirthdayTrigger error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ── Helper: MEMBER_REQUESTS sheet banao ya lo ──────────────────
function getOrCreateRequestSheet_() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sh = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER_REQUESTS');
  if (!sh) {
    sh = ss.insertSheet('MEMBER_REQUESTS');
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
      'Request ID', 'User ID', 'Type', 'Details',
      'Amount', 'Scheme', 'Date', 'Status + Comment',
      'Branch Code', 'Updated On'
    ]]);
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#1a237e')
      .setFontColor('#ffffff');
    sh.setFrozenRows(1);
  }
  return sh;
}


// ── FUNCTION 1: Member request submit kare ─────────────────────
// HTML call: .submitRequest(requestData)
function submitRequest(requestData) {
  try {
    var sh = getOrCreateRequestSheet_();
    var requestId = 'REQ' + Date.now().toString().slice(-8);
    var today     = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm');

    // Branch code — login ke waqt sessionStorage se aata hai
    var branchCode = String(requestData.branchCode || '').trim();

    // Agar branch nahi hai toh USER_DETAILS / CREDENTIALS se fetch karo
    if (!branchCode && requestData.userId) {
      branchCode = getBranchCodeFromUser(requestData.userId) || '';
    }

    sh.appendRow([
      requestId,                    // A: Request ID
      String(requestData.userId   || '').trim().toUpperCase(), // B
      String(requestData.type     || '').trim(),               // C
      String(requestData.details  || '').trim(),               // D
      requestData.amount  || '',                               // E
      requestData.scheme  || '',                               // F
      today,                                                   // G: Date
      'Pending',                                               // H: Status+Comment (default)
      branchCode,                                              // I: Branch Code
      ''                                                       // J: Updated On
    ]);

    Logger.log('✅ Request submitted: ' + requestId + ' | User: ' + requestData.userId + ' | Branch: ' + branchCode);
    return { success: true, message: 'Request submitted successfully!', requestId: requestId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('submitRequest error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}


// ── FUNCTION 2: Member apni requests dekhe ─────────────────────
// HTML call: .getUserRequests(currentUserId)
function getUserRequests(userId) {
  try {
    userId = String(userId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!userId) return { success: false, message: 'User ID missing' };

    var sh = getOrCreateRequestSheet_();
    if (sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, requests: [] };

    var data     = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    var requests = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][1] || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== userId) continue;

      var statusComment = String(data[i][7] || 'Pending');
      // Status aur comment alag karo display ke liye
      var statusParts   = statusComment.split('|');
      var statusOnly    = statusParts[0].trim();
      var commentOnly   = statusParts.slice(1).join('|').trim();

      requests.push({
        requestId:  String(data[i][0] || ''),
        type:       String(data[i][2] || ''),
        details:    String(data[i][3] || ''),
        amount:     Number(data[i][4])  || 0,
        scheme:     String(data[i][5] || ''),
        date:       String(data[i][6] || ''),
        status:     statusOnly,
        comment:    commentOnly,
        updatedOn:  String(data[i][9] || '')
      });
    }

    requests.reverse(); // Latest pehle
    Logger.log('✅ getUserRequests: ' + requests.length + ' | userId: ' + userId);
    return { success: true, requests: requests };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getUserRequests error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ── FUNCTION 3: Supervisor apni branch ki requests dekhe ────────
// HTML call: .getAllRequests(supervisorId)
function getAllRequests(supervisorId) {
  try {
    supervisorId = String(supervisorId || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    var supBranch = getBranchCodeFromUser(supervisorId) || '';
    if (!supBranch) {
      return { success: false, requests: [], message: 'Supervisor branch not found. Check CREDENTIALS or USER_DETAILS sheet.' };
    }

    var sh = getOrCreateRequestSheet_();
    if (sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, requests: [] };

    var data     = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    var requests = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var reqBranch = String(data[i][8] || '').trim(); // Col I: Branch Code

      // Same branch ya blank branch (purani entries)
      if (reqBranch !== supBranch && reqBranch !== '') continue;

      var statusComment = String(data[i][7] || 'Pending');
      var statusParts   = statusComment.split('|');
      var statusOnly    = statusParts[0].trim();
      var commentOnly   = statusParts.slice(1).join('|').trim();

      requests.push({
        rowIndex:   i + 2,
        requestId:  String(data[i][0] || ''),  // A
        userId:     String(data[i][1] || ''),  // B
        type:       String(data[i][2] || ''),  // C
        details:    String(data[i][3] || ''),  // D
        amount:     Number(data[i][4])  || 0,  // E
        scheme:     String(data[i][5] || ''),  // F
        date:       String(data[i][6] || ''),  // G
        statusComment: statusComment,          // H: full value
        status:     statusOnly,
        comment:    commentOnly,
        branchCode: reqBranch,                 // I
        updatedOn:  String(data[i][9] || '')   // J
      });
    }

    Logger.log('✅ getAllRequests: ' + requests.length + ' | Supervisor: ' + supervisorId + ' | Branch: ' + supBranch);
    return { success: true, requests: requests };

  } catch (e) {
