    Logger.log('getAllRequests error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}


// ── FUNCTION 4: Supervisor status update kare ──────────────────
// HTML call: .updateRequestStatus(rowIndex, statusWithComment, supervisorId)
// statusWithComment format: "APPROVED | Loan approved as requested"
//                        or "UNDER REVIEW"
//                        or "CLOSED | Issue resolved"
//                        or "REJECTED | Insufficient documents"
function updateRequestStatus(rowIndex, statusWithComment, supervisorId) {
  try {
    rowIndex          = parseInt(rowIndex);
    statusWithComment = String(statusWithComment || '').trim();
    supervisorId      = String(supervisorId      || '').trim().toUpperCase();

    if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Invalid row index' };
    }
    if (!statusWithComment) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Status required' };
    }

    var sh = getOrCreateRequestSheet_();
    if (rowIndex > sh.getLastRow()) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Row not found' };
    }

    var rowData   = sh.getRange(rowIndex, 1, 1, 10).getValues()[0];
    var userId    = String(rowData[1] || '');  // Col B
    var reqType   = String(rowData[2] || '');  // Col C
    var timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm');

    // Col H: Status+Comment save karo
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 8).setValue(statusWithComment);  // H
    sh.getRange(rowIndex, 10).setValue(timestamp + ' by ' + supervisorId); // J: Updated On

    Logger.log('✅ Request updated | Row: ' + rowIndex + ' | Value: ' + statusWithComment + ' | By: ' + supervisorId);

    // Member ko notification
    if (userId) {
      try {
        var msg = '🔔 Your ' + reqType + ' request status updated\n' +
                  '📋 ' + statusWithComment + '\n' +
                  '🕐 ' + timestamp;
        createNotification(userId, msg, 'REQUEST_UPDATE');
        sendRequestUpdateEmail(userId, reqType, statusWithComment, '');
      } catch (ne) {
        Logger.log('Notification error (non-fatal): ' + ne.toString());
      }
    }

    return { success: true, message: 'Status updated successfully!' };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('updateRequestStatus error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// TREASURER AUTO DATE-CHANGE BALANCE SAVER
// Jab bhi date change hoti hai — kal ka closing save karo,
// aaj ka opening = kal ka closing
// ================================================================
function autoSaveTreasurerDayBalance(treasurerId, officeId) {
  try {
    var props    = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var key      = 'TRES_LAST_DATE_' + treasurerId;
    var ss       = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var tz       = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var today    = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var lastDate = props.getProperty(key) || '';

    // ── CASE 1: Pehli baar — sirf aaj ka date save karo ──────
    if (!lastDate) {
      props.setProperty(key, today);
      Logger.log('Treasurer first date set: ' + today);
      return;
    }

    // ── CASE 2: Date same hai — kuch nahi karna ───────────────
    if (lastDate === today) return;

    // ── CASE 3: Date change hui — kal ka closing save karo ────
    Logger.log('Treasurer date changed: ' + lastDate + ' → ' + today + ' | Saving closing balance');

    // Kal ka closing = abhi wallet mein jo hai
    var walletRes  = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
    var currentBal = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;
    var sh         = _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss);
    var logKey     = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;

    // ── Kal ka closing save karo ──────────────────────────────
    var kalClosed = false;
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
        if (String(rows[i][0]).trim() === lastDate &&
            String(rows[i][1]).trim() === logKey) {
          // Record mila — closing update karo
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 5).setValue(currentBal);  // Col E: Closing
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('CLOSED');     // Col F: Status
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date());   // Col H: CloseTimestamp
          kalClosed = true;
          Logger.log('Kal ka closing updated: ' + lastDate + ' = ₹' + currentBal);
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Agar kal ka record hi nahi tha — naya banana
    if (!kalClosed) {
      sh.appendRow([
        lastDate,     // A: Date (kal ka)
        logKey,       // B: Key
        treasurerId,  // C: TreasurerId
        currentBal,   // D: Opening (kal ka opening pata nahi, current se hi)
        currentBal,   // E: Closing (kal ka closing = current bal)
        'CLOSED',     // F: Status
        '',           // G
        new Date()    // H: CloseTimestamp
      ]);
      Logger.log('Kal ka record banaya: ' + lastDate + ' closing = ₹' + currentBal);
    }

    // ── Aaj ka opening save karo = kal ka closing ─────────────
    sh.appendRow([
      today,        // A: Date (aaj ka)
      logKey,       // B: Key
      treasurerId,  // C: TreasurerId
      currentBal,   // D: Opening = kal ka closing
      0,            // E: Closing (abhi 0 — din mein update hoga)
      'OPEN',       // F: Status
      new Date(),   // G: OpenTimestamp
      ''            // H
    ]);
    Logger.log('Aaj ka opening saved: ' + today + ' = ₹' + currentBal);

    // ── Date update karo ──────────────────────────────────────
    props.setProperty(key, today);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('autoSaveTreasurerDayBalance error: ' + e.toString());
  }
}
// ── Get Treasurer Saved Opening Balance from DAILY_BALANCE_LOG ─
function getTreasurerSavedOpening(treasurerId, officeId, targetDateStr) {
  try {
    var ss  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh  = ss.getSheetByName('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return null;
    var key  = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;
    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();

    // Pehle us exact date ka opening dhundho
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0]).trim() === targetDateStr &&
          String(rows[i][1]).trim() === key) {
        Logger.log('Treasurer saved opening found for ' + targetDateStr + ': ₹' + rows[i][3]);
        return parseFloat(rows[i][3]) || 0; // Col D: OpeningBalance
      }
    }

    // Us date ka record nahi mila — previous din ka closing dhundho
    for (var j = rows.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
      if (String(rows[j][1]).trim() === key &&
          String(rows[j][0]).trim() < targetDateStr &&
          String(rows[j][5]).toUpperCase() === 'CLOSED') {
        Logger.log('Treasurer prev closing found for ' + rows[j][0] + ': ₹' + rows[j][4]);
        return parseFloat(rows[j][4]) || 0; // Col E: ClosingBalance
      }
    }

    Logger.log('No treasurer balance record found for ' + targetDateStr);
    return null; // koi record nahi — fallback use hoga
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerSavedOpening error: ' + e.toString());
    return null;
  }
}

// ── Get Treasurer Wallet Balance ──────────────────────────────
function getTreasurerWalletBalance(treasurerId) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };

    // Verify role
    const credSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      let ok = false;
      for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
        if (String(credData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
            String(credData[i][2] || '').toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER') {
          ok = true; break;
        }
      }
      if (!ok) return { success: false, message: 'Not a treasurer account' };
    }

    // ✅ FIX P4: Date change check — auto closing/opening save
    var officeId = '';
    var coSheet  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < coData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(coData[ci][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId) {
          officeId = String(coData[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    autoSaveTreasurerDayBalance(treasurerId, officeId); // ← SIRF YEH LINE IMPORTANT HAI

    // Get or initialize wallet
    const walletResult = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
    if (walletResult && walletResult.success && walletResult.exists) {
      return { success: true, balance: parseFloat(walletResult.balance) || 0 };
    }

    // Auto-initialize if not found
    initializeWallet(treasurerId, 'TREASURER', '', 0);
    return { success: true, balance: 0 };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerWalletBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// TREASURER CASH BOOK REPORT
// Har din ka: Opening → Receipts (branch se) → Payments (branch ko) → Closing
// Closing balance = Treasurer wallet balance hona chahiye
// ================================================================
function getTreasurerCashBook(treasurerId, reportDate) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };

    // Verify treasurer
    const ss         = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const credSheet  = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    let officeId     = '';
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      let ok = false;
      for (let i = 0; i < credData.length; i++) {
        if (String(credData[i][0] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
            String(credData[i][2] || '').toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER' &&
            String(credData[i][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
          ok = true; break;
        }
      }
      if (!ok) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Treasurer access only' };
    }

    // Get treasurer's office
    const coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < coData.length; i++) {
        if (String(coData[i][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
            String(coData[i][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
          officeId = String(coData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Parse date
    const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    let targetDate;
    if (reportDate && String(reportDate).trim()) {
      // Accepts yyyy-MM-dd
      const parts = String(reportDate).trim().split('-');
      if (parts.length === 3) {
        targetDate = new Date(parseInt(parts[0]), parseInt(parts[1]) - 1, parseInt(parts[2]));
      } else {
        targetDate = new Date();
      }
    } else {
      targetDate = new Date();
    }
    targetDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    const targetDateStr     = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    const targetDateDisplay = Utilities.formatDate(targetDate, tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');

    // ── Opening Balance ──────────────────────────────────────────
    // ✅ FIX P4: Pehle DAILY_BALANCE_LOG se saved opening dhundho
    // Agar mila → use karo directly (accurate past date balance)
    // Agar nahi mila → transaction sum se calculate karo (fallback)
    const txnSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE_TXN');
    let openingBalance = 0;
    let todayReceipts  = [];
    let todayPayments  = [];

    const savedOpening = getTreasurerSavedOpening(treasurerId, officeId, targetDateStr);

    if (savedOpening !== null) {
      openingBalance = savedOpening;
      Logger.log('CashBook: Using saved opening for ' + targetDateStr + ': ₹' + openingBalance);
    } else {
      Logger.log('CashBook: No saved balance for ' + targetDateStr + ' — calculating from transactions');
      if (txnSheet && txnSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        const txnDataFb = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
        for (let fi = 0; fi < txnDataFb.length; fi++) {
          const fbOfficeId = String(txnDataFb[fi][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          if (officeId && fbOfficeId !== officeId) continue;
          const fbDateVal = txnDataFb[fi][1];
          if (!fbDateVal) continue;
          const fbDateStr   = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(fbDateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          const fbDirection = String(txnDataFb[fi][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          const fbStatus    = String(txnDataFb[fi][8] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          const fbAmount    = parseFloat(txnDataFb[fi][5]) || 0;
          if (fbDateStr < targetDateStr) {
            if (fbDirection === 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE' && fbStatus === 'COMPLETED') openingBalance += fbAmount;
            else if (fbDirection === 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH' && fbStatus === 'COMPLETED') openingBalance -= fbAmount;
          }
        }
      }
      if (openingBalance < 0) openingBalance = 0;
    }

    // ── Aaj ke receipts/payments collect karo ───────────────────
    if (txnSheet && txnSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      const txnData = txnSheet.getRange(2, 1, txnSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < txnData.length; i++) {
        const txnOfficeId = String(txnData[i][2] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (officeId && txnOfficeId !== officeId) continue;
        const txnDateVal  = txnData[i][1];
        if (!txnDateVal) continue;
        const txnDateStr  = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(txnDateVal), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        const direction   = String(txnData[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        const status      = String(txnData[i][8] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        const amount      = parseFloat(txnData[i][5]) || 0;
        const branchCode  = String(txnData[i][3] || '').trim();
        const remarks     = String(txnData[i][6] || '').trim();
        const txnId       = String(txnData[i][0] || '').trim();
        const processedBy = String(txnData[i][7] || '').trim();
        if (txnDateStr === targetDateStr) {
          if (direction === 'BRANCH_TO_OFFICE' && status === 'COMPLETED') {
            todayReceipts.push({ txnId, branchCode, amount, remarks, by: processedBy, status });
          } else if (direction === 'OFFICE_TO_BRANCH' && status === 'COMPLETED') {
            todayPayments.push({ txnId, branchCode, amount, remarks, by: processedBy, status });
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (openingBalance < 0) openingBalance = 0; // safety

    const totalReceived = todayReceipts.reduce(function(s, r) { return s + r.amount; }, 0);
    const totalSent     = todayPayments.reduce(function(s, p) { return s + p.amount; }, 0);
    const closingBalance = openingBalance + totalReceived - totalSent;

    // Cross-check with wallet
    const walletRes = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
    const walletBal = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;
    const balanceMatch = Math.abs(closingBalance - walletBal) < 1;

    return {
      success:         true,
      treasurerId:     treasurerId,
      officeId:        officeId || '—',
      reportDate:      targetDateDisplay,
      openingBalance:  openingBalance,
      receipts:        todayReceipts,
      payments:        todayPayments,
      totalReceived:   totalReceived,
      totalSent:       totalSent,
      closingBalance:  closingBalance,
      walletBalance:   walletBal,
      balanceMatch:    balanceMatch,
      difference:      Math.abs(closingBalance - walletBal)
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerCashBook error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ================================================================
// TREASURER DAY BEGIN / END + STATUS FUNCTIONS
// In teeno functions mein token nahi — login se already authenticated
// ================================================================

function saveTreasurerOpeningBalance(treasurerId) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // Role verify
    var credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    var isTreasurer = false;
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < credData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(credData[ci][0] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
            String(credData[ci][2] || '').toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER' &&
            String(credData[ci][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
          isTreasurer = true; break;
        }
      }
    }
    if (!isTreasurer) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Treasurer access only' };

    // Office ID
    var officeId = '';
    var coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var oi = 0; oi < coData.length; oi++) {
        if (String(coData[oi][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId) {
          officeId = String(coData[oi][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); break;
        }
      }
    }

    var tz     = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var today  = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var logKey = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;
    var sh     = _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss);

    // Already exists today?
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
        if (String(rows[i][0]).trim() === today && String(rows[i][1]).trim() === logKey) {
          var existingOpening = parseFloat(rows[i][3]) || 0;
          Logger.log('Treasurer Day Begin: already exists for ' + today);
          var existingStatus = String(rows[i][5] || 'OPEN').toUpperCase();
          return {
            success: true, alreadySaved: true,
            status: existingStatus,  // ✅ Frontend ko pata chale OPEN/CLOSED
            message: '✅ Day Begin already done today!\n\nOpening Balance: ₹' +
              existingOpening.toLocaleString('en-IN', {minimumFractionDigits:2}),
            openingBalance: existingOpening, date: today
          };
        }
      }
    }

    // Previous CLOSED day ka closing = today's opening
    var openingBal = 0;
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var allRows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (var j = allRows.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
        if (String(allRows[j][1]).trim() === logKey &&
            String(allRows[j][0]).trim() < today &&
            String(allRows[j][5]).toUpperCase() === 'CLOSED') {
          openingBal = parseFloat(allRows[j][4]) || 0;
          Logger.log('Opening from prev closing: ₹' + openingBal); break;
        }
      }
    }

    // First day — wallet se lo
    if (openingBal === 0) {
      var walletRes = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
      openingBal = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;
    }

    sh.appendRow([today, logKey, treasurerId, openingBal, 0, 'OPEN', new Date(), '']);
    logActivity(treasurerId, 'TREASURER_DAY_BEGIN', 'Opening: ₹' + openingBal + ' | Office: ' + officeId);
    Logger.log('✅ Treasurer Day Begin: ' + today + ' Opening: ₹' + openingBal);

    return {
      success: true,
      status: 'OPEN',   // ✅ Frontend ke liye explicit status
      message: '✅ Day Begin complete!\n\nDate: ' + today +
        '\nOpening Balance: ₹' + openingBal.toLocaleString('en-IN', {minimumFractionDigits:2}),
      openingBalance: openingBal, date: today, officeId: officeId
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveTreasurerOpeningBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function saveTreasurerClosingBalance(treasurerId) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // Role verify
    var credSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CREDENTIALS');
    var isTreasurer = false;
    if (credSheet && credSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var credData = credSheet.getRange(2, 1, credSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < credData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(credData[ci][0] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId &&
            String(credData[ci][2] || '').toUpperCase() === 'TREASURER' &&
            String(credData[ci][4] || 'ACTIVE').toUpperCase() === 'ACTIVE') {
          isTreasurer = true; break;
        }
      }
    }
    if (!isTreasurer) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Treasurer access only' };

    // Office ID
    var officeId = '';
    var coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var oi = 0; oi < coData.length; oi++) {
        if (String(coData[oi][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId) {
          officeId = String(coData[oi][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); break;
        }
      }
    }

    var tz      = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var today   = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var logKey  = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;
    var sh      = _ensureBalanceLogSheet(ss);

    // Current wallet = closing balance
    var walletRes  = getWalletBalance(treasurerId);
    var closingBal = (walletRes && walletRes.success) ? (parseFloat(walletRes.balance) || 0) : 0;

    // Find today's OPEN row and update it
    var found = false;
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
        if (String(rows[i][0]).trim() === today && String(rows[i][1]).trim() === logKey) {
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 5).setValue(closingBal);
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 6).setValue('CLOSED');
          sh.getRange(i + 2, 8).setValue(new Date());
          found = true;
          Logger.log('✅ Treasurer closing saved: ' + today + ' = ₹' + closingBal); break;
        }
      }
    }

    // No today record — create new CLOSED row
    if (!found) {
      var openingBal = 0;
      if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
        var allRows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
        for (var j = allRows.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
          if (String(allRows[j][1]).trim() === logKey &&
              String(allRows[j][0]).trim() < today &&
              String(allRows[j][5]).toUpperCase() === 'CLOSED') {
            openingBal = parseFloat(allRows[j][4]) || 0; break;
          }
        }
      }
      sh.appendRow([today, logKey, treasurerId, openingBal, closingBal, 'CLOSED', new Date(), new Date()]);
      Logger.log('✅ Treasurer closing (new row): ' + today + ' = ₹' + closingBal);
    }

    logActivity(treasurerId, 'TREASURER_DAY_END', 'Closing: ₹' + closingBal + ' | Office: ' + officeId);
    return {
      success: true,
      message: '✅ Day End complete!\n\nDate: ' + today +
        '\nClosing Balance: ₹' + closingBal.toLocaleString('en-IN', {minimumFractionDigits:2}),
      closingBalance: closingBal, date: today, officeId: officeId
    };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveTreasurerClosingBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function getTreasurerTodayStatus(treasurerId) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!treasurerId) return { success: false, message: 'Treasurer ID required' };

    var ss    = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh    = ss.getSheetByName('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
    var tz    = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    var officeId = '';
    var coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < coData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(coData[ci][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId) {
          officeId = String(coData[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); break;
        }
      }
    }

    var logKey = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;

    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: true, status: null, date: today };
    }

    var rows = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0]).trim() === today && String(rows[i][1]).trim() === logKey) {
        return {
          success:        true,
          status:         String(rows[i][5]).toUpperCase(),
          openingBalance: parseFloat(rows[i][3]) || 0,
          closingBalance: parseFloat(rows[i][4]) || 0,
          date:           today
        };
      }
    }

    return { success: true, status: null, date: today };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerTodayStatus error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getTreasurerBalanceLog(treasurerId) {
  try {
    treasurerId = String(treasurerId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    var ss  = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh  = ss.getSheetByName('DAILY_BALANCE_LOG');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, records: [] };

    var officeId = '';
    var coSheet = ss.getSheetByName('CASH_OFFICE');
    if (coSheet && coSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var coData = coSheet.getRange(2, 1, coSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
      for (var ci = 0; ci < coData.length; ci++) {
        if (String(coData[ci][6] || '').toUpperCase() === treasurerId) {
          officeId = String(coData[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase(); break;
        }
      }
    }

    var logKey  = treasurerId + '_' + officeId;
    var rows    = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 8).getValues();
    var records = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][1]).trim() === logKey) {
        records.push({
          date:    String(rows[i][0]).trim(),
          opening: parseFloat(rows[i][3]) || 0,
          closing: parseFloat(rows[i][4]) || 0,
          status:  String(rows[i][5]).toUpperCase()
        });
      }
    }

    records.sort(function(a, b) { return b.date.localeCompare(a.date); });
    return { success: true, records: records.slice(0, 30) };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getTreasurerBalanceLog error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ============================================
// 📅 HOLIDAY CALENDAR SYSTEM
// ============================================

// Admin holidays set kare — HOLIDAYS sheet mein store hoti hain
// Columns: A=Date (dd/MM/yyyy) | B=Description | C=Block (YES/NO)
function isHolidayToday() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('HOLIDAYS');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { isHoliday: false };

    var tz      = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var today   = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
    var data    = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getValues();

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var dateVal = data[i][0];
      var desc    = String(data[i][1] || '');
      var block   = String(data[i][2] || 'YES').toUpperCase();

      // Date format handle karo — Date object ya string dono
      var dateStr = '';
      if (dateVal instanceof Date) {
        dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(dateVal, tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
      } else {
        dateStr = String(dateVal || '').trim();
      }

      if (dateStr === today && block === 'YES') {
        return { isHoliday: true, description: desc || 'Office Holiday' };
      }
    }
    return { isHoliday: false };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('isHolidayToday error: ' + e.toString());
    return { isHoliday: false }; // Error pe block mat karo
  }
}

// Admin: Holiday add kare
function addHoliday(dateStr, description, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only Admin can manage holidays' };
    }
    dateStr     = String(dateStr     || '').trim();
    description = String(description || '').trim();
    if (!dateStr) return { success: false, message: 'Date required (dd/MM/yyyy)' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('HOLIDAYS');
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('HOLIDAYS');
      sh.getRange(1,1,1,3).setValues([['Date','Description','Block Login (YES/NO)']]);
      sh.getRange(1,1,1,3).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a237e').setFontColor('#ffffff');
    }

    // Duplicate check
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var existing = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < existing.length; i++) {
        var ex = existing[i][0] instanceof Date
          ? Utilities.formatDate(existing[i][0], Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
          : String(existing[i][0]).trim();
        if (ex === dateStr) {
          return { success: false, message: 'Holiday already exists for: ' + dateStr };
        }
      }
    }

    sh.appendRow([dateStr, description, 'YES']);
    logActivity(adminId, 'ADD_HOLIDAY', dateStr + ' — ' + description);
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Holiday added: ' + dateStr };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// Admin: Holiday delete kare
function deleteHoliday(rowIndex, adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Only Admin can manage holidays' };
    }
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('HOLIDAYS');
    if (!sh) return { success: false, message: 'HOLIDAYS sheet not found' };
    sh.deleteRow(parseInt(rowIndex));
    logActivity(adminId, 'DELETE_HOLIDAY', 'Row ' + rowIndex + ' deleted');
    return { success: true, message: '✅ Holiday deleted' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// Admin: Saari holidays list kare
function getHolidayList(adminId) {
  try {
    if (!isAdmin(adminId)) return { success: false, message: '⛔ Access denied' };
    var sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('HOLIDAYS');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, holidays: [] };

    var tz   = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getValues();
    var list = [];
    data.forEach(function(row, idx) {
      var d = row[0] instanceof Date
        ? Utilities.formatDate(row[0], tz, 'dd/MM/yyyy') : String(row[0]||'').trim();
      if (d) list.push({ rowIndex: idx + 2, date: d, description: String(row[1]||''), block: String(row[2]||'YES') });
    });
    return { success: true, holidays: list };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// ✅ DATA MODIFICATION SYSTEM
// Maker-Checker: Operator submits → Supervisor approves
//
// Entry Types:
//   MEMBER_MODIFY  → MEMBER ENTRY sheet update
//   ACCOUNT_MODIFY → ACCOUNT OPEN sheet update
// ================================================================

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// 1. Get current member + account data for pre-filling form
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function getMemberAndAccountForModification(memberId, operatorId) {
  try {
    memberId   = String(memberId   || '').trim();
    operatorId = String(operatorId || '').trim();

    if (!memberId) return { success: false, message: 'Member ID required' };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // ── MEMBER ENTRY ───────────────────────────────────────────
    // Cols: A(0)=MemberId B(1)=Name C(2)=Contact D(3)=UserId E(4)=Email F(5)=BranchCode
    var memberSh = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    var memberData = null;

    if (!memberSh || memberSh.getLastRow() < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'MEMBER ENTRY sheet not found or empty' };
    }

    var mRows = memberSh.getRange(2, 1, memberSh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < mRows.length; i++) {
      if (String(mRows[i][0] || '').trim() === memberId) {
        memberData = {
          memberId:   String(mRows[i][0] || '').trim(),
          name:       String(mRows[i][1] || '').trim(),
          contact:    String(mRows[i][2] || '').trim(),
          userId:     String(mRows[i][3] || '').trim(),
          email:      String(mRows[i][4] || '').trim(),
          branchCode: String(mRows[i][5] || '').trim(),
          rowIndex:   i + 2
        };
        break;
      }
    }

    if (!memberData) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Member not found: ' + memberId };
    }

    // ── Branch check ───────────────────────────────────────────
    if (operatorId) {
      var brRes = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (brRes && brRes.success && brRes.branchCode &&
          memberData.branchCode && brRes.branchCode !== memberData.branchCode) {
        return { success: false, message: '⛔ Member belongs to a different branch.' };
      }
    }

    // ── ACCOUNT OPEN ───────────────────────────────────────────
    // Cols: A(0)=MemberId B(1)=Name C(2)=AccountNo D(3)=OpenDate E(4)=AccountType
    //       F(5)=Nominee G(6)=Relation H(7)=Status I(8)=Email J(9)=UserId
    //       K(10)=PhotoUrl L(11)=DOB M(12)=BranchCode
    var accountSh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    var accounts  = [];

    if (accountSh && accountSh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var totalCols = accountSh.getLastColumn();
      // Min 12 cols read karo — L=DOB bhi chahiye
      var readCols  = Math.max(totalCols, 12);
      var aRows     = accountSh.getRange(2, 1, accountSh.getLastRow() - 1, readCols).getValues();

      for (var j = 0; j < aRows.length; j++) {
        var rowMemberId = String(aRows[j][0] || '').trim(); // Col A

        if (rowMemberId !== memberId) continue;

        // DOB formatting
        var dobRaw  = aRows[j][11] || ''; // Col L
        var dobStr  = '';
        if (dobRaw) {
          if (dobRaw instanceof Date) {
            dobStr = Utilities.formatDate(dobRaw, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'dd/MM/yyyy');
          } else {
            dobStr = String(dobRaw).trim();
          }
        }

        accounts.push({
          accountNo:    String(aRows[j][2]  || '').trim(),   // C
          accountType:  String(aRows[j][4]  || '').trim(),   // E
          nomineeName:  String(aRows[j][5]  || '').trim(),   // F
          relationship: String(aRows[j][6]  || '').trim(),   // G
          status:       String(aRows[j][7]  || '').trim(),   // H
          email:        String(aRows[j][8]  || '').trim(),   // I
          photoUrl:     String(aRows[j][10] || '').trim(),   // K
          dob:          dobStr,                              // L
          rowIndex:     j + 2
        });
      }
    }

    Logger.log('getMemberAndAccountForModification: memberId=' + memberId +
               ' | member found=' + (memberData ? 'yes' : 'no') +
               ' | accounts count=' + accounts.length);

    return {
      success:  true,
      member:   memberData,
      accounts: accounts
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getMemberAndAccountForModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// 2. Search member by ID or name — for operator search
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function searchMemberForModification(searchTerm, operatorId) {
  try {
    searchTerm = String(searchTerm || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!searchTerm || searchTerm.length < 2) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Enter at least 2 characters to search' };
    }

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    // Get operator branch for filtering
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, members: [] };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    var members = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var mId      = String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var mName    = String(data[i][1] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var mUserId  = String(data[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var mBranch  = String(data[i][5] || '').trim();

      // Branch filter
      if (branchCode && mBranch && mBranch !== branchCode) continue;

      // Search match — ID, name, or userId
      if (mId.indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1 ||
          mName.indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1 ||
          mUserId.indexOf(searchTerm) !== -1) {
        members.push({
          memberId: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          name:     String(data[i][1] || ''),
          contact:  String(data[i][2] || ''),
          userId:   String(data[i][3] || '')
        });
        if (members.length >= 10) break; // max 10 results
      }
    }

    return { success: true, members: members };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('searchMemberForModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// 3. Operator submits modification request
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function operatorSubmitMemberModification(operatorId, modData, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    modData.memberId = String(modData.memberId || '').trim();
    if (!modData.memberId) return { success: false, message: 'Member ID required' };

    // Validate fields
    if (modData.contact && !/^\d{10}$/.test(modData.contact)) {
      return { success: false, message: '❌ Mobile number must be 10 digits' };
    }
    if (modData.email && !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(modData.email)) {
      return { success: false, message: '❌ Invalid email format' };
    }

    // Sanitize
    var skipKeys = ['dob', 'photoUrl'];
    Object.keys(modData).forEach(function(k) {
      if (skipKeys.indexOf(k) === -1 && typeof modData[k] === 'string') {
        modData[k] = sanitizeInput(modData[k]);
      }
    });

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    var branchCode   = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    modData.branchCode  = branchCode;
    modData.modType     = 'MEMBER_MODIFY';

    return saveToPendingEntries('MEMBER_MODIFY', operatorId, modData, branchCode);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitMemberModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function operatorSubmitAccountModification(operatorId, modData, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    modData.accountNo = String(modData.accountNo || '').trim();
    modData.memberId  = String(modData.memberId  || '').trim();
    if (!modData.accountNo) return { success: false, message: 'Account Number required' };

    // Sanitize
    var skipKeys = ['dob', 'photoUrl'];
    Object.keys(modData).forEach(function(k) {
      if (skipKeys.indexOf(k) === -1 && typeof modData[k] === 'string') {
        modData[k] = sanitizeInput(modData[k]);
      }
    });

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    var branchCode   = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    modData.branchCode = branchCode;
    modData.modType    = 'ACCOUNT_MODIFY';

    return saveToPendingEntries('ACCOUNT_MODIFY', operatorId, modData, branchCode);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitAccountModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// 4. Supervisor approves — actual sheet update
// Called from approveEntry() switch-case
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function saveMemberModification(entryData) {
  try {
    var ss       = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var memberSh = ss.getSheetByName('MEMBER ENTRY');
    if (!memberSh) return { success: false, message: 'MEMBER ENTRY sheet not found' };

    var memberId = String(entryData.memberId || '').trim();
    if (!memberId) return { success: false, message: 'Member ID required' };

    // Find row
    var lastRow = memberSh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No member records found' };

    var rows = memberSh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 6).getValues();
    var targetRow = -1;

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][0] || '').trim() === memberId) {
        targetRow = i + 2;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (targetRow === -1) return { success: false, message: 'Member not found: ' + memberId };

    // Update only provided fields (non-empty values)
    // MEMBER ENTRY cols: A=MemberId(1) B=Name(2) C=Contact(3) D=UserId(4) E=Email(5) F=BranchCode(6)
    if (entryData.name    && String(entryData.name).trim())    memberSh.getRange(targetRow, 2).setValue(String(entryData.name).trim());
    if (entryData.contact && String(entryData.contact).trim()) memberSh.getRange(targetRow, 3).setValue(String(entryData.contact).trim());
    if (entryData.email   && String(entryData.email).trim())   memberSh.getRange(targetRow, 5).setValue(String(entryData.email).trim());

    // Also update ACCOUNT OPEN sheet — name + email sync
    if (entryData.name || entryData.email) {
      var accountSh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
      if (accountSh && accountSh.getLastRow() > 1) {
        var aRows = accountSh.getRange(2, 1, accountSh.getLastRow() - 1, 9).getValues();
        for (var j = 0; j < aRows.length; j++) {
          if (String(aRows[j][0] || '').trim() === memberId) {
            if (entryData.name)  accountSh.getRange(j + 2, 2).setValue(String(entryData.name).trim());   // Col B
            if (entryData.email) accountSh.getRange(j + 2, 9).setValue(String(entryData.email).trim());  // Col I
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // Also update CREDENTIALS email if changed
    if (entryData.email && entryData.userId) {
      // CREDENTIALS mein email column nahi hai by default — skip
    }

    Logger.log('✅ Member modified: ' + memberId);

    return {
      success:  true,
      message:  'Member data updated successfully',
      memberId: memberId
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveMemberModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

function saveAccountModification(entryData) {
  try {
    var ss        = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var accountSh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!accountSh) return { success: false, message: 'ACCOUNT OPEN sheet not found' };

    var accountNo = String(entryData.accountNo || '').trim();
    if (!accountNo) return { success: false, message: 'Account Number required' };

    // Find row
    var lastRow = accountSh.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return { success: false, message: 'No account records found' };

    var rows = accountSh.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 13).getValues();
    var targetRow = -1;

    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      if (String(rows[i][2] || '').trim() === accountNo) {  // Col C = AccountNo
        targetRow = i + 2;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (targetRow === -1) return { success: false, message: 'Account not found: ' + accountNo };

    // ACCOUNT OPEN cols:
    // A(1)=MemberId B(2)=Name C(3)=AccNo D(4)=OpenDate E(5)=AccType
    // F(6)=Nominee G(7)=Relation H(8)=Status I(9)=Email J(10)=UserId
    // K(11)=PhotoUrl L(12)=DOB M(13)=BranchCode

    if (entryData.nomineeName  && String(entryData.nomineeName).trim())  accountSh.getRange(targetRow, 6).setValue(String(entryData.nomineeName).trim());
    if (entryData.relationship && String(entryData.relationship).trim()) accountSh.getRange(targetRow, 7).setValue(String(entryData.relationship).trim());
    if (entryData.email        && String(entryData.email).trim())        accountSh.getRange(targetRow, 9).setValue(String(entryData.email).trim());
    if (entryData.photoUrl     && String(entryData.photoUrl).trim())     accountSh.getRange(targetRow, 11).setValue(String(entryData.photoUrl).trim());
    if (entryData.dob          && String(entryData.dob).trim())          accountSh.getRange(targetRow, 12).setValue(String(entryData.dob).trim());

    Logger.log('✅ Account modified: ' + accountNo);

    return {
      success:   true,
      message:   'Account data updated successfully',
      accountNo: accountNo
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveAccountModification error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
// ================================================================
// SAVINGS MANAGEMENT SYSTEM
// Sheet: SAVINGS MANAGEMENT
// Cols: A=AccountNo | B=Name | C=Amount | D=TXN_TYPE(DEPOSIT/WITHDRAWAL)
//       E=Balance | F=Date | G=Remarks | H=Email | I=UserId | J=BranchCode
// ================================================================

// ── Get SAVINGS accounts for operator (branch filtered) ──────────
function getSavingsAccountsForOperator(operatorId) {
  try {
    var branchCode = '';
    if (operatorId) {
      var br = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
      if (br && br.success) branchCode = String(br.branchCode || '').trim();
    }

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, accounts: [] };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 13).getValues();
    var accounts = [];

    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var accountType = String(data[i][4]  || '').toUpperCase().trim(); // Col E
      var status      = String(data[i][7]  || '').toUpperCase().trim(); // Col H
      var rowBranch   = String(data[i][12] || '').trim();               // Col M

      if (accountType !== 'SAVINGS') continue;
      if (status !== 'ACTIVE') continue;
      if (branchCode && rowBranch && rowBranch !== branchCode) continue;

      accounts.push({
        accountNo: String(data[i][2] || ''),  // Col C
        name:      String(data[i][1] || ''),  // Col B
        userId:    String(data[i][9] || ''),  // Col J
        email:     String(data[i][8] || '')   // Col I
      });
    }

    return { success: true, accounts: accounts };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSavingsAccountsForOperator error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Get current SAVINGS balance ───────────────────────────────────
function getSavingsBalance(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    if (!accountNo) return { success: true, balance: 0 };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('SAVINGS MANAGEMENT');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, balance: 0 };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    var balance = 0;
    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() === accountNo) {
        balance = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0; // Col E: Balance
        break;
      }
    }
    return { success: true, balance: balance };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSavingsBalance error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, balance: 0 };
  }
}

// ── Operator submits savings deposit ─────────────────────────────
function operatorSubmitSavingsDeposit(operatorId, savingsData, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    savingsData.accountNo = String(savingsData.accountNo || '').trim();
    if (!savingsData.accountNo || !savingsData.amount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account No and Amount required' };
    }

    // Server-side: verify SAVINGS scheme
    var schemeCheck = getAccountScheme(savingsData.accountNo);
    if (!schemeCheck.success || schemeCheck.scheme !== 'SAVINGS') {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Sirf SAVINGS scheme accounts allowed hain.' };
    }

    // Date check
    if (savingsData.date && !isToday(savingsData.date)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai.' };
    }

    savingsData.txnType = 'DEPOSIT';

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    var branchCode   = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    savingsData.branchCode = branchCode;

    return saveToPendingEntries('SAVINGS_DEPOSIT', operatorId, savingsData, branchCode);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitSavingsDeposit error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Operator submits savings withdrawal ──────────────────────────
function operatorSubmitSavingsWithdrawal(operatorId, savingsData, token) {
  try {
    var sess = validateSession(operatorId, token);
    if (!sess.valid) return { success: false, message: '🔒 ' + sess.reason };

    savingsData.accountNo = String(savingsData.accountNo || '').trim();
    if (!savingsData.accountNo || !savingsData.amount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account No and Amount required' };
    }

    // Server-side: verify SAVINGS scheme
    var schemeCheck = getAccountScheme(savingsData.accountNo);
    if (!schemeCheck.success || schemeCheck.scheme !== 'SAVINGS') {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Sirf SAVINGS scheme accounts allowed hain.' };
    }

    // Balance check
    var balCheck = getSavingsBalance(savingsData.accountNo);
    var available = balCheck.success ? (parseFloat(balCheck.balance) || 0) : 0;
    var requested = parseFloat(savingsData.amount) || 0;
    if (requested > available) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: '⛔ Insufficient balance!\n\nAvailable: ₹' + available.toFixed(2) +
                 '\nRequested: ₹' + requested.toFixed(2)
      };
    }

    // Date check
    if (savingsData.date && !isToday(savingsData.date)) {
      return { success: false, message: '⛔ Sirf aaj ki date allowed hai.' };
    }

    savingsData.txnType = 'WITHDRAWAL';

    var branchResult = getBranchCodeFromOperator(operatorId);
    var branchCode   = branchResult.success ? branchResult.branchCode : '';
    savingsData.branchCode = branchCode;

    return saveToPendingEntries('SAVINGS_WITHDRAWAL', operatorId, savingsData, branchCode);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('operatorSubmitSavingsWithdrawal error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Supervisor approves — save to SAVINGS MANAGEMENT sheet ───────
function saveSavingsEntry(entryData) {
  var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  try { lock.waitLock(15000); } catch (le) {
    return { success: false, message: '⏳ Server busy, please try again.' };
  }
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('SAVINGS MANAGEMENT');

    // Sheet auto-create
    if (!sh) {
      sh = ss.insertSheet('SAVINGS MANAGEMENT');
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10).setValues([[
        'Account No', 'Name', 'Amount', 'TXN Type',
        'Balance', 'Date', 'Remarks', 'Email', 'User ID', 'Branch Code'
      ]]);
      sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, 10)
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#0d7377')
        .setFontColor('#ffffff');
      sh.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
      sh.setColumnWidth(4, 110);
      sh.setColumnWidth(5, 110);
      sh.setColumnWidth(6, 110);
    }

    if (!entryData.accountNo || !entryData.amount) {
      return { success: false, message: 'Account No and Amount required' };
    }

    var txnType = String(entryData.txnType || 'DEPOSIT').toUpperCase();
    var amount  = parseFloat(entryData.amount) || 0;

    // Previous balance
    var prevBalance = 0;
    if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var allData = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
      for (var i = allData.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (String(allData[i][0]).trim() === String(entryData.accountNo).trim()) {
          prevBalance = parseFloat(allData[i][4]) || 0;
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    // Balance calc
    var newBalance;
    if (txnType === 'WITHDRAWAL') {
      if (amount > prevBalance) {
        return {
          success: false,
          message: '⛔ Insufficient balance!\nAvailable: ₹' + prevBalance.toFixed(2) +
                   '\nRequested: ₹' + amount.toFixed(2)
        };
      }
      newBalance = prevBalance - amount;
    } else {
      newBalance = prevBalance + amount;
    }

    sh.appendRow([
      entryData.accountNo  || '',    // A
      entryData.name       || '',    // B
      amount,                        // C
      txnType,                       // D: DEPOSIT / WITHDRAWAL
      newBalance,                    // E: Running Balance
      entryData.date       || new Date(), // F
      entryData.remarks    || '',    // G
      entryData.email      || '',    // H
      entryData.userId     || '',    // I
      entryData.branchCode || ''     // J
    ]);

    // Operator wallet update
    if (entryData.operatorId) {
      try {
        var walletInfo = getWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId);
        if (walletInfo && walletInfo.success) {
          var newWalletBal;
          if (txnType === 'WITHDRAWAL') {
            // Operator cash deta hai member ko → wallet kam hoga
            newWalletBal = (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) - amount;
          } else {
            // Operator cash leta hai member se → wallet badhega
            newWalletBal = (parseFloat(walletInfo.balance) || 0) + amount;
          }
          updateWalletBalance(entryData.operatorId, newWalletBal);
        }
      } catch (we) {
        Logger.log('Savings wallet update warning: ' + we.toString());
      }
    }

    // Email
    try {
      if (txnType === 'WITHDRAWAL') {
        sendSavingsTransactionEmail(entryData, amount, newBalance, 'WITHDRAWAL');
      } else {
        sendSavingsTransactionEmail(entryData, amount, newBalance, 'DEPOSIT');
      }
    } catch (emailErr) {
      Logger.log('Savings email warning: ' + emailErr.toString());
    }

    Logger.log('✅ Savings ' + txnType + ' saved: ' + entryData.accountNo +
               ' ₹' + amount + ' | Prev: ₹' + prevBalance + ' | New: ₹' + newBalance);

    return {
      success:     true,
      message:     'Savings ' + txnType.toLowerCase() + ' saved successfully',
      newBalance:  newBalance,
      prevBalance: prevBalance,
      txnType:     txnType
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('saveSavingsEntry error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: 'Error: ' + e.toString() };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

// ── Get savings history for account ──────────────────────────────
function getSavingsHistory(accountNo, limit) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    limit = parseInt(limit) || 20;
    if (!accountNo) return { success: true, transactions: [], balance: 0 };

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('SAVINGS MANAGEMENT');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: true, transactions: [], balance: 0 };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 10).getValues();
    var transactions = [];
    var latestBalance = 0;

    for (var i = data.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      if (String(data[i][0]).trim() !== accountNo) continue;
      latestBalance = parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0;
      if (transactions.length < limit) {
        transactions.push({
          accountNo: String(data[i][0] || ''),
          name:      String(data[i][1] || ''),
          amount:    parseFloat(data[i][2]) || 0,
          txnType:   String(data[i][3] || 'DEPOSIT'),
          balance:   parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0,
          date:      data[i][5] ? formatDate(data[i][5]) : '',
          remarks:   String(data[i][6] || '')
        });
      }
    }

    return { success: true, transactions: transactions, balance: latestBalance };
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getSavingsHistory error: ' + e.toString());
    return { success: false, message: e.toString() };
  }
}

// ── Email for savings transactions ───────────────────────────────
function sendSavingsTransactionEmail(data, amount, newBalance, txnType) {
  try {
    var email = String(data.email || '').trim();
    if (!email || email.indexOf('@') === -1) return;

    var isWithdrawal = txnType === 'WITHDRAWAL';
    var subject = (isWithdrawal ? 'Withdrawal' : 'Deposit') +
                  ' Confirmed - Rs.' + amount.toFixed(2) + ' | ' + data.accountNo;

    var body = [
      'Dear ' + (data.name || 'Member') + ',',
      '',
      'Your Savings account ' + (isWithdrawal ? 'withdrawal' : 'deposit') +
        ' has been approved and processed.',
      '',
      '----------------------------------------',
      '   SAVINGS ' + txnType + ' CONFIRMATION',
      '----------------------------------------',
      '',
      'Account No     : ' + data.accountNo,
      'Transaction    : ' + txnType,
      'Amount         : Rs.' + amount.toFixed(2),
      'Balance After  : Rs.' + newBalance.toFixed(2),
      'Date           : ' + (data.date || ''),
      'Branch         : ' + (data.branchCode || ''),
      '',
      '----------------------------------------',
      '',
      isWithdrawal
        ? 'If you did not request this withdrawal, contact your branch immediately.'
        : 'Thank you for your savings!',
      '',
      'Best Regards,',
      'Team DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION',
      'Contact: +91-XXXXXXXXXX | Email: xxxxxxxxxxxxx'
    ].join('\n');

    MailApp.sendEmail(email, subject, body);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('sendSavingsTransactionEmail error: ' + e.toString());
  }
}

// ── getAccountScheme helper (used in multiple places) ────────────
function getAccountScheme(accountNo) {
  try {
    accountNo = String(accountNo || '').trim();
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sh = ss.getSheetByName('ACCOUNT OPEN');
    if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { success: false, scheme: '' };

    var data = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][2] || '').trim() === accountNo) {
        return {
          success: true,
          scheme: String(data[i][4] || '').trim().toUpperCase(),
          name:   String(data[i][1] || '').trim()
        };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, scheme: '' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, scheme: '' };
  }
}
